“Kunjalo Qwabe. Bonke abantu bangabeNkosi futhi 
bangabathandekayo kuyo. Ngisho sebeyihlamukile, yona 
iyabathanda,” kwenanela uZuma. 

“Manje-ke mfo kaZuma, mina ngibona kuyinhlamba embi 
kabi lokhu okushiwo nguSokhela ngami ethi ngiyamthakatha. 
Indaba yomuthi angiyingeni nakancane nje. Ngikhule ngingaka 
nje angikaze ngiwuthi mbibi ngowami umlomo. Angazi-ke 
ukuthi umfo kaSokhela ukususelaphi lokhu akushoyo ngami. 
Mhlawumbe yena angakuchaza kangcono ukuthi unginuka nje 
ungizweni. Uma kungukuthi konke lokhu akushoyo ukuzwe 
esangomeni, kumele saziwe leso sangoma ukuze sethule ubufakazi 
balokhu esikushilo. Kuyangihlupha kakhulu emoyeni ukusukelwa 
ngumuntu angibhece ngobende inyama ngingayidlanga. Sengize 
ngalubikela nomhloli omkhulu lolu daba lukaSokhela.” 

“Wathini?” 

“Wathi uzozama ukuzifikela yena mathupha azochazela othisha 
ngokulethwa kwami lapha esikoleni. Naye kuyamkhathaza 
kakhulu lokhu okwenzekayo.” 

Enkulumweni yakhe uMnguni kwacaca ukuthi yayimphethe 

50 



kabi le ndaba yokubizwa ngomkhumnkuli engayazi nakuyazi 
imithi. Wayengakwazi ngisho nokuphalaza ngentolwane yodwa 
lena. Ayisaphathwa-ke eyobulawu bokuziphunga ukuze ube 
nogazi kwabanye abantu. Wayekholelwa ekutheni imithi idalelwe 
ukuhlobisa umhlaba, hhayi ukugiliswa yonke imigilingwane 
lena engathi shu. UZuma wakuqaphela ukukhathazeka okwase 
kubhalwe ebusweni bukaMnguni. Wabona kahle ukuthi 
okuyiyona nto eyabe imphethe kabi kakhulu kwakuyilena 
yokuthi athi uSokhela uyamthakatha. Wayengenandaba kangako 
nokumpongoloza kwakhe ngesikhundla ayesifuna. Wayenethemba 
lokuthi ngokuhamba kwesikhathi uyogcina esezibone ubulima 
uSokhela bese eguquka. 

“Mina Qwabe ngithi mayingakukhathazi le nto. Uhlanya 
lwendawo lolu. Akekho ongamazi lo muntu. Udume ngakho 
ukusangana lokhu. Uma singanakana naye, singasangana sonke 
lapha esikoleni kuze kwedlulele nasezinganeni. Yinye kuphela 
into esilele kulo muntu. Kusele ukuba simbone eshaya ngesudi 
leselesele emini libalele ethwayiza emagcekeni esikole. Sidinga 
ukwelashwa lesiya siduphunga, nobubi sengathi yinkunzi 
yemvubu. Ungafunga ukuthi weqa esiqiwini evalelwe khona.” 
Washo uZuma ezihlekela samuntu owayengakugqizi qakala konke 
lokhu okwakwenzeka. 

Eqinisweni uZuma wayezama ukuyesula le nto engqondweni 
kaMnguni. Nokho inkulumo yakhe esahlaya yayithola indawo 
kuMnguni ngoba wake walithola nethuba lokuhleka, nokwabe 
kuyinto eyayingasavamile ecabanga ngalolu daba. Wezwakala 
uMnguni esethi, “Hhayi, impela uyakhuluma Nxamalala. 
Sengathi wakuqeqeshelwa ukukhuluma ngale ndlela. Uthi 
awunazo nje iziqu zokwedelela?” 

Wajabula uZuma uma ezwa lowo mbuzo ngoba uMnguni 
wayewubuza ehleka. 

“Akunjalo Qwabe, ngimane ngidinwa nje yizenzo 

51 



zalolu hlanya. Baqinisile labo abathi, ayihlabi ngakumisa. 
Ungambuka umethembe uSokhela ngala mapaklaza esisu 
sengathi yigula lamasi, ucabange ukuthi nengqondo ingangaso 
kanti uyazikhohlisa. Ingangeyezenze. Abanye bathi akufanele 
ukuthi uthi uyindlulamithi uphinde ube ngubhejane. Lokhu 
kukhinyabeza ingqondo ingabe isasebenza ngendlela efanele.” 

“Kahle ngamatshe Nxamalala. Sekwanele manje,” kukhuza 
uMnguni esefile yinsini. 

“Sesikhathele thina yizilima ezazalwa zithumuzela nokucaca 
kahle kamhlophe ukuthi ziyofa zithumuzela.” Asho asukume 
uZuma. 

Waphuma ehhovisi likaMnguni uZuma enethemba lokuthi 
ukwazile ukumsindisa uThish’omkhulu wakhe kule nkinga 
eyayilokhu imudla. Naye uZuma wasala esenokuzinikela 
okukhulu ekusebenzeleni umphakathi walapha eMangweni, 
akhohlwe ngezinye izinto ezazingeyukumusa ndawo. Waqala 
ukuzizwa esenguye futhi lowo Mnguni owasuka eMgungundlovu 
enofuqufuqu lokuzokhuphula izinga lemfundo kulesi sikole. 
Konke wayekubhekise kuMdali yena owabe aze ngaphambili 
ukuthi ngolunye usuku wayezoba ngumphathi walapha 
eBonokuhle. 

Ngemuva kwamahora ambalwa bexoxile oMnguni noZuma, 
othisha bezwa sebebizelwa emhlanganweni ophuthumayo 
bengazelele. Bathuka kakhulu uma sebebona ukuthi kulowo 
mhlangano kwakukhona nomhloli omkhulu. UMnguni wethula 
umhloli omkhulu kothisha wase emdedela ukuba akhulume nabo. 

Wasukuma uMseleku maqede wakhwela phezu kodaba 
ayeze ngalo. Waqala ngokucacisa ukuthi uThish’omkhulu 
omusha waqokwa nguMnyango wezeMfundo ukuba azophatha 
iBonokuhle. Lokhu uMnyango wakwenza ngoba wayeseke 

52 



waphatha isikole ayekuso eMgungundlovu okwesikhashana. 
UThish’omkhulu wakhona wayegula. Ikhono alikhombisa 
ezinyangeni eziyisithupha ebambile uMnguni, lashiya 
enkulu inselelo eMnyangweni wezeMfundo. Kwacaca ukuthi 
kwakuzodingeka ukuba kucatshangelwe kuMnguni kuqala uma 
kukhona isikole esasizodinga uThish’omkhulu. UMnyango 
wezeMfundo wawudinga abantu ababezokhuphula izinga 
lemfundo. Wawungakhathalele zikhundla kanye nokuthi 
umphathisikole omusha wayezoqhamuka kuyiphi indawo. 

Iningi lothisha layizwa incazelo kaMseleku. Lasibona sifanele 
lesi sinyathelo esasithathwe nguMnyango wezeMfundo. USokhela 
akumenelisanga lokhu okwashiwo nguMseleku. Wazama kakhulu 
ukuzibamba angaphawuli kodwa intukuthelo yamehlula. 
Waphakamisa isandla. Wamdedela uMseleku ukuba akhulume. 

“Mina angiyizwa yonke le nto oyishoyo mhloli futhi 
angiyikholwa. Kuyabonakala nje ukuthi kunokwenzelelana kule 
nto. Wehluleka ukuzoyethula kothisha yonke le nto oyishoyo 
mhla ulethe uMnguni kuvulwa izikole. Wawungenasinqe, 
ungabambeki. Namuhla usuqhamuka nale nsumansumane 
yakho engenaso isisekelo uzosikhohlisa. Ngisho nengane ezelwe 
izolo ingayibona le nto oyishoyo ukuthi ingumbhedo. Ngifisa 
ukukubeka ngingahlonizi namuhla ukuthi yinina bahloli 
eniqhatha othisha. Aninalo iqiniso. Namuhla nisho lokhu, kusasa 
nisho lokhuya. Nethembisa abantu izinto nijike ningazifezi. 
Ngempela nicabanga ukuthi sizokholwa kanjani ukuthi izinto 
enizishoyo zingamaqiniso? Kwasakhona nje ukuthi kushiywe 
abantu khona lapha eduzane kuyolandwa abantu balena 
eMgungundlovu, akulona iqiniso.” Asho ahlale phansi uSokhela. 
Wayesegane unwabu ekhefuzela. 

“Ngiyalizwa ilaka lakho Mnumzane Sokhela, kodwa angiqondi 
kahle ukuthi ufuna ukuthini uma uthi silala siphenduka, siqhatha 
othisha. Angizikhumbuli ngithembisa uthisha into ethile 

53 



maqede ngingasamniki. Indaba yokulandwa komuntu kude 
azophatha isikole, akuyona into okufanele kuphikiswane ngayo 
leyo. UMnguni walandwa ngoba selike labonakala igalelo lakhe 
ngaphambili. UMnyango wezeMfundo wawungeke usukele noma 
ngubani umnike izintambo zokuphatha isikole ngoba nakhu 
engowendawo. Lokho kufanele kuphume nje ezingqondweni 
zenu.” 

Asiphakamise futhi isandla uSokhela maqede athi, “Kungani 
nabanye benganikwa ithuba lokubamba okwesikhashana ukuze 
baveze amakhono abo? Angithi nalapha esikoleni bekuzobonakala 
ukuthi ukhona yini onekhono lokuphatha noma akekho. 
Uma nisicindezela ningasiniki amathuba okuziveza ukuthi 
sinamakhono angakanani, nicabanga ukuthi nizosibona kanjani?” 

“Uma ekhona umuntu owaziwayo ukuthi angasiphatha 
kangcono lesi sikole, akudingekile ukuthi kuchithwe isikhathi 
kuvivinywa abanye abantu ukuze kutholakale lowo ongavala 
isikhala esivulekile.” 

“Ayikho le nto oyishoyo. Yitiye nje leli,” kusho uSokhela 
enikina ikhanda. Khona manjalo sibonakale isandla sikathisha 
uZuma siphakama. Amdedele naye uMseleku ukuba akhulume. 

“Mina ngokwami angiboni lutho olonakele nolungaze 
lubilise abantu ngale ndlela. Umhloli usechaze kahle konke futhi 
incazelo yakhe iyezwakala. Uma singanaka into esaqashelwa yona 
nguMnyango wezeMfundo, konke kungahamba kahle. Le ndaba 
yokugijimisa izikhundla ingumbhedo wodwa nje. Asisebenzeni 
bakithi sikhohlwe yizinto ezingasifanele. Kufanele sifunde 
ukubekezela. Siyeza isikhathi sethu sokuphatha izikole. Akufanele 
ukuthi sigxambukele ezintweni okungezona ezethu okwempukane 
ibhukuda obisini. Ngingakahlali phansi, ngifisa ukubonga 
kuwena mhloli ngokusilethela uThish’omkhulu onekhono 
lokuphatha. Ngiyakwethembisa ukuthi sizomeseka ngazo zonke 
izindlela.” Ahlale phansi. 

54 



“Umuntu uzwakala olimini ukuthi uvuthiwe futhi unguthisha 
wangempela. Ngiyawabonga amazwi akho mfo kaZuma. 
Sengathi bonke othisha bangalubuka ngeso elifana nelakho lolu 
daba, balubuke ngeso lokuhlakanipha nokucabangela isizwe. 
Makufundiswe abantwana kungabangwa izikhundla. Njengoba 
sisanda kuthola inkululeko nje kulindeleke ukuthi zingane 
zabantu bakithi abahluphekayo zifundiswe ukuze zikwazi 
ukubhekana nezinselelo zakule lizwe. Siyophumelela kuphela kule 
lizwe uma izikhundla eziphezulu sezenganyelwe ngabantu bakithi, 
abakwaziyo ukuhlupheka komuntu omnyama.” kuphawula 
uMseleku ngokugcizelela. 

“Noma ningasekana kuze kushone ilanga, kodwa ngithanda 
ukunixwayisa ukuthi lo mkhuba woMnyango wezeMfundo 
wokuqasha ngetiye usuphelelwe yisikhathi. Kungekudala 
kuzophasiswa umthetho ozonika imikhandlu emele abazali 
ezikoleni amandla okwenza izincomo ngokuqashwa 
kothisha. Lokhu kukhohlakala koMnyango nosekwaba 
yinsila engcolile kuwona, kuzophela nya. Siyoke sibone phela 
ukuthi kuzogwazelwana kanjani ngoba nezinyunyana zizobe 
zikhona ziqaphile.” Washo umfo kaSokhela kwathula umoya. 
Kwabonakala nje ukuthi wayegadle ngempela kulokhu. Akekho 
owayengayazi le nto ayekhuluma ngayo ngoba imfundo kanye 
nezimo zokusebenza kwase kuqala ukuguquka njengoba 
iNingizimu- Afrika yayisanda kungena emhlabeni wenkululeko. 

Abanye othisha babethulile bengaphawuli. NoMnguni 
akazange aphawule lutho ngalolu daba. Wazithulela waze waphela 
umhlangano. 

Umhlangano waphela sesishayile isikhathi sokuphuma 
kwesikole. Yilowo nalowo wabamba ebheke ekhaya. UMseleku 
wayezibonele ngokwakhe isimo ayephila ngaphansi kwaso 
uMnguni kulesi sikole. Wamdabukela kakhulu. Kodwa ukuba 
khona komuntu onjengoZuma, kwakumnike ithemba. Lokho 

55 



wakuphawula nakuyena uMnguni ngaphambi kokuba bahlukane. 
Wameluleka ngokuthi angalokothi ambeke kude uZuma. 
Amsondeze kuyena ukuze abe ludondolo lwakhe. 

56 



ISAHLUKO SESITHUPHA 

Zahamba izinsuku. UNguzunga wayematasatasa ehla 
enyuka, enza amalungiselelo okuxosha uMnguni. Wayezimisele 
ukusheshe awuqede lo msebenzi ukuze athole iholo lakhe. 
Isikole sasisheshe siphume ngoLwesihlanu. Lokho kwamnika 
ithuba elanele uNguzunga lokuzama ukuxhumana nalabo 
bafundi ababekhononda ngempatho kaMnguni. Wabe azi kahle 
ukuthi uma ebangena ngokuhlushwa kwabo lapha esikoleni, 
bazovumelana nombono wakhe bese ephumelela enhlosweni 
yakhe. 

Engxoxweni yabo kwahlala obala ukuthi bonke labo bafundi 
ababenamacala abathweswa wona lapha esikoleni, babehambisana 
nalokhu okwakushiwo nguNguzunga. Abanye babekubeka ukuthi 
kwakusweleke zona izinsizwa ezazifana noNguzunga ukuba 
ziyiqonde ngqo le ndlovu engaphikiswa ziyikhiphe inkani. Basho 
nokuthi bona babezimisele ukubambisana noNguzunga kuze 
kube sekugcineni. Ukuzithela kwabo ngabandayo kwakungeke 
kubasize ngalutho ngaphandle kokugcina benelwe wumgwaqo. 

Ekugcineni kwavunyelwana ngokuthi kubizwe umhlangano 
ophuthumayo wabafundi ngosuku olulandelayo. Kulowo 
mhlangano kwakuzodingidwa, kuboniswane nangempatho 
eyayingeyinhle lapha esikoleni. Kwakuzoba lula ukubiza lowo 
mhlangano ngoba uMongameli woMkhandlu Omele Abafundi 
wayengomunye walabo ababesengcupheni yokuxoshwa. Icala 
ayethweswe lona kwakungelokufuquza umthunzi wezinkukhu 
ngaphakathi esikoleni. 

Okunye okwakuzobangela ukuthi abafundi bakubone 
kuyisidingo sangempela ukuhlangana, kwakuwudaba lomfundi 
ongumfana owayexoshwe ezinsukwini ezimbili ezedlule. 
Kuthiwa lo mfana watholakala endlini yamantombazane 

57 



eyofuna incwadi yakhe komunye umfundi ayefunda nayo 
ibanga lesishiyagalombili. Kwala ngisho esethi uyachaza 
ukuthi akawephulanga ngamabomu umthetho wesikole kodwa 
wayephoqwe yisivivinyo esasizobhalwa ngosuku olulandelayo, 
lamgojela kunjalo icala. 

Ingxoxo yabo oNguzunga bayiphetha ngokuthi kuzonamekwa 
izingqwembe ezibika umhlangano kuzo zonke izindlu ezihlala 
abafundi. Zazizonamekwa yibona labo bafundi ababehlanganiswe 
nguNguzunga. 

UNguzunga waqinisekisa ukuthi uzoba khona emhlanganweni 
ngosuku olulandelayo. Bavumelana ngokuthi uBen Mabanga 
owayenguMongameli woMkhandlu Omele Abafundi 
kwakunguyena owayezonekela abafundi ingqikithi yomhlangano. 
Kwahlukanwa. 

Kwathi lapho selisikaza ukuyozilahla kunina ilanga, yabe 
isigcwele isikole sonke indaba yomhlangano. Kuwona wonke 
amagumbi esikole, kwakugcwele izingqwembe. Abafundi abaningi 
babedidekile, bekhexe imilomo, bengakuqondi okwakwenzeka. 
Babebonakala bebuthene kuzo zonke izingqwembe lezo befunda. 
Iningi labo lalibonakala ngokunikina amakhanda ukuthi 
lalingayizwisisi indaba yalo mhlangano. Sasingabhaliwe isizathu 
esasiyisisusa sawo. Abanye-ke babewuthakasela lo mhlangano 
kwazise ukuthi babenolwazi lwezinto okwakuyoxoxwa ngazo 
kuwona. Abafundi balala ngalolu suku benexhala lokuzwa ukuthi 
babebizelweni. 

NgoMgqibelo ekuseni watheleka ngezinkani umfo 
kaNyakanyaka esikoleni. Wayegqoke isikhindi esimhlophe 
esasiwubhemuda kanye nesikibha esibomvu esasinophawu 
lwenhlangano yabasebenzi i-COSATU. Wayethwele ikapisi 
elibomvu. Ezinyaweni wayegqoke amateki namasokisi amhlophe. 
Kwathi ngehora leshumi ekuseni waqala umhlangano. 

58 



“Ngiyanibingelela zingane zakwethu,” kubingelela uBen 
ephakamisa isandla. 

“Sibona wena mfowethu,” kuvuma abafundi beshaya izandla 
namakhwelo bekhombisa ukulithakasela izwi lakhe. 

“Zingane zakwethu, ngithe manginihlanganise ukuze 
sibonisane ngekhambi lokuqeda nanti unya lwalo mfokazi 
osiphethe lapha esikoleni. Akekho ongazi ukuthi uThish’omkhulu 
omusha usiphethe kanjani lapha esikoleni. Kuliqiniso elimsulwa 
ukuthi siphethwe ngesandla esifana ncamashi nesohlanga 
olumhlophe olwake lwaphatha le lizwe. Kuyaziwa-ke ukuthi 
sasihlala sisentanyeni empisholo. Ngesikhathi kusaphethe 
uThish’omkhulu uChonco kwakungenjena. Kuthe kungafika 
lona okungazeki nakahle ukuthi uliqhamukisaphi, lavele lagaya 
ngomunye umhlathi itshe. Kumanje ngikhuluma nje uDumisani 
Sikhakhane uxoshiwe. Isizathu sokuxoshwa kwakhe singumbhedo 
nje. Kuthiwa uphule umthetho wesikole ngokutholakala eMzana 
eyolanda incwadi yakhe. Nale mbebhedla enguTholakele ivele 
yaphusha le sisukazi sayo yayomceba kuThish’omkhulu ngale 
kokuzwisisa kuqala ukuthi kungani uDumisani etholakale lapho 
kungafanele khona. Kwasayona le mbebhedla kufanele iyekiswe 
ukugada emahositela ngoba iyahlanya. Kuliwa nathi lapha 
esikoleni. Bona kanye laba bantu okuthiwa bangabazali bethu 
bayasihlukumeza. 

“We bakwethu, sizoxoshwa sonke uma singanakile. Akukho 
hlamvu lo mmbila oluyosinda kule mbokodwe yalo mgayi. 
Nakhu phela sesingasakwazi ukungena ezindlini zodadewethu 
ngoba sesaba ukuxoshwa.” Athi ukudonsa umoya uBen. 

Ngemuva kokuthula isikhashana, aphinde ayiqhube inkulumo 
yakhe uBen. “Nabo odadewethu abasakwazi ukungena ezindlini 
zethu ngakho belu ukwesaba ukuxoshwa. Bekungezwakala 
kangcono ukuba kuthiwa singangena ezindlini zabo kodwa 
singalali khona. Indaba yokuxoshelwa ukuvakasha nje ithule 

59 



du ayizwakali neze. Uma sifuna ukuya edolobheni kufanele 
silengisane nala mathikithi afana nawezinja zakudala ezazithelelwa. 
Uma kuke kwenzeka ngengozi alahleka, kufanele siwakhokhele. 

“Asivunyelwe ukuphuma yinoma ngasiphi isikhathi 
emagcekeni esikole. Uma kushaya ihora lesikhombisa kusihlwa, 
siyavalelwa kuhle kweziboshwa ezingobhulubhantshi. Uma 
sibhadanywe sibhema ugwayi ezindlini ezincane, sititinywa 
ngemvubu ezinqeni sithenjiswe nokuxoshwa. Nikhumbule njalo 
bakithi ukuthi sinabantu abashadile lapha esikoleni. Ake ucabange 
nje ukwebulwa kwabantu abashadile ezinqeni.” Asho achaye 
izandla uBen. “Ukuthi bangabafundi, akuchazi ukuthi sekufanele 
bashaywe yize sebengabazali. Kwakhona ukusetshenziswa 
kwenduku ezikoleni akuvumelekile ngoba wakuvala uhulumeni. 
Yicala elibomvu leli elenziwa yilo muntu.” 

“Kunjalo mfowethu,” kusho abanye abafundi. 

“Child abuse!” kusho omunye. 

Bangquzuke bonke bahleke. 

“Kunabafowethu engikhuluma nje babhalwe emabhukwini 
agunyaza ukuba baxoshwe ngenxa yokubhema nje. Ayisaphathwake 
ekalowo oxoshwe esefunda umatikuletsheni ngenxa 
yokubhema nje. Le mali engaka abazali bakhe abayikhokha 
kanzima isivele yemuka nomfula. UThish’omkhulu uthatha imali 
yabazali bethu abayisebenzele kanzima ayoyidla nohulumeni 
maqede asixoshe uma sebeyisuthi. Kwasakhona lokhu kudla 
esikudlayo lapha esikoleni akucacile neze. Engani phela kuthiwa 
imali esiyikhokhayo incane. Ngithanda ukuzwa kini-ke zingane 
zakwethu ukuthi nithi makwenziwe njani uma kunje?” Athule 
uBen alindele ukuphakama kwezandla. 

Kuthe kusaphele imizuzwana kuthulekile, sabonakala isandla 
siphakama emuva. Amqhwebe uBen lowo ophakamise isandla 
ukuba eze phambili. 

60 



“Okokuqala nje ngizothi ngimzwile uSihlalo walo mhlangano 
ngalokhu asekubekile ngomphathi omusha. Mina ngibona 
ukuthi makaziswe lo muntu ngazo zonke lezi zinto ezisiphethe 
kabi lapha esikoleni, atshelwe nokuthi silindele ukuba aziqede 
nya lingakapheli isonto elizayo. Uma ehluleka ukwenza lokho, 
siyamphelela isikhundla kulesi sikole.” Ahlale phansi. 

“Yebo! Yebo Nguzunga omnyama!” kwenanela abanye 
abafundi beshaya ihlombe namakhwelo kunjeya. 

“Ngonyama! Sikhafulagazi! Into engalali!” kusaqhubeka bona 

abafundi. 

Kusukume omunye umfundi kulabo abasohlwini lokuxoshwa 
eze phambili. “Mina ngisukuma nokubonga amazwi 
okuhlakanipha kumfowethu oqeda kuhlala phansi. Phela ushaye 
into ecokeme lo muntu. 

Nami ngithi ayiphakwe impi iyohlasela ihhovisi 
lomcindezeli, untamolukhuni omnyama ngawo uMsombuluko 
wangomhlomunye. Ngikubeka emahlombe oMkhandlu osimele 
ukuba uyosikhulumela nomphathi ngoMsombuluko ekuseni.” 
Ahlale phansi. Kushaywe izandla. 

“Ngiyanizwa madoda ukuthi nithi thina ngoMsombuluko 
kufanele sihambise izikhalo zenu, nina niqhubeke nokufunda. 
Nizosiphasisa yini uma singasaphumeleli ekupheleni konyaka?” 
kubuza uBen. 

Asukume futhi uNguzunga aqonde phambili. “Ngiyakuzwa 
mfo wethu. Owami umbono uthi, asibuthaneni kulesiya 
sikwele sezimoto ngoMsombuluko ekuseni sinilinde khona 
uma seniyokhuluma nale ndoda. Asizukubuyela emakilasini 
engakaphumi nazwi elisigculisayo umphathi.” 

“Nyamazane!” kusho abafundi. Kulokhu libonakale iningi 
labafundi seliqala ukuyizwisisa le ngqikithi yalo mhlangano. 
Kwabanye kwase kubuye inkumbulo kaThish’omkhulu 

61 



ohambile. Babekhumbula indlela ayebaphethe ngayo beyibona 
imnandi. Babezigcagcazela nje esikoleni benza lokhu nalokhuya 
ngoba kuthiwa badala. Babekhumbula nokuthi uhlelo lonyaka 
lwalwenziwa ukhona uMkhandlu obamele. UMnumzane 
uChonco wayebafundela imithetho yesikole yize kwakungabi 
ndaba zalutho uma bengasayilandelanga eminye yayo. Yonke le 
micabango yayinyakanyakaza ezingqondweni zabanye ngemuva 
kwenkulumo kaNguzunga. 

Waqhubeka njalo umhlangano abafundi bezibala bezibalile 
izinto ezimbi nokuthiwa zazenziwa othisha abamhlophe kubona 
ngoba bempisholo. Babesho abafundi ukuthi konke lokhu 
kwakwenzeka ngentando kaMnguni. Nguyena owayenika lawo 
maBhunu igunya lokusinela emakhanda abo. Wayesagcinelwenike 
umuntu owayedayisa ngabantu bakubo ezitheni? 

Sezibhalwe zonke phansi izikhalo zabafundi, wavalwa 
umhlangano. UBen wacela uNguzunga ukuba afike ngosuku 
olulandelayo lapha esikoleni ekuseni azobelekelela ukuhlela 
izikhalo zabo phansi. Babezodingida nangesu ezazizobekwa ngalo 
kumphathi. Kwahlukanwa. 

Ngakusasa ekuseni oBen bavuswa nguNguzunga. Bawutikatika 
umsebenzi kwaze kwaba semini. UNguzunga wahamba ngemuva 
kwedina esephindela kwaBhekuzulu. Wayenelisekile kakhulu 
yindlela ezaziqhubeka ngayo izinto. Ithemba lokuxosha uMnguni 
lalinqwabelene ngaphakathi kuyena okwendunduma yodaka 
lwentabamlilo. Kwakumkhanyela ukuthi wayezoyinqoba le mpi. 
Wayekuphawulile ukuthi bonke abafundi babemhlonipha futhi 
bemethemba. Lokhu kwakufakazelwa yindlela ababemthakasela 
futhi bewutusa ngayo umbono wakhe. Wazitshela ukuthi 
uyothola ukuphumula emoyeni uma esewuphothulile umsebenzi 
wakhe, neholo ayethenjiswe lona selisezandleni zakhe. 

62 



NgeSonto emini umhlangano wabalimi waphela sekukubi 
kungasekho ukubekezelelana nokuhloniphana kumalungu. 
Ingxabano yayidalwe yinkulumo eyayithulwe yikhehla lejazi. 

Ngesikhathi uSihlalo weNhlangano Yabalimi evula ithuba 
lokubeka imibono ngodaba okwakuhlangenwe ngalo, ikhehla 
lejazi laveza udaba lokwephucwa kukaSokhela isikhundla sakhe 
ngumuntu wokuhamba. Lawunxusa kakhulu umhlangano ukuba 
ungenelele kulokho ukuze kuqedwe la maqili aphuca abantu 
bendawo izikhundla zabo. 

Kwathi lapho uSihlalo weNhlangano ethi uyalikhalima 
ikhehla lejazi ulibuyisa esihlokweni somhlangano, kwasuka 
esikhulu isidumo. Phela uSihlalo wayekubeke kwacaca 
ukuthi lo mhlangano wawungewona owepolitiki yezikole. 
Wawungowabalimi futhi uphathelene nezokulima kwaphela nje. 
Izindaba ezaziphathelene nezikhundla zothisha zazingaqondene 
nakancane nomphakathi, kodwa zaziqondene noMnyango 
wezeMfundo. Lapaquza ikhehla lejazi laze lathamba. Wayelokhu 
emile uSihlalo emazwini akhe engafuni ukugudluzwa yilona. 

Kulo mhlangano kwakukhona amanye amakhehla amabili 
ayeseka ikhehla lejazi. Elinye lawo lalikhala ngamazwi kaSihlalo 
lithi ayekhombisa ukweseka izigebengu ezazisuka emadolobheni 
zizoqola izingane zendawo. Lasho nokuthi kwakuyithuba elihle 
leli lokuveza izinto ezazihlukumeza othisha esikoleni. Lona 
lalibona ukuthi umhlangano wabalimi wawusuphelile ngoba 
uSihlalo wayesekushilo konke ayefuna ukukusho. Ngaleyo ndlela 
lalingaqondi ukuthi ikhehla lejazi lalone ngaliphi ngokufaka 
isihloko esasithe phecelezi kulo mhlangano. 

Kusenjalo, kwasukuma elinye ikhehla lafakazela elaliqeda 
kukhuluma. Nalo lakhwela ladilika kuSihlalo wenhlangano. Lathi 
kwasayena wayeyisihambi kulesi sigceme saseMoyeni engeyena 
owokuzalwa khona. Yingakho wayekhuluma ngale ndlela sengathi 
wehla phezulu njengemvula. Abelungu ababemlethile ukuba 

63 



azobasiza abathuthukise kwezolimo, babeqonde ukuhlomula 
ngandlela thize ezivunweni zabo. Kwakungekhona ngempela 
ukuthi babeqonde ukubasiza. 

Le nkulumo yamakhehla yezwakala kabi impela 
ezindlebeni zabanumzane ababethamele lo mhlangano. Baqala 
ngokuwahlonipha la makhehla bewabonisa ngenhlonipho 
ukuthi uSihlalo wenhlangano wayengonanga ngokulichitha 
udaba lukaSokhela. Vele lwaludinga uMnyango wezeMfundo. 
Bona njengabazali bezingane, babengenandaba nokuthi 
isikole sasiphethwe ngubani futhi ephumaphi. Bakubeka 
nokuthi babelindele usuku lomhlangano wokwethulwa 
kukaThish’omkhulu omusha kubona ngokusemthethweni. Bona 
babezimisele ukubona izingane zabo zifundiswa, kungadlalwa 
ngazo. Kodwa ngenxa yokubhoka kwamakhehla engafuni 
ukulalela, nabo abanumzane bagcina sebecikekile. Bavele banxusa 
uSihlalo ukuba asale esewuchitha umhlangano ngoba okuningi 
base bekuxoxile nakuba kwakusele iphuzu lokubuzwa kwemibuzo. 

Iningi labanumzane lalisola ukuthi uSokhela wayesebenzisa 
la makhehla ukucindezela umphakathi ukuba umelekelele 
ukuthola lesi sikhundla sokuphatha. Bafunga bagomela ukuthi 
abazukulungena lolu daba. Bazolungena kuphela uma seluthinta 
ukufunda kwezingane zabo. 

NgoMsombuluko ekuseni kwahlwa emini kothisha uma 
bebona abafundi bengayishayi mkhuba insimbi eyayibabizela 
ehholo ukuyothandaza. Abanye babo babelunguza emafasiteleni 
bengawugqokile umfaniswane wesikole. 

Yaphinde yakhala insimbi ibakhumbuza ukuthi kwakufanele 
banyakaze. Kwavele kwafana nje akwaze kwaba khona mehluko. 
Besakhungathekile othisha bengazi ukuthi kwenzakalani, 
laqhamuka iqembu likaBen lilandelwa yiqulu labafundi 

64 



elalivuma ingoma yomzabalazo. Amagosa akhona

NGOMPHATHI ONGUNTAMOLUKHUNI!” Olunye 
uqwembe lwalunomfanekiso wekhanda likaMnguni. 
Ngenhla kwalelo khanda kwakubhalwe ukuthi, “BUYELA 
KWELAKINI! PHANSI NGENGCINDEZELO! PHEZULU 
NGENKULULEKO!” 

Abafundi bonke basala epaki yezimoto. UBen noMkhandlu

kukhuzwa iziqubulo zomzabalazo. 

Othisha base bekhohliwe ukuthi basesikoleni. Yilowo nalowo 
wayecabanga ukuthi uyaphupha. Yayingakaze yenzeke into efana 
nalena kulesi sikole. Kothisha abadala kwabe kunguSokhela 
kuphela owayengakhombisi ngisho noluncane uvalo ngalokhu 
okwakwenzeka. Wayezokhathazekelani ngoba kwakufezeka

Kwathi ngesikade wabonakala uZuma esondela kuSokhela. 

“Nithule nithini Sokhela izingane ziqhuba ukweyisa phambi 
kwenu? Angithi yinina abaphathi besikole?” 

“Nansi imihlola yami bo! Uthi niyangizwisa nje bothisha?”

“Yeyi wena! Ngithi phendula umbuzo wami, ungalokhu 
ubakaza sengathi yinkukhu inethiwe! Ngithi uthothobele nje 
ucabangani ngalezi zingane ezisigibela emakhanda? Angithi zolo 
lokhu kade ukhononda ngokuthi uThish’omkhulu ukwephuce

emakilasini. Yisona-ke isikhathi lesi sokuveza ubuholi bakho 
ngokuba uzeluleke ukuthi le nto eziyenzayo angeke izisize 
ekwakheni ikusasa lazo. Shona khona-ke!” Washo uZuma 
emkhomba indlela. 

65 



“Hhayi bo! Kanti ufunani kimi wena mfana? Yini lena 
engakudlela yona? Uthi uyazi nje ukuthi umfana engagcina 
ngimshaye ngempama wawa phansi wayengaphezulu kwakho 
futhi eyinsizwa eyondlekile? Angazi-ke ukuthi ubuyini wena lo 
mnenke lona! Nx! Yehlukana nami-ke!” 

“Wayephethwe amathumbu lowo mfana okhuluma ngaye. 
Ngeke ungenze lutho mina ngisho usuthanda. Ukwazi kahle 
lokho.” 

“Ake wehlukane nami wena! Kanti ufuna ukubonani ngempela 
we Zuma? Ngizothi ngisuka ngibe ngiphelelwa yisineke bese 
ngikusakaza ngempama. Usukwejwayele ukungeyisa wena 
mqhamuka ndini! Iyona nhlonipho lena abakufundisa yona kini? 
Ngiphendule mduka ndini!” 

“Uyangimangaza wena ngokulokhu ukhonkotha sengathi yinja 
enqena ukuzingela. Selokhu uyayaleza kodwa awushayi. Izandla 
ziboshiwe yini? Awushayi ngani ngempama elahla phansi ukuze 
ngikukhombise ukuthi ngisishaya kanjani isithutha. Uyisilima 
phela wena ngoba uyashesha ukukhohlwa ukuthi ngisishaya 
kanjani isiduphunga. Ngizokuphinda futhi. Uyazi-ke nawe ukuthi 
eyami impama ayinalo isekela lomphathisikole. Iyahlala nje 
kumuntu kungabi ndaba zalutho. Mina ngizalwa yishinga lensizwa, 
angizalwa yizimuzimu eligxishe amatshe ebuchosheni njengawe.” 

Zimnethe kanjalo uSokhela izinduku zikaZuma. Acasuke aze 
anxaphe uSokhela. Aphefumulele phezulu ebambelele okhalweni 
ngenxa yentukuthelo. “Kungcono ngihambe ngoba ngizoze 
ngenze amacala ngisakaze le nto ngempama kanti vele izizacele 
nje.” Asho athathe izinyawo uSokhela. 

“Liphume nobovu! Hamba uyolala lesi siduphunga! Uyisilima 
kabi wena sithwalambiza ndini!” 

Pho wayesakhuluma nobani uZuma ngoba wayeseshaye 
utshani umfo kaSokhela. 

66 



Laphaya ehhovisi likaMnguni kwakonakele. UBen wayeqale 
wangena yedwa besele ngaphandle ababehambisana naye. 
Wabingelela uMnguni ngenkulu inhlonipho. Wase ecela ukuba 
abavumele bewuMkhandlu Omele Abafundi ukuba baxoxe naye. 

“Nifuna ukuxoxa nami ngesikhathi sokufunda? Angithi 
nganitshela kahle ukuthi uma nifuna ukuxoxa nami kufanele 
nize ngesikhathi okungesona sokufunda? Angikushongo lokho 
Ben?” kubuza uMnguni ngokukhulu ukunengwa yilo mfana 
wakwaMabanga obonakala eyisaphulamthetho esikhulu. 

“Wakusho Thish’omkhulu.” 

“Nifunani-ke lapha ngoba yisikhathi sokufunda lesi 
enidlala ngaso? Angithi kumanje nje kufanele ukuthi ngabe 

seniyathandaza?” 

“Ukuthi Thi…” 

“We mfana kaMabanga! Ukuthi nimele abafundi lapha 
esikoleni akusho ukuthi seninelungelo lokuziphathela umthetho 
ngezandla. Uyangizwa ukuthi ngithini?” Yasho into kaMnguni 
isimkhombe ngomunwe emehlweni uBen. 

“Ngiyakuzwa Thish’omkhulu.” 

“Njengamanje ngithi phuma lapha ehhovisi lami! Ngifuna 
ukunibona nisehholo khona manje!” 

“Yehlisa umoya Thish’omkhulu. Kubi laphaya phandle. 
Kungeze kwakusiza ukuthetha ngoba uzozidonsela amanzi 
ngomsele ungabe usazi ukuthi uzowakhipha kanjani endlini. 
Hamba kancane ngoba uzoshayisa. Khohlwa yindaba yokutatazela 
sengathi uchatha uhlanya.” Washo umfo kaMabanga emhleka 
usulu. 

“Habe, uCetshwayo eseNkandla! Usongela mina kanjalo 
mfana? Uthi uyazizwa nje ukuthi uyangisongela?” Washo 
uMnguni emkluluza ngamehlo avutha ulaka. 

67 



“Angikusongeli Mphathi wami. Ngizama ukukubonisa ngoba 
awazi ukuthi bathukuthele kanjani abafundi. Ngikhuluma 
nje bayabhikisha laphaya phandle ngenxa yokunganeliswa 
yindlela osiphethe ngayo lapha esikoleni. Khona manje sizama 
ukuwubhula lo mlilo osuvutha isikole sonke ngenxa yakho. Wena 
kanye futhi ufaka amafutha okuwubhebhethekisa. Kuseyikho 
njalo ukungazi. Impela baqinisile abadala uma bethi, ukungazi 
kufana nokungaboni.” 

Ethuke kuthi makaqimuleke phansi uMnguni uma ezwa 
ukuthi izinto zimi ngalolu hlobo. 

“Angizwa kahle mfana. Uthi bayabhikisha abafundi? Hhayi 
bo! Ngeke! Khuluma kahle wena mfana, uthini?” Wayibuza leyo 
mibuzo engaphendulwa uMnguni eseyolunguza efasiteleni. 

“Ngithi Thish’omkhulu abafundi bathelwe ngezibonkolo 
emehlweni okwemidlwembe. Siye savumelana ngokuthi 
sixoxisane nawe ngoba sikuzwela futhi sikuhlonipha. Ulaka 
alusoze lwakusiza. Nakuba kuyakhulunywa nje kungenxa yami 
engibancenge ubusuku bonke abafundi. Ngibe sengibethembisa 
ukuthi sizocela ukuxoxisana nawe namuhla ekuseni ukuze 
sisheshe siyixazulule le nkinga kungakadaleki umonakalo 
omkhulu. Angazi-ke ukuthi ufuna ukubonani ngokungixosha 
kwakho lapha ehhovisi lakho. Bayalwa laba bantu,” kucindezela 
uBen ngenhloso yokumgoba inkani uThish’omkhulu. 

Aphumele phandle uMnguni ukuyobona le nto eyayishiwo 
nguBen. Avele abikelwe wuthuli lubheke phezulu ukuthi 
konakele. Izingqwembe zazindiza emoyeni. Aphindele ehhovisi 
lakhe. “Umthetho wenu nifuna ukuguqula lesi sikole sibe 
yisidleke sikathekwane, ngiyayibona le ngqondo eniza nayo. 
Ngifuna ukunitshela kahle ukuthi ngeke nikubone lokho. Uma 
uThish’omkhulu walapha eBonokuhle kusenguGulukudela 
Mnguni, ngithi ngeke nikubone lokho! Ningamane ningikhande 
ngamatshe ngiphenduke uSitefani. Niyokubona emathuneni 

68 



lokho! Angisoze ngidlale nina mina. Suka lapha phambi kwami! 
Phuma!” 

Azibonele naye uBen ukuthi kuyashisa manje. Aphume ngale 
kokudaza inkani. 

Uthe esuka uMnguni wayethatha umshini wokukhuluma 
onezipikha ezixhonywe obondeni lwezindlu ezihlala abafundi 
wabeluleka ukuba baye emakilasini. Wakubeka ukuthi uma 
bengakwenzi lokho bazothathelwa izinyathelo ezinzima. 

Bekuzwa lokhu abafundi, bavele bawuchapha ngenhlamba 
umbhobho lowo baqhubeka nomduvo. 

Kwakwenzeka lokhu nje uSokhela wayezivalele ehhovisi lakhe 
ebukela ngefasitela. Wayebukeka enethemba ngaphakathi emoyeni 
ngoba sengathi lo mfana wayewenza ngempela umsebenzi wakhe. 
Okwakumthokozisa kakhulu ngukuthi wayengekho owabe azi 
ngalo mshoshaphansi ngaphandle kwakhe noNguzunga. 

UMkhandlu wafike wayendlala indaba kubafundi. 
Wabachazela ukuthi awubange usakwazi ukuxoxa nomphathi 
ngoba uvele wakhombisa ulaka olwesabekayo. 

“Angazi-ke nami ukuthi sizokwenzenjani ngoba nakhu 
usekhulumile ngombhobho ukuthi usifuna emakilasini 
lingakashayi ihora lesishiyagalombili. Uma ngibheka ewashini 
lami, ngibona sisalelwe yimizuzu ethi mayibe lishumi kuphela 
ngaphambi kokuba sithathelwe izinyathelo ezinqala. Bengicela 
ukuzwa kini bafowethu nodadewethu ukuthi yiziphi izinyathelo 
esizozithatha ukusukela manje.” Kubuza uBen. 

“Mina bafowethu, ngibona ukuthi kungcono ukuba sikushaye 
indiva lokhu okushiwo ngumphathi ukuze abone kahle ukuthi 
sithukuthele. Akakhohliwe sisinisa amahleza. Siyoke sibone phela 
ukuthi kuyogcina bani phakathi kwethu naye. Uzoyithobela 
ngenkani imithetho yethu ngisho engathandi. Unikiwe ithuba 
lokubonisana nathi ngezinkinga ezidalwe nguyena. Ngenxa 

69 



yokuthi uzenza umuntu osile nowazi kakhulu ngoba ephuma 
kwelezinkinsela eMgungundlovu, wenqabile. Mina ngithi 
asimlindeni sibone ukuthi yiziphi lezi zinyathelo ezinqala 
asesabisa ngazo,” kuphawula uNguzunga ngokuzethemba 
okukhulu. Kuzwakale u ‘elethu!’, bagiye abanye abafundi ngenxa 
yenjabulo. 

“Hhayi-ke bafowethu, uma nisho kanjalo, kulungile. 
Ingaqhubeka impi yomzabalazo,” kusho uBen. 

Uqhubeke umzabalazo. Uqhubeke njalo kuze kushaye isikhathi 
esinqunywe nguMnguni. Uphinde umpongoloze umbhobho 
ubexwayisa ukuba baphuthume emakilasini. Ukuphawule ukuthi 
uma bengakwenzi lokho, umthetho uzobaphoqa ukuba baphume 
baphele emagcekeni esikole. Ukuphawule nokuthi kube ngumusa 
nje ukuba banikezwe ithuba lesibili lokuphindela emakilasini. 
Bekufanele ukuthi ngabe sebexoshiwe. 

Kulokhu akekho owake wazikhathaza ngokwakushiwo 
nguMnguni. Baziqhubekela nomzabalazo abafundi. 
Kwabakhanyela bonke abasebenzi ukuthi itshe laligaya ngomunye 
umhlathi ngalelo langa. Babefisa ukubona isiphetho sale ndaba 
ukuthi sizoba njani. NoSokhela wayecabanga okufanayo 
nalaba abanye. Abafundi bazitshela ukuthi abazukuhamba 
lapha esikoleni lungakashayi usuku lokuvalwa kwezikole 
ngokusemthethweni. Bona babengazelanga ukuzokwethuswa 
ngekhasi lenyoka efile lapha esikoleni. Lowo owayethi 
uyabaxosha, wayebulawa wukugula okwakuhlasele ikhanda 
lakhe kabuhlungu. Babengezukuya ndawo bona ngoba lesi 
sikole sasingesabo. Kwakungesona esikalo muntu owayephilela 
ukubashaya ngofezela abanye bebashaya ngesiswebhu. Phambili 
ngomzabalazo wokuchitha ijoka lomlungu omnyama! 

Bathe bethuka abafundi babebona izinqola ezinkulu 
zamaphoyisa zingena ngaphakathi esikoleni. Baqale bama isibindi 
bathi bazowatshela kahle amaphoyisa ukuthi babengalwi nawo 

70 



kodwa babefuna izidingo zabo kule ndoda yakwaMnguni. 
Ngebhadi amaphoyisa enza umsebenzi athunywe wona, awanaso 
isikhathi sokulalela insumansumane eyahlula umntakaZondi 
wancamela ukuhlala phezu kwezikhali, wayibamba eyamakhanda. 

Zithe zingangena izinqola zamaphoyisa ngaphakathi esikoleni, 
ehla amaphoyisa ephethe izibhamu nezimvubu, afike angabuza 
kubafundi. Yaqhuma imvubu, lasho ibhuzi. Kwasuka esikhulu 
isidumo sebebaleka abafundi. Kwase kuphelile ukuthi isikole 
singesabo, abayindawo. Babonakala sebebelethe izithende 
beyophuma ngesango. 

Konke lokhu kwakwenzeka uSokhela esephumile ehhovisi 
lakhe lapho ayezivalele khona. Wayebukeka engeneme 
yilesi senzo samaphoyisa. Wayebona kahle ukuthi uMnguni 
wayengazimisele nakancane nje ukuhamba. Okwakumhlupha 
kakhulu ngukuthi wayengenalo ulwazi lokuthi kuze kufikwe 
lapha nje kwakuqalwephi. Wayengakwazi nokuzidlisa satshanyana 
kuNguzunga ngenxa yokuthi wayemdonse ngendlebe ukuba 
angalokothi amthinte kungakasho yena. 

Akabonakalanga uMnguni ezoxoxa nawothisha ngale nkinga. 
Wavele wakhuluma ngombhobho wabayala ukuba bahambe 
babuye ngakusasa. Bahamba-ke. 

Ngehora lesikhombisa kusihlwa uSokhela ezihlalele kwakhe 
endlini yokuphumula, wezwa isimemezelo somhlangano 
sikhishwa nguThish’omkhulu waseBonokuhle. Babecelwa bonke 
abazali bezingane ezazifunda khona ukuba beze emhlanganweni 
ngoMgqibelo ngehora leshumi ekuseni. 

Lesi simemezelo samkhathaza kakhulu uSokhela. Wayefisa 
ukwazi ukuthi uMnguni wayezozihlangula ngaliphi kubazali uma 
befuna ukwazi ngembangela yokuxoshwa kwezingane zabo. 

“Angingabazi ukuthi uyoqeketha amanga wodwa kubazali 
bezingane. Uyoziveza emsulwa. Icala lonke uyolinameka 

71 



ezinganeni. Pho-ke abazali bakule ndawo bayizidididi ezivuma 
yonke into. Khona manje balethelwe umuntu abangamazi ukuba 
azophatha isikole. Kunokuba bakusukumele lokho, bayihlabe 
inhla…” 

Aphazanyiswe nguMaMhlongo uSokhela emlethele 
itiye. “Kanti Baba uhleli nendaba enkulu kangaka?” Abuze 
uMaMhlongo ebeka izitsha zetiye phezu kwetafula elaliphambi 
kukaSokhela. 

“Ndabani leyo okhuluma ngayo Thoko?” kubuza uSokhela 
ngokuhluthuka. Wayengafuni ukumthambela unkosikazi wakhe 
ngoba wayemshumayeza ngokuthi kufanele ahlukane nale 
ngqondo yakhe yokulwa noMnguni. 

“Ngisho indaba yokuxoshwa kwabafundi esikoleni. Ngempela 
baxoshelweni?” 

“Angazi.” 

“Awazi kanjani Baba ube unguthisha wabafundi abaxoshiwe?” 

“Musa ukungifundekela ngento engingahlangene nayo 
Thoko. Uhlulwa yini ukuyobuza kuMnguni ukuthi ubaxosheleni 
abafundi? Wazi kahle ukuthi ngikhishwa inyumbazane kulesiya 
sikole. Ayikho into engibikelwa yona. Nami ngiyefana nawe, 
angazi ukuthi kwenzenjani.” 

Wamane wafunda kwezakhe uMaMhlongo ukuthi lukhulu 
olwalwenzekile. Wakhetha ukuthula. 

72 



ISAHLUKO SESIKHOMBISA 

Batheleka ngezinkani abazali bezingane ngoMgqibelo ekuseni 
esikoleni bezokwethamela umhlangano. UMnguni wayememe 
bonke othisha ukuba babe khona kulowo mhlangano kodwa 
uSokhela akezanga. 

Esezibekile uMnguni izizathu ezazibe yimbangela yokuvalwa 
kwesikole, kwezwakala ukukhononda okukhulu kubazali. Kuleso 
sixuku esasikhononda kwakukhona nekhehla lejazi. Lona-ke 
lalide linikina ikhanda samuntu ongeneliswa yilokhu akuzwayo. 
Lalisukuma, lisineke kuvele ugqinsi lwezisini ezingenamazinyo, 
liphinde lihlale phansi ngesikhathi uMnguni elandisa abazali 
ngembangela yesinyathelo asithatha. Kwathi makhathaleni 
labonakala seliphakamisa isandla. Waliqhweba uMnguni ukuba 
lizokhuluma embhojeni. 

“Mgcinisihlalo, ngiyakuzwa okushoyo. Ngisakulalele 
ukhuluma, kukhona lapho engidideke khona. Uthe abafundi 
wabaxosha ngoba bengafuni ukungena emakilasini kodwa 
awusitshelanga ngokuyiyona mbangela eyadala ukuba banqabe 
ukufunda. Ukuze sikhulumele phezu kwento ezwakalayo, 
ngicela ukuba usitshele kuqala ngembangela yokwenqaba 
kwabo ukufunda. Bebengeke bamane banqabe nje ngaphandle 
kwesizathu. ” Lisho liwufulathele umbhobho ikhehla liyohlala 
phansi. Kushaywe ihlombe. 

“Wafika uMkhandlu Omele Abafundi ekuseni ehhovisi 
lami wacela ukukhuluma nami sewuvele uqhubeka umduvo. 
Ngawucela ukuba uphindele kubo abafundi uyobatshela ukuthi 
kufanele bayofunda kuqala bese kuthi wona uze kimi ngokuphuma 
kwesikole sizoxoxa. Ngawubonisa nangengozi eyayingase ivele uma 
sithatha isikhathi sesikole sisisebenzise ekuxazululeni izinkinga. 
Okukhulu kunakho konke esikuzele lapha esikoleni yimfundo.” 

73 



Bahhahhama abantu bengeneliswa yincazelo kaMnguni. 
Ikhehla lejazi laqhweba insizwa eyayihlezi eduze kwalo lathi, 
“Ndodana, uyabona kodwa ukuthi lokhu komfana kulishinga 
umthetho wako?” 

“Ulisho ngaliphi lelo mkhulu?” kubuza insizwa. 

“Yini nje lena asitshela yona lo muntu? Ukhona umqondo kule 

nto ayishoyo?” 

“Phela mkhulu naye uchaza isizathu sokuteleka kwabafundi.” 

“We mfana, ngimdala uma ngingaka. Kudala ngiwadla 
amabele. Ngutsotsi lona. Akukho nto azixoshele yona lezi 
zingane.” Lisho bese lithula futhi ikhehla lapho selibona sengathi 
le nsizwa ayisakuthandi ukuxoxa nalo. Ilalele ukuqhubeka 
komhlangano. 

Kusenjalo kusukume umnumzane obukeka eyisifundiswa. Yena 
ubelokhu ebhala amaphuzu phansi uma kukhulunywa. Aqonde 
phambili. 

“Mphathimhlangano, ngingakaqhubeki nengithanda 
ukukusho, ngicela ukuzichaza ukuthi ngingubani. 
NginguMabanga, ummeli omkhulu lapha eMtshezi. UBen 
ofunda lapha esikoleni uyindodana yami. Ngisahlezi phansi 
ngikulalele uchaza, ngithanda ukukutshela ukuthi incazelo yakho 
ayingigculisi neze.” 

“Uyezwa-ke ndodana? Angithi uyezwa? Angishongo kuwena 
ukuthi incazelo yalo muntu ayenelisi?” kuhleba ikhehla lejazi 
ensizweni. 

“Yindlela naye azibona ngayo izinto uMabanga,” kuphendula 
insizwa isikhombisa ukucikeka yileli khehla elilokhu liyiphazamise 
njalo. 

“Lapho ngiyaphika ndodana. Akuyona indlela acabanga ngayo 
uMabanga. Ngumuntu womthetho lona ndodana. Awukho 
umthetho angawazi. Wayigogoda eyalapha kwelakithi waze 

74 



wayofunda neyangaphesheya kwezilwandle. Nakhona kuthiwa 
wayigogoda eyakhona. AmaBhunu alapha kwelakithi amesaba 
kabi ngoba kuthiwa uma esekhuluma isiNgisi umane asikhiphe 
ngamakhala. Ezinkantolo ukhuluma nabelungu abamhlophe 
qwa babhale kome amapensela. Uma icala liphethwe nguyena, 
uphendulana nejaji kushikishe ufudu enkantolo. Hhawu, uyothi 
ulibona ijaji lansondo libe seliluma ipensela yalo lapha ngemuva 
lingasazi ukuthi lizothini. Kwale khona-ke ukuthi liyivume 
engeqiwa ntwala ngoba nakhu empisholo uMabanga. Kodwa 
izethameli zecala ziba ngofakazi bokuthi lehluliwe ijaji. Ngumfo 
kaMabanga lowo ndodana.” Lisho lisineka isikhathi eside ikhehla 
kuvele izisini. 

Liphinde lilalele inkulumo kaMabanga ikhehla. Aqhubeke 
uMabanga. “Sebefikile abafundi kuwe njengobaba wabo bezobika 
izikhalo zabo, wakhombisa ukungabanaki. Wabatshela ukuthi 
kufanele bayofunda kuqala ngaphambi kokuba baxoxisane 
nawe. Konke lokhu kusakweneka obala ukuthi awubakhathalele 
abantwana bakho njengobaba wabo.” 

Aphinde athathe amandla uMabanga. Akhiphe iduku lakhe 
elimhlophe qwa ekhukhwini lebhantshi asule ubuso bese 
eqhubeka. “Ngicela ukubuza ukuthi mithetho mini owayinika 
uMkhandlu Omele Abafundi okufanele uyilandele uma uzothula 
izikhalo zabo?” 

“Ngingeze ngakwazi ukuyibalula ngokulandelana kwayo 
okwamanje ngoba angiyiphethe. Kodwa bayazi kahle abafundi.” 

“Mnumzane Mnguni, ngiqonde ukubuza ukuthi wawutsheliwe 
yini lo Mkhandlu ukuthi kufanele ulethe izikhalo zabafundi uma 
sekuphume isikole?” 

“Kunjalo Mhlonishwa,” kuphendula uMnguni. 

“Wazama yini ukuthola ukuthi kungani lo Mkhandlu weqe 
umthetho owanikwa wona?” 

75 



Abone manje uMnguni ukuthi ubhekene nezimbila zithutha 
nokwenza ziholwa ngemhlophe phambili. Nakhu phela 
empheka ngemibuzo ummeli wansondo kanti ubezitshela 
ukuthi uzobabamba kalula nje abazali. Waze wanekhanda 
elilukhuni lo mnumzane njengengane yakhe! Imibuzo yakhe 
ikhombisa ngokusobala ukuthi ungummeli ovuthiwe. Lapho-ke 
usemgqolozele emehlweni umfo kaMabanga ulindele impendulo. 

“Ngabe nginamanga Mhlonishwa wami uma ngingathi 
ngazama ukuthola lokho ngoba sasishayisana ngemibono 
nendodana yakho uBen futhi yaze yangisongela.” 

Liphinde liqhwebe insizwa ikhehla lejazi. “Bheka-ke ndodana, 
uyambona uThish’omkhulu wakho ukuthi wethukile? Akudlalwa 
kumfo kaMabanga. Mubheke emehlweni lo Thish’omkhulu 
ndodana. Yisigebengu sokuzalwa lesi. Ubecabanga ukuthi 
uzothatha kanye kwehlele lapha kithi ngoba nakhu singafundile.” 
Lisho ikhehla lihlalisisa esihlalweni ukuze liluzwe kahle lolu 
daba. Lithi ukusineka, liphothe ngezandla izinsansa zamadevu 
aqhephula inkomishi. 

Aqhubeke uMabanga ngemuva kokulalelisisa inkulumo 
kaMnguni. 

“Ngikubeka kuwe-ke Mnumzane Mnguni ukuthi nguwena 
kanye obe yimbangela yokuxoshwa kwezingane. Kwakufanele 
uwubuze kuqala uMkhandlu lowo ngembangela yokwephula 
kwawo umthetho wesikole. Kungenzeka ukuthi izinkinga 
ababenazo abafundi zazihambisana nezifundo zabo. Umthetho 
wezeMfundo uthi uma kunento ehlupha umfundi emoyeni, 
ikakhulukazi ephathelene nezemfundo, ayikho into azoyizwa 
lowo mfundi ekilasini. Ukuba khona kwakhe ekilasini kuzofana 
nokuthi akekho ngoba uzoba khona ngesiqu, angabibikho 
ngokomoya nangokwengqondo. Uma kunjalo-ke, sasingekho 
isidingo sokuba baye kofunda kuqala ngoba lokho kwakuzobe 
kungukudlala ngamandla othisha. Kufanele kulungiswe kuqala 

76 



izinkinga ngaphambi kokuba kuqalwe izifundo. Kwasakhona nje 
ukungawumemi lo Mkhandlu Omele Abafundi ukuba ube khona 
kulo mhlangano uzozethulela ubufakazi, kusakhomba khona 
ukuwubandlulula nokuwubukela phansi.” Isho incwansimende 
yakwabo maqede ihlale phansi igaxe umlenze phezu komunye. 
Ithi ukulungisa izibuko zayo kancane emehlweni bese iqhiyama 
esihlalweni ehlezi kuso. 

“Nsi! Ziyime emthumeni kuThish’omkhulu wakho ndodana,” 
kunyenyeza ikhehla lejazi ensizweni. “Zimpumpile kumkhulu 
wakho, mubheke kahle ukuthi wethuke kanjani. Kanti ubeqinisile 
lo mfana kaSokhela ukuthi akazi lutho lo muntu? Ayikho phela 
into eyaziwa yilo muntu wokuhamba. Akafundile enjalo nje. 
Yinye kuphela into ayaziyo. Wazi ukuthakatha nje. Akavele anike 
uSokhela isikhundla sakhe bese emuka.” 

Izizwe insizwa isiyithanda le ndaba yekhehla. “Akusona 
esikaSokhela lesi sikhundla mkhulu. USokhela uyisekela lale 
ndoda,” kuphawula insizwa imamatheka. 

Lagigitheka laze lagxumagxumisa izinyawo ikhehla. “Woshi 
mame! Lalela lapha-ke ndodana. Wena awazi lutho ngiyakubona. 
USokhela ungitshele ngezwa ngalezi ezami izindlebe izolo 
kusihlwa ngesikhathi ngiyombuza ngalo mhlangano. Uthe le 
ndoda yamhambela phambili yayogwazela umhloli ngemvu ukuze 
ayinike lesi sikhundla sokuphatha isikole. UChonco wahamba 
egcobe uSokhela. Kuthiwa lokho wakumemezela kothisha 
nasezinganeni imbala.” 

Liphazanyiswe wukushuba kwesimo ehholo ikhehla ngemuva 
kwenkulumo kaMabanga. Babodwa abase bemi ngezinyawo 
behlongoza ukuwushiya lo mhlangano. Babethi bashiyiswe 
imisebenzi yabo ebalulekile bazolaleliswa imbudane nje into 
engenakhanda namsila. Abanye babekhala ngokuphutha 
kwabo emihlanganweni yamasonto ngenxa yensumansumane 
imali yamakhanda. Isalukazi simbe sasilokhu sikhale njalo 

77 



ngamakhasimende aso esiqatha ayesezonqandeka nemali yaso 
ngenxa yalo mhlangano ongathi shu. Uma singekho ekhaya, 
akubi khona umuntu osidayisela isiqatha. 

UMnguni wayesethule ngaleso sikhathi ebeke izandla 
ezihlathini. Ingqondo yayimile. Kwaze kwasukuma uSihlalo 
woMkhandlu Omele Abazali, uNdukuzempi wakwaDlangalala 
phesheya kweNcintshana wancenga abazali ukuba bahlale phansi 
ukuze kuphethwe lolu daba. Nokho bazithoba bamlalela. Yena-ke 
wazama ukuwubuyisa umhlangano owawusuphumile ezandleni 
zikaMnguni ngokuba acele abazali ukuba baphume nekhambi 
lokuxazulula le nkinga yokuxoshwa kwabafundi. Kulapho-ke 
abavumelana khona ngazwi linye abazali ukuba kuthunyelwe 
abafundi esikoleni ngoMsombuluko ekuseni. 

USihlalo woMkhandlu wacela kubazali ukuba bazeluleke 
izingane zabo ukuba ziyihloniphe imithetho yesikole. 
Wahlakazeka umhlangano. 

UMnguni wavuka ngeSonto ekuseni washayela uMfundisi 
uDubazana ucingo wamazisa ngesimo esasimehlele esikoleni 
ngosuku olwedlule. 

“Kahle-ke mzalwane. Konje kungenzeka ukuthi lo thisha 
angitshela ngaye unkosikazi wakho ukuthi uyasifuna lesi 
sikhundla sokuphatha isikole, nguyena lona osekunyundele 
kubazali bezingane?” kubuza uMfundisi ngokusola okukhulu. 

“Cha, angiboni kanjalo Baba. Bebezokubeka lokho 
emhlanganweni abazali ukuba bebekade bengangifuni kulesi 
sikole. Manje into esixabanise ngempela nabo, yilena yokuxoshwa 
kwabafundi ngenxa yokushaya kwabo umduvo, bangayi 
emakilasini. Bona bakhala ngokuthi yimina engaba yimbangela 
yokuthi abantwana babo benze lo mkhuba.” 

“Hhayi-ke, uyangehlula mzalwane. Ngamanye amazwi 

78 



singasho ukuthi yidimoni leli elilwa nenhloso kaNkulunkulu 
yokukunika lesi sikhundla esihle kangaka!” 

“Impela Baba. Nami ngiyakubona lokho. Manje senginakho 
ukwesaba ukuthi akuzukugcina ngalokhu okungehlele. Lukhulu 
oluseza, luyanyelela. Wake wakuzwaphi Baba ukuthi umuntu 
athi efika nje esikoleni esisha ungakenziwa nomhlangano 
wokumethula kubazali, ahlangane nabo sekuliwa?” 

“Yima isibindi mzalwane. UNkulunkulu uzoba nawe. Akasoze 
akunikele ezandleni zomubi.” 

“Khona ngiyamethemba uNkulunkulu Baba. Yikhona-ke 
nje ukuthi kuke kumfikele umuntu ukudideka empilweni yize 
eyikholwa, ikakhulukazi uma ethi ubhula umlilo ngalapha uvuke 
ngalena.” 

“Yize kunjalo mzalwane, uNkulunkulu akehluleki. Yisivivinyo 
sesikhashana lesi, kodwa sizokwedlula. Sizokhuleka nabazalwane 
ize inqotshwe le mpi yomubi. Nawe mzalwane ungakhohlwa 
ukuzikhulekela.” 

Bayiphetha ingxoxo yabo oMnguni noMfundisi maqede 
zavaleka izingcingo. UMnguni wamfihlela uMaCele 
ngesimo ayehlangabezane naso emhlanganweni ngesikhathi 
emshayela ucingo ngemuva komhlangano. Wabe azi ukuthi 
babengezukuzwana ngemiqondo. 

79 



ISAHLUKO SESISHIYAGALOMBILI 

NgoMsombuluko ekuseni batheleka ngothi lwabo abafundi 
esikoleni. Kwamane kwachwaza nje emagcekeni esikole 
kubonakala ukuthi abafundi bayakuthokozela ukubuyela kwabo 
esikoleni. Babebingelelana, bexhawulana, behleka, kumnandi 
kudelile. Kwaze kwalamula yona insimbi eyayibabizela ehholo. 

Sebethandazile abafundi, wasondela kubona uMnguni. 

“Ngiyethemba ukuthi ukuhlala kwenu emakhaya 
kuyishintshile imiqondo yenu. Ngenxa yokungafuni kwenu 
ukuvula izindlebe uma ngikhuluma, nibonile-ke ukuthi nizithole 
senibhayiza kanjani? Namanje ngisaphinda futhi ngiyaniyala 
ngithi, qaphelani abakhohlisi ngoba bayizinyoka ezibulala 
ngobuthi. 

“Kunabantu okuthi lapho uhlola imisebenzi yabo yesikole 
ushaywe ngamahloni. Kuthi uma ubheka izenzo zabo uthole 
ukuthi zingcole njengokusebenza kwabo emakilasini. Labo 
bantu bahlala beyingozi ngaso sonke isikhathi ngoba bathi 
uma bebona ukuthi ikusasa labo lifiphele bese befaka abafundi 
abasebenza kahle umoya wezikhova. Lokho bakwenza ngenjongo 
yokufeza izinhloso zabo. Basuke bazi ukuthi ngeke kubonakale 
ukuthi bebekade bedlala uma kungezukubhala wonke umuntu 
ekupheleni konyaka. 

“Abanye baphuma emakhaya afudumele, banakho konke 
abakudingayo ezimpilweni zabo. Bazi kahle ukuthi uma 
isikole sivalwa unomphela, bazoqhubeka nokuziphilela kahle 
ngale kokukhathaza abanye abantu. Wena-ke uyalwazi usizi 
lwakini. Uyawazi umndeni ophuma kuwona ukuthi unjani. 
Uyazi nokuthi imali ofunda ngayo itholakala kanzima kanjani. 
Okufanele nikwazi ngukuthi baqashiwe laba bantu abanishayisa 
umduvo. Bahola imali ebomvu ngani. Baniphendula izikhali 

80 



zabo zokulwa ukuze badle basuthe. Manje-ke ngenxa yokuthi 
nani anifuni ukusebenzisa ubuchopho benu, nizithole senihlezi 
emakhaya ningazi ukuthi nihlaleleni. Kufanele kunikhanyele 
bha ukuthi nizokwenzani lapha. Anizanga ukuzoba ngamajaji 
nibone izinto ezingalungile. Anizanga futhi ukuzoba ngamathulisi 
ezigcwelegcwele. Nize ukuzofunda kuphela.” Adonse umoya umfo 
kaQwabe. 

USokhela wayesejuluke emanzi ngenxa yentukuthelo ihlangene 
novalo. Engani phela uMnguni wayesethinte indaba yabantu 
ababeqashwe ukufeza izinhloso zabanye. Konje kwakungenzeka 
nje ukuthi kwakukhona okuthile ayesekwazi uMnguni ngesu 
labo noNguzunga? Lokho kwakuzobe kuchaza ukuthi lo mfana 
waye wadakwa ngandlela thize wase ephahluka kubangani bakhe 
ngale ndaba. Phela uma kunjalo uzobe efe olwembiza uSokhela 
ngoba singagadla kuqala isitha athuke esexoshwa lapha esikoleni. 
Aphinde awuphebeze lo mcabango engqondweni yakhe uSokhela. 
Ngeke ayenze into enjalo uNguzunga. Ubemane esho nje 
uMnguni ngenhloso yokwethusa izingane. 

Aphinde aqhubeke uMnguni nenkulumo. “Kunamafomu 
enizonikezwa wona ukuba niwagcwalise. Wonke umfundi 
uzowagcwalisa. Akekho-ke umuntu ozozama ubugebengu obufile 
ngoba ngizowacwaninga wonke uma seniwagcwalisile ukuze 
ngiqinisekise ukuthi niwagcwalise nonke. Imibuzo ekuwona 
kufanele iphendulwe yonke bese kuthi ngezansi umfundi abhale 
igama lakhe nesibongo, ibanga alifundayo, usuku agcwalise 
ngalo ifomu bese kuthi ekugcineni uyasayina. Uma niqedile-ke 
nizobe seniwanika othisha benu ngokwamabanga eniwafundayo 
bese niphuthuma emakilasini.” Asho uMnguni maqede aphume 
ehholo aqonde ehhovisi lakhe. 

Kuse ngokunye manje kwabanye abafundi lapho sebegcwalisa 
lawa mafomu. Kubakhanyele ukuthi phela sebeyazibopha manje 
ukuze kuthi uma bephinda bebhikisha, baxoshwe unomphela. 

81 



Kube yilowo nalowo azitshele ukuthi noma bangathini oBen, 
uzobatshela kahle ukuthi yena akasayingeni le ndaba yabo ngoba 
kungenzeka ukuthi bona bayasebenza ngalokhu kubatelekisa 
kwabo. Nangomhla wombhikisho bathi angeke bahambe ngoba 
isikole ngesabo. Kodwa kwathi lapho sekufika amaphoyisa 
kukhala isibhaxu, bacela empunzini. Bona kanye labo ababezenza 
izihonga babaleka kuqala. 

UNguzunga wayengungqondongqondo. Ngesikhathi 
behlezi emakhaya wakucabanga ukuthi kungenzeka basayiniswe 
izincwajana ukubethusa. Pho-ke kuthuswe ubani ngoba yena 
uyibhubesi elichofoza konke okumi endleleni yalo? Noma 
angazama mzamo muni uMnguni ukuzilwela kodwa kuzogcina 
bona benoSokhela. Lesi kwakuyisifungo ayehlala esifunga nsuku 
zonke. 

Ekucabangeni kwakhe uNguzunga okwakungase kwenziwe 
nguMnguni kubafundi, wadala isu lokuwabhidliza wonke lawo 
macebo. Wayesekucabangile nokuthi abafundi bazokwethuswa 
bese bemela kude. Nebala kwenzeka njengoba ecabangile. 

Ngosuku lwesibili bebuyile abafundi esikoleni, uBen watshela 
uNguzunga ukuthi abafundi sebemtshelile ukuthi bayahoxa 
manje kule mpi yabo noMnguni. Lowo mbiko wadala ukuba 
uNguzunga ashayele uSokhela ucingo ngemuva kokuphuma 
kwesikole, amazise ngokubhuntsha kwesu lakhe lokuxosha 
uMnguni ngabafundi. 

“Manje ubona ukuthi kwenziwe njani ndodana?” kubuza 
uSokhela ocingweni. 

“Mina sengibona kungcono manje ukuba ngiwuqhube 
ngedwa lo msebenzi. Okubana nje ngukuthi usuzoba nzima 
kakhulu. Uhlale ukwazi-ke lokho ukuze singahluphani.” Washo 
uNguzunga eluvala ucingo engasavalelisanga. 

“Awu, usangene yini lo mfana? Ake nibheke nje ukuthi 

82 



wenzani. Usevala ucingo ngingakaphenduli. Khona la mazwi athi, 
angihlale ngazi ukuze singahluphani, asho ukuthini? Yini lena 
engehlelayo bakithi?” 

Wasala njalo edidekile uSokhela. Wayengasayiqondi neze 
ingqondo eyabe idlalwa yilo mfana. Yayidida ngisho nezihlakaniphi. 

UNguzunga wathi angaluvala ucingo, wasuka waqonda kuBen 
wafike wamchazela ngesu ayeselicabangile nelalizodinga bona 
bobabili. Babengasadingekile abanye abafundi. Okubuhlungu nje 
ngukuthi uBen wayengazi ukuthi wayezobe elekelela uNguzunga 
emsebenzini wakhe owawuzomnika imali. Yena wayecabanga 
ukuthi babesaqhuba ngokwezikhalo zabo kanti useshaye phansi. 
Bheka-ke ngoba baze benza izifungo ezinzulu zokuthi uma 
omunye phakathi kwabo eboshwa, uzoba yisimungulu. Ngeke 
amdalule osele ukuze asale ezama izindlela zokukhulula oboshiwe 
etilongweni. 

Lokhu kwamnika isibindi uBen ngoba wayesohlwini 
lwababengaxoshwa. Akakhohlwanga ethole umuntu 
omkhathalelayo. Bavumelana noNguzunga ngokuthi bazobhala 
uqwembe olukhulu balunameke esicabheni sehhovisi likaMnguni. 
Kulolu qwembe kwakuzolotshwa ukuthi: 

“Ngenxa yokuqinisa kwakho ikhanda uzenza ukhandalensimbi 
ngokwesabisa abafundi lapho belwela amalungelo abo, kusukela 
namuhla uyaziswa ukuthi ususalelwe yizinsuku ezintathu 
kuphela ubonakala emagcekeni akulesi sikole. Sesiphelile isineke 
sokukubekezelela. Uma uqhubeka nokuqinisa ikhanda, uzohamba 
usuya emakhazeni. Ungalokothi wazise amaphoyisa ngalolu daba 
ngoba uzokufa nokufa!” 

Ngezansi kwalawa mazwi kwakuzodwetshwa umuntu 
odutshulwayo nokwakuzobe kuchaza isimo esasizolandela uma 
uMnguni eqhubeka nokuqinisa ikhanda. Waqalwa-ke umsebenzi. 

Ngemuva kokuphothulwa komsebenzi, uNguzunga wayala 

83 



uBen ukuba asale elunameka lolu qwembe phakathi kwamabili 
ebusuku. Wahamba. 

Nangempela waluthatha uBen uqwembe wayolunameka 
ehhovisi likaMnguni sebelele bonke abantu. Wenza isiqiniseko 
sokuthi akabonwa muntu. 

Ngakusasa ekuseni uMnguni wawotha ubomvu uma efica 
uqwembe olumsongelayo ehhovisi lakhe. Waluthatha waqonda 
nalo ehholo wafike wacela uMkhandlu Omele Abafundi 
ngokushesha, waqonda nawo ehhovisi lakhe. Kwaba wukungena 
nje wahlala phezu kwalo udaba. 

“Nginibiza nje ngoba ngifuna ukunikhumbuza ukuthi 
njengoba nilapha esikoleni, nizofunda. Anizanga ukuzokhombisa 
ubuhlongandlebe benu. Anizanga nokuzokhombisa abathile 
ukuthi ninezikhali zokulwa ezinamandla kangakanani.” Asho 
uMnguni ebeka uqwembe olumsongelayo phezu kwetafula. 
“Fundani lapha!” Asho esukuma esihlalweni umfo kaQwabe afake 
izandla emakhukhwini ebhulukwe. 

Wakufunda uMkhandlu okwakubhalwe oqwembeni maqede 
wakhombisa ukukhathazeka okukhulu. Kwawukhathaza 
kakhulu ukubona umdwebo obuhlungu kangaka! UMnguni 
wakuqaphela ukuthi uBen wayengakushayi mkhuba konke lokhu 
okwakwenzekile kanti vele wayemsolile. 

“Angifuni-ke ukulokhu ngikhuluma kakhulu. Ngizoyiqeda 
nya yonke le nto. Ngiyabona ukuthi lesi sikole sesithanda 
ukuphunyuka ezandleni zami. Lokho kuzokwenzeka ngifile. 
Ngiyazi ukuthi amanye amalungu alo Mkhandlu wenu anolwazi 
ngale nto. Ngifuna ukuthi niphindele emakilasini khona manje. 
Wena Ben ungahambi, ngisafuna ukuxoxa nawe.” 

Bushintshe ubuso bukaMnguni. Bushintshe nobukaBen. 
Baphume abanye bengakuqondi okwakwenzeka phakathi 
kukaMnguni noBen. 

84 



“Ben, angithandi ukuthi sixabane noma ulahlekelwe yisikole. 
Kumanje nje usohlwini lwabangaxoshwa noma yinini lapha 
esikoleni. Manje-ke ngifuna ukuba ukhulume lonke iqiniso 
okomuntu efa. Angifuni ukuthi senzane izilima.” Asho abuyise 
izinhlonze umfo kaQwabe ukwethusa uBen. “Ngifuna ungitshele 
kahle ukuthi wazini ngale nto?” 

“Angazi lutho Thish’omkhulu.” 

“Besengishilo njalo ukuthi angithandi ukwenziwa 
isiphukuphuku. Ngimdala kabi ukuthi ngingadlala umacashelana 

nawe. Ngubani owenze le nto Ben?” 

Athule uBen abheke phansi. 

“Umthetho wakhona ngikhuluma nomuntu noma 

ngikhuluma nezindonga zale ndlu?” 

Azithulele nje uBen. 

Asukume uMnguni efuthekile ahlale izithonto phezu kukaBen. 
Amgxavule ngezingubo entanyeni. “Ufuna ukubonani wena 
mfana?” Amxukuzise ngezingubo. Aqhubeke uBen nokuyihlaba 
inhlali. 

Ngaleso sikhathi kuthi akafe uMnguni. Nakhu edelelwa 
yingane madoda! Ize imehlise isithunzi impela nje? “Uma 
ungafuni ukuvula lo mlonyana wakho, ngizophoqeka ukuba 
ngikufake indlela. Ungithola kahle Ben?” 

“Ngifanele ukuthula Thish’omkhulu. Wena ulindele ukuthi 
ngithini uma ungehla ngale ndlela? Okokuqala nje angazi lutho 
ngale nto. Angazi-ke ukuthi kufanele ngithini ngoba ngiyasoleka.” 
Amdedele uMnguni. 

“Uthini mfana?” 

“Sengishilo.” 

“Yimihlola yamaQwabe yini? Ukhuluma nobani kanjalo 

wena?” 

85 



“Kanti ngikhuluma nobani Thish’omkhulu ngoba ngithi 
sisobabili lapha endlini? Angithi ubadedele laba abanye 
bayofunda, wangibamba mina ukuze ungifake le mibuzo yakho 
engasile? Angazi-ke ukuthi usafunani kimi ngoba ungibonile 
phela ngikwenza lokho.” 

“We mfana ndini! Ngithi we mfanakazana! Ake ungishiye 
kancane. Phuma lapha ehhovisi lami ngingaze ngikushaye 
ngesibhakela. Phuma!” 

Afulathele uBen bese enxapha. 

Wo, kwabe useyinyathele emsileni imamba yalukile. Agxume 
uMnguni avale isicabha. “Unxaphela bani wena mfana? Ngibuza 
ukuthi unxaphela bani lowo oyinja yakho?” Asho esakaza 
uBen ngempama aye ayofumbeka phansi kudume opotiyane 
ezindlebeni. 

“Vuka uzibambe ziqine bhoklolo ndini! Angithi usuyindoda? 
Uyangibhodlela nginguThish’omkhulu wakho? Uyizambane 
elibolile wena mfana kaMabanga! Phuma lapha ehhovisi lami!” 
kusho uMnguni emfaka unyawo. 

Aphume uBen engxame efile. Asale uMnguni ethatha ebeka. 
Kufike umcabango wokuba ambizele amaphoyisa lo mfana. 
Nakanjani uzolikhipha lonke iqiniso alibeke lapha. Azoyiqeda 
nya lenkanyana anayo. Uma eqhubeka nale ngqonjwana yakhe 
yokudaza inkani, uzoboshwa. Maye, kuyahlupha ukuphatha 
izingane zabantu abaqhakambisa izikhundla zabo ngoba nazo 
zisuke zifuze bona! Phela lo mfana uluhlaza njengoyise. Naye 
akazikhohliwe ehlakaniphile ukwedlula bonke abameli emhlabeni. 

Angabe esachitha sikhathi uMnguni, avele ahlale phezu 
kwezintambo zabelungu abize amaphoyisa aseLoskop. 
Awendlalele lonke udaba. Kuthi nalapho ethanda ukwazi 
amaphoyisa ukuthi yena usola ubani, avele akubeke ngaphandle 
kokunanaza ukuthi usola uBen Mabanga. 

86 



Asukumela phezulu amaphoyisa ayokwenza uphenyo. UBen 
wezwa esebizwa ngombhobho ebizelwa ehhovisi likaMnguni. 
Wathi engena nje ehhovisi wazithela phezu kwamadoda amabili 
omthetho. Amthatha ayomphenyela emotweni kahulumeni. 
Abukhipha bonke ubuciko bokuphenya amaphoyisa kodwa 
ahluleka ukuthola iqiniso. UBen waphendula ngelithi 
wayengeke ayenze into enjalo ngoba babesayiniswe imithetho 
enzima ngemuva kokushaya kwabo umduvo. Washo nokuthi 
le nto yokusongela uThish’omkhulu yayenziwe ngumuntu 
owayenekhanda elingathathi kahle. Umuntu onjengaye 
nonengqondo ekhaliphile ubengeke akwenze lokhu. Amdedela 
amaphoyisa. Amtshela ukuthi asazoqhubeka nokumphenya. 

UMnguni akumgculisanga neze ukubona amaphoyisa eyeka 
isitha sakhe angasibophi. Lokho kwawushintsha kwawuqeda 
umqondo wakhe. Wabiza uBen ngokushesha wamtshela ukuthi 
kuyodingeka ukuba ame ukuza esikoleni buze buvele ubufakazi 
bokuthi akanacala. Wake wazama ukuzabalaza uBen kodwa 
akaphumelelanga. Wamane wabizelwa onogada bamkhipha 
ngesibhaxu emagcekeni esikole. 

Esezwile uNguzunga ngokuxoshwa kukaBen, wazimisela 
ukuba aye kovakashela uMnguni ebusuku lapho ayehlala khona. 
Wazitshela ukuthi ngeke amnike ngisho nelincane ithuba. 
Wayezomfunda amqonde ngalobo busuku. Wayezoyeswela le 
motshwana yakhe kanokusho. 

Ngabo lobo busuku uNguzunga watheleka ngezinkani 
eNgonyameni lapho ayehlala khona uMnguni. Wakhipha 
isaha lensimbi wasaha isango maqede washo ngaphakathi. 
Wayesekhipha uxhaxha lokhiye wayigwedla imoto kaMnguni yaze 
yavuleka. Washo phezulu. Wakhumula ibhuleki lesandla, yahlehla 
yaze yayophuma ngesango ngoba igceke laliqethukile. Kwasuka 
amaphepha. 

Ngakusasa ekuseni akawakholwanga amehlo akhe uMnguni 

87 



uma ebona igceke licwebile. Lwamshaya uvalo lwamgeqa 
amadolo. Isishonephi-ke imoto? Wabona kahle ukuthi 
kwakuyimisebenzi yomfana kaMabanga yonke lena. Wabona 
kungcono ukuba ayibikele amaphoyisa le ndaba. 

Esiteshini samaphoyisa kwakuhlezi uKaputeni ekhuluma 
yedwa. “Impela kunzima lapha emnyango. Kuliqiniso elimsulwa 
ukuthi ngiphethe isiteshi esingenamaphoyisa. ONgubane bagabise 
izihhanqahhanqa zamakhanda agcwele utshwala. Ubuchopho 
abukho ngempela. Utshwala phambili; umsebenzi ngemuva. 
Angikaze ngisibone isidwedwe sikaSayitsheni esiyisigqila 
sotshwala ngale ndlela. Umuntu usuke emuhle kuNgubane 
uma ekhuluma ngotshwala. Ngiyazisa ngalowo owamnika lesi 
sikhundla. Asimfanele nakancane nje. Laze lahlupheka naleli 
phoyisa elinguZondo ngokuphathwa yileli saka likaSayitsheni. 
Awukho umsebenzi elizowufunda kulesi silima. Kwakuyoba 
ngcono ukuba kwakhushulwa lona laba nguSayitsheni ngoba 
linekhanda elingconywana. 

“Nsuku zonke sithola izingcingo ezivela kubantu bekhala 
ngobelelesi obudla umunyu kule ndawo. Bashiselwa imizi 
ebusuku, bathathelwa izimoto, bayabulawa kodwa umthetho 
ukhona. Zolo lokhu uThish’omkhulu waseBonokuhle kade 
esongelwa yizigebengu ezingaziwa. Ziphi zona lezo zigebengu 
ngoba kumanje nje akukho noyedwa umuntu oseke walethwa 
phambi kwenkantolo? Kwasalo mfana osolekayo uwehlulile 
amaphoyisa. Yikhona kanye lokhu okuweneka obala ukuthi 
ayizidwedwe eziphindwe kalishumi. Kwake kwenzekaphi ukuthi 
amaphoyisa alethelwe umsolwa bese wona ehluleka ukumklinya 
ngemibuzo aze amgojele? Impela ngiyoyizekela amagwababa 
echobana le ndaba.” 

Athukuthele uKaputeni kuthi akazisakaze phansi uma 
ekhumbula ukuthi wayezixhakathisa kanjani izigebengu ngisho 

88 



sekuthiwa akuyi lubuyayo kuzo. Akukho ngisho nesisodwa 
kwezazilandelwa nguye esake saphunyuka. Wayesilandela 
isigebengu esehlehle onke amaphoyisa. Ekugcineni asibambe. 
Azisabalwa-ke izindondo ayeklonyeliswa ngazo ngomsebenzi 
oncomekayo ayewenza. 

Esathukuthele kanjalo uKaputeni, kukhale ucingo. 

“Kusesiteshini samaphoyisa, ngingakusiza?”

Amaphoyisa alwa nesu lokunqoba le nkinga eyayibhekene

Ngabo lobo busuku obulandela obezimanga, ubuthongo

nangomonakalo owawudaleke esikoleni. Wamchazela nokuthi 
lonke udaba lwase lusezandleni zamaphoyisa. 

Kwathi lapho embuza uMaCele ukuthi wayesewabikele yini 
amaphoyisa ngoSokhela, walandula. Wathi lokho kwakuzodala 
ukuba amaphoyisa asole uSokhela angabe esabaphenya 
nabanye abantu kanti yena wayengenaso isiqiniseko sokuthi 
kwakunguyena owayengumenzi walo monadalo. 

Le mpendulo kaMnguni yamthukuthelisa kakhulu uMaCele. 
Wamane waluvala ucingo maqede wanikela kwaMfundisi 
eyomnxusa ukuba akhulume noMnguni amkhuthaze ukuba 

100 



abikele amaphoyisa ngalo thisha ongamthandi. Naye futhi 
uMfundisi wahamba emazwini kaMnguni. Wathi ngumkhuleko
