wamane waphelelwa ngamandla, waphindela ekhaya edumele. 

“Sekuphikelele ukusa ngiqwashile. Yimina lo osephenduke 
ibhola lezelelesi ngale ndlela? Angisenamoto, ihhovisi lishile, 
unogada ubulewe, nasemhlanganweni bathi abangidle bangifele 
abazali bezingane. Kanti konakelephi ngempela?” 

Athule uMnguni abuyise esinye isehlakalo esike samehlela 
ekuseni ngesikhathi eya emsebenzini. Kuleso sehlakalo ufunde 
ukuthi kwesinye isikhathi impilo iphikwa yiqiniso, uyibone 
isifana namafu amhlophe abukeka emahle futhi engenasici. 
Okuthi athi emahle kodwa abonakale esenyelela kancane 
esibhakabhakeni njengesela eyozishutheka ngaphansi kwamafu 
amnyama khwishi avutha ulaka lwezikhukhula. Bese kuthi nawo 
lawa amahle agcine esephelelwe wubuhle bawo kanye nomusa 
abheje ulaka. 

“Kodwa lo mfana wethekisi ubengizwa ukunuka yini? 
Ngempela yashonaphi inhlonipho kulowa sikhotheni ebengigibele 
kuye? Wangihlukumeza umfana waze wangehlisa impela nje 
ethekisini lakhe ngenxa yemali ehlangene. Cha, yibhadi elixakile 
phela leli. Akathandanga ukulalela ngisho sengimchazela 
ukuthi akahambe nayo yonke le mali, uzongibuyisela ushintshi 
uma esewutholile. Impela kubuhlungu ukungabi nemoto 
nokwenza ube unesikhundla esihloniphekile emphakathini. 
Kuba sengathi nabantu bakujezisela kona lokho. Ngiyambonga 
uthisha uMazibuko ngokungicosha sengilaxazwe esibakabakeni. 
Bengizoba yini kodwa kulesiya sibhabhadlolo sokushisa kwelanga 
njengoba eyindlala nje namathekisi adlula eBonokuhle? 
Besengibona kahle ukuthi kuzodingeka ukuba ngibambe wona 
la mathekisi aya eZakhiweni bese ngehla eGothoni. Laphoke 
bengizoyincenga kancane indlela ngezinyawo ngize ngifike 

101 



esikoleni. Ngibonga nokuthi uMazibuko azinikele ekutheni 
uzongilanda nsuku zonke ekuseni lapha ekhaya aphinde 
angibuyise ngemuva kokuphuma kwesikole. Kodwa phela nesoka 
alikaze lidle kahle imbangi ikhala. 

“Khona kufanele ukuba ngizilindele izilingo njengoba 
ngisesikhundleni nje. Yebo, ngiyavuma ukuthi zinzima futhi 
zithanda ukuba ngenhla kwamadolo. Kodwa akuyona into 
esenhliziyweni yami ukushiya eBonokuhle. Ngisazoqhubeka 
nokuyibamba ishisa injalo le nsimbi. Ngifunga ngiyagomela 
ukuthi angisoze ngiyivumele intando yomuntu ukuba yenzeke.” 

Wathatha wabeka uMnguni ezinika isibindi sokuthi 
uzoyinqoba le mpi, waze wazunywa wubuthongo. 

102 



ISAHLUKO SESISHIYAGALOLUNYE 

Ukufa kukanogada kanye nokusha kwehhovisi likaMnguni 
kwabaphatha kabi abazali bezingane. Babebona isikole 
esasihlonishwa kakhulu eLoskop sivuma phansi. Abanye babesola 
uMnguni bethi uyehluleka ukusebenzisana nabafundi. Ufuna 
ukuhlala njalo engundlovu kayiphikiswa. 

Ikhehla lejazi nalo lalingazibekile phansi. Laliphuma lingena 
nemizi linxenxa izakhamizi ukuba zilusukumele lolu daba 
lukaMnguni. Lalithi ukuba amadoda alusukumela ngosuku 
lomhlangano wabalimi, ngabe akuzange kwenzeke konke lokhu 
okwase kwenzekile esikoleni. Lona ngokwalo lalifisa ukuthi 
amadoda endawo asukume ayombonga uMnguni eMnyangweni 
wezeMfundo bese ewunxusa ukuba ugcobe umfana wendawo. 

Abantu abayi nganxanye bengemanzi. Phezu kwazo zonke lezi 
zinsolo nemibono ngoMnguni, babekhona labo ababevumelana 
nezenzo zakhe. Babekubeka ngokusobala nasekhehleni lejazi 
ukuthi uMnguni wayengenacala. Indaba yayinabafundi. 
Babebagxeka bethi yibona ababengafuni ukufunda, befuna 
ukuziphatha. Bona babengabathumelanga esikoleni ukuba 
bayoba ngamabhoklolo bashayele othisha imithetho. Babebabaza, 
bekhuza umhlola bethi, babengakaze bakubone okunjena. 
Njengasiphi isikole esadedela abafundi ukuba bazenzele 
umathanda qede zonke izinto zahamba kahle? 

Babekhona nabanye ababelimisa ngesihloko elithi izingane 
zabo zazimncoma kakhulu uMnguni zithi uhlala elwela ukuba 
zifunde. Umuntu ezazimhlaba kakhulu kwakunguyena umfo 
kaGambushe okuthiwa wayengakukhathalele neze ukufunda 
kwazo. Wayekhathalela umndeni wakhe kuphela. Ezakhe izingane 
zazifunda ezikoleni zabelungu, zisikhipha ngamakhala isiNgisi. 

Othisha nabo sasibakhathaze kakhulu lesi simo esase 

103 



sidunge isikole esihle kangaka saphenduka inkundla yokufa. 
Nakubona ukudideka kwakubhalwe ebusweni. Kwase 
kujwayelekile ukuthi isikole sishiywe sisesimweni esifanele, kuthi 
ngakusasa sificwe sesikwesinye. Lalingashoni lingenazindaba 
zalo eBonokuhle. USokhela yena wayekhululekile emoyeni. 
Emphakathini wayekubeka kucace ukuthi lo Thish’omkhulu 
omusha wayehluleka ukuphatha isikole. Nokho wayengakuvezi 
ukuthi naye wayesigaqele lesi sikhundla sokuphatha isikole. 
Kwakuyikhehla lejazi kuphela elalikwazi lokho. Nalo labe lazi 
ukuthi wephucwe isikhundla sakhe. 

Ngalezo zinsuku wayengaphumuli uSokhela yizingcingo 
ezazivela kuNguzunga emazisa ngokuqhubeka komsebenzi. 
Wayengakhohlwa uNguzunga ukubeka ngokusobala ukuthi 
lo msebenzi wawunzima kakhulu kunokuwucabanga kwakhe. 
Wayekugcizelela njalo nokuthi ucela ukuba bangahluphani uma 
sebekhokhelana. 

Ezinsukwini ayenqunyelwe zona uMnguni ngabantu 
abangaziwa, kwase kusele olulodwa vo ngesikhathi evuswa 
wucingo kusempondozankomo. 

“Yebo-ke Mnumzane, kwakuhle ngakuthola. Ngiludinga 
kakhulu usizo lwakho,” kusho indoda ngale ocingweni. 

“Ngubani engikhuluma naye?” kubuza uMnguni evuka, ehlala 
ngezinqe embhedeni. 

“Akufuni wena-ke lokho. Yinye kuphela into engifuna 
ungenzele yona. Angikuceli futhi angikuncengi. Ngifuna ukuthi 
uyenze uthanda ungathandi.” Yasho ngokugcizelela indoda. 

“Nanti ibhadi lami bo!” 

“Kahle-ke ndoda! Ungalokothi uphazame. Akukhulunywa 
nami kanjalo. Ukhumbule futhi ukuthi awukhulumi nomkakho. 
Zama-ke ukucwecwa amazwi akho ndoda ndini!” 

“Nx!” Aluvale ucingo uMnguni. “Waze wangeyisa umuntu 

104 



nokwenza ngingamazi nakumazi. Aze angivuse ekuseni kangaka 
pho angivusele ukungeyisa? Bhadi lini kodwa leli elingehlelayo 
bakithi?” 

Lukhale futhi ucingo. Aqale anqikaze ukuluphendula 
uMnguni. Acabange ukuthi uzothi uyaluphakamisa aphinde 
ahlangane nale ndoda eyeyisayo. Nokho ugcine umehlulile 
umqondo othi kuzomele aluphendule lolu cingo ngoba 
kungenzeka ukuthi akuselona oluvela kulo muntu angamazi. 
Aluphakamise. 

“Yeyi wena sithutha ndini! Thela amafutha ensimango 
ezindlebeni zakho yikhona uzokuzwa kahle. Uma uke waphinda 
waluvala lolu cingo, angeke iphele imizuzu emihlanu ngingakafiki 
lapho. Lokho kuzobe sekuchaza ukuthi usuyehlukana nokudla 
amabele,” kusonga indoda ngokukhulu ukungancengi. 

Lumdukluze uvalo uMnguni. Iqhubeke indoda. 

“Nakhu-ke engifuna ungenzele khona. Ngiyethemba 
usakhumbula ukuthi kusasa wusuku lwakho lokugcina 
ukubonakala emagcekeni aseBonokuhle. Ngiyazi-ke ukuthi ngeke 
uhambe ngoba unenkani yeselesele. Ngiyazi futhi ukuthi uthi 
awuyi ndawo, ungamane uhambe uyisidumbu. Ngiyabubonga 
ubuqhwaga bakho ndoda yamadoda. Ngiyabona ucabanga ukuthi 
ukufa kufana nokukhamisa nje ehhovisi ungenzi lutho, uhlalele 
ukubhaxabulana nezingane ngemvubu njengezimbongolo. 
Nokho mina ngadaleka kahle. Anginalo unya njengawe. 
Ngiyayikhathalela impilo yabanye abantu. Nginesihe nginjalo 
nje. Yingakho ngibone kungcono ukuba ngikushayele ucingo 
ngikwazise ukuthi ngizofika lapho kusasa ngehora lesithathu 
ntambama. Ngifuna ukukweluleka ukuze uhambe kahle usaphila. 
Nakanjani kufanele ushiye kulesiya sikole. Ungalingi ubize 
amaphoyisa ukuba azokuqapha ngoba uzobe usuzimbela igodi 
usaphila. Kuyezwakala?” 

105 



“Kuyezwakala mfowethu,” kuphendula uMnguni sekubhakuza 
isifuba ngenxa yovalo. 

Walubeka phansi ucingo uNguzunga. Wasala elubambile 
ngalena uMnguni ezimukelwe yikhanda. 

“Nakho-ke okukhulu. Ngimane ngisongelwe ngumuntu 
engingamazi kalula kanjalo nje? Kakade uyithathephi inombolo 
yocingo lwami? Konje kufanele ngenze njani? Ngiwabikele 
amaphoyisa? Uma le ndoda isikuzwa lokho ngizothi webani, 
asabele kuphi? Impela sengiyezwa manje ukuthi siyashisa lesi 
sihlalo engihlezi kuso. Ziyangishuka izinkinga. Okubi nje 
ngukuthi kubukeka kunabantu abacashile nabangemuva kwayo 
yonke le nto. Ngeshwa angibazi ukuthi bangobani. Namaphoyisa 
akule ndawo ayehluleka ukubathola. Khona ngiyavuma ukuthi 
uSokhela uyisitha sami kodwa manje angikwazi ukumbeka icala 
ngithi unesandla kule nto. Anginabo ubufakazi obuphathekayo 
ngalokho. Umuntu engimsola kakhulu enhliziyweni yami 
nguyena lo mfana wakwaMabanga. Kodwa futhi ngivele 
ngidideke kakhulu ngaye ngoba amaphoyisa ayehluleka 
ukumthola enecala.” 

Limdumele ngamandla ikhanda uMnguni. Lezi zinto 
ezazenzeka esikoleni zaziwubufakazi bokuthi wayehlezi phezu 
kwegeja lishisa. Into eyayingase imsize kukho konke lokhu, 
wukuba abone eze ngayo. Manje-ke yena wayencamela ukufa 
kunokuba adlale abantu angabazi bamlahlise isikhundla ayesifuna 
iminyakanyaka. 

Esacabange kaningana uMnguni ngale ndaba yokwesatshiswa 
kwakhe ngocingo, wanquma ukuba athinte amaphoyisa awazise 
ngalokhu. “Cha, ngeke ngidlale izigebengu mina. Kunini 
zangiqala? Ngizowashayela impela nje amaphoyisa ucingo 
ngiwacele ukuba azongiqapha. Ngiyethemba ukuthi asekhona 
onke emsebenzini manje. Sekusile.” 

106 



Walushaya ucingo uMnguni walubika udaba lwakhe 
kuKaputeni. Walwendlala kwabonakala ukuthi ukhathazekile 
futhi uyawadinga kakhulu amaphoyisa kule ngxaki yakhe. 

Ngesikhathi ekhuluma uMnguni, uKaputeni wayethatha ebeka 
ngengqondo engazi ngempela ukuthi uzomphendula athini. Phela 
selokhu wawabikela amaphoyisa ngesimo saseBonokuhle, akukho 
okugculisayo aseke akwenza la maphoyisa akhe ukuvikela isikole 
nomphakathi waso. Kunokuba izinto ziye ngokuba ngcono, 
konke kwamane kwakhombisa ukubisha nje. 

Kwathi lapho eseqedile ukukhuluma uMnguni, kwavele 
kwathuleka ocingweni. Lokho kwamdida kakhulu wangabe esazi 
ukuthi kwenzekani. Kwamthatha imizuzwana impela uKaputeni 
andukuba aphendule. 

“Eyi, ngiyezwa Qwabe. Ngiyasizwa nesicelo sakho mfowethu. 
Ukhuluma nje ngizibuza ngiyaziphendula ukuthi kazi yini lena 
owazidlela yona lezi zigebengu njengoba zikuphilisa impilo 
ebuhlungu kangaka?” 

“Umbuzo wakho ufana nalona engihlala ngizibuza wona nami. 
Ngeshwa-ke akekho ongichazelayo ukuze ngicacelwe. Kimi impilo 
isiphenduke isihogo uqobo lwaso. Angikutholi ukuphumula. 
Okunzima kakhulu yikhona ukuthi angibazi laba bantu abagila 
lo mkhuba. Nomuntu engimsolayo usesitokisini. Ngabe ngithi 
nguyena lona ongisongelayo.” 

“Mina Qwabe, ngizizwa nginamahloni ngale nto eyenzeka 
empilweni yakho. Ukuba kuya ngami ngabe sikhuluma nje 
zigcwele esitokisini izelelesi. Manje akunjalo. Inkinga esinayo 
ngukuthi sibhekene nongqondongqondo, imigulukudu emidala. 
Indaba yomfana kaMabanga iphathisana ngekhanda. Ukuboshwa 
kwakhe akusiniki umkhondo wezigebengu. Kodwa-ke mfowethu, 
lokho akuchazi ukuthi akanacala. Okwesibili akuchazi ukuthi 
nathi asiwenzi umsebenzi kumbe sesihlulekile. Sisazoqhubeka 

107 



nokumphenya size saneliseke ukuthi ngempela umsulwa. Khona 
kungenzeka ukuthi uxhumene ngandlela thize nalezi zigebengu 
esingakwazi ukuzithola.” 

“Lonakele izwe bakithi. Sithi sifundisa izingane kanti sifundisa 
izigebengu.” 

Bayixoxa eyezigebengu oMnguni noKaputeni bagcina 
bengafikanga ndawo. UKaputeni wagcina ethembise uMnguni 
ukuthi uzomthumelela amaphoyisa ukuba azomgada. Nebala 
wawathumela ngokushesha. Ahamba naye uMnguni ukuya 
esikoleni emgadile. 

Waqhubeka ngokujwayelekile umsebenzi esikoleni uMnguni 
egadwe ngamaphoyisa. Kwakungavunyelwe muntu ongaziwa 
ukuba angene ehhovisi lakhe engazange aphenywe kabanzi 
ukuthola ukuthi wayengeyona ingozi. Nalapho esededelwe 
lowo muntu ukuba ayoxoxa naye, wayephelekezelwa ngelinye 
lamaphoyisa liyomngenisa ehhovisi likaMnguni. 

UMnguni wayematasatasa ehhovisi lakhe ngesikhathi 
kukhala ucingo. Waluphakamisa. “KuseBonokuhle, nguMnguni 
okhulumayo, ngingakusiza?” 

“Ngiyakubingelela Mnumzane Mnguni. Ngummeli uMabanga 
lona okhuluma naye.” 

Lumuthi heqe uvalo uMnguni. Adonse kakhulu umoya 
aphinde awudedele. “Ngiyavuma Mhlonishwa. Sakhunjulwa 
abantu bomthetho namhlanje, kwenzenjani?” kubuza uMnguni 
ngezwi eliqhaqhazelayo. Wabe azi kahle kamhlophe ukuthi 
kwakumayelana noBen. 

“Yizinkinga mfo kaMnguni. Ngikushayela nje ngifuna ukwazi 
ukuthi njengoba unikele ngengane yami nje emaphoyiseni, 
unesiqiniseko esingakanani ukuthi iyona eyimbangela yalo 
monakalo owenzeka esikoleni sakho?” 

Adonse umoya futhi uMnguni bese ewudedela. “Anginaso 

108 



isiqiniseko Mhlonishwa, kodwa indodana yakho yangisongela.” 
“Ngamanye amazwi uqonde ukungitshela ukuthi umntanami 

uboshwe njengomsolwa?” 

“Kunjalo Mhlonishwa.” 

“Okuchaza ukuthi kungenzeka ukuthi uboshelwe amahhala 

nje akanalo icala?” 

“Nakho lokho kungenzeka, kodwa…” 

“Cha, ungabe usaqhubeka ngoba sengiyitholile impendulo. 
Ngicela ukuthi ungizwe kahle Mnumzane Mnguni. Angiqondile 
ukuvuna umntanami, kodwa ngithanda ukuthi izinto zihambe 
ngeqiniso. Uma kungukuthi uBen utholakala enecala, 
kufanele ajeze ngokona kwakhe. Kodwa-ke uma inkantolo 
imthola engenacala, ngiyonibopha nibolele ejele ngoba niyobe 
nimhlambalazile namlahlekisela nangethuba lokufunda. 
Njengoba ebhadle esitokisini nje uyasala ezifundweni zakhe. 
Mina ngokwami angimazi uBen eyihlongandlebe njengoba 
nimchaza nina. UBen ngimazi eyingane ehloniphayo neziphethe 
kahle. Kuphela nje akezwani nokuxhashazwa aphathiswe 
okwembongolo. Uyawazi amalungelo akhe njengesakhamuzi 
saseNingizimu-Afrika.” 

Ajuluke uMnguni ocingweni. Ludlale ngaye uvalo. Phela 
uMabanga uyaziwa ukuthi akalibheki icala. Kusobala ukuthi 
uzoyilwela indodana yakhe kuze kube sekugcineni. Kuyoba nzima 
kakhulu uma kuke kwatholakala ukuthi iboshelwe amahhala, 
ayinacala. Uyobaphendula ibhola uMabanga abakhiphe yonke 
inkanyana lena. 

Aphinde afikelwe wukuthukuthela uMnguni uma esewahlaziya 
kahle amazwi kaMabanga. Bekunani athule abone kuqala ukuthi 
igcinaphi indodana yakhe. Ngemuva kwalokho azithathe-ke 
izinyathelo zomthetho uma kungukuthi itholwa ingenacala. 
Kuwubulima nje ukusukeleka usongele abantu ngento ongenaso 

109 



isiqiniseko sayo. Sekusobala manje ukuthi kungumkhuba 
wakwaMabanga ukusongela abantu. 

Akhumbule uMnguni ukuthi usalubambile ucingo. Avele athi, 
“Kulungile Mhlonishwa, umthetho yiwona oyohlukanisa inhloko 
nesixhanti. Mina nawe asazi lutho. Ungakhohlwa ukuthi izingane 
ziyaphoxana. Angeke ukuqinisekise ukuthi uyazazi.” 

Aluvale ucingo uMabanga engasavalelisanga. 

“Mhn! Kulukhuni kuyitshe. Phela uyinyongo nangu ummeli. 
Sekuyangikhanyela manje ukuthi lo mfana udelela kangaka nje 
yingoba igunya elithole kuyise. Yena uMabanga unesiqiniseko 
esingakanani ukuthi indodana yakhe ayinacala? Kanti ingane 
ingamtshela yini umzali wayo ukuthi iyisigebengu? Konje vele 
kungumsebenzi wabo abameli ukumela izelelesi bazikhiphe 
emajele ngoba bethi zinamalungelo okumelwa. Ziyasuka lapho 
zihlukumeza umphakathi ongenacala ngoba zazi kahle ukuthi 
bakhona abameli bazozikhulumela.” 

Lumshukashuke uMnguni udaba lukaMabanga aze agcine 
esefikelwe ngumbono othi akabize uZuma azomxoxela 
ngezinsongo zikaMabanga. Uyazi ukuthi ukhona umqondo 
azowuthola kuye. Athathe umshini wokuxhumana abize ngawo 
uZuma, amcele ukuba aphuthume ehhovisi lakhe. Nebala angene 
uZuma ahlale phansi. Avele azibonele uZuma ukuthi kuyabheda. 
Babuphaphathekile ubuso bukaMnguni ngenxa yovalo. 

“Zimbi izinto Nxamalala,” kusho uMnguni ehlalisisa 
esihlalweni. 

“Wo, singathini mfowethu, yizinkinga zomhlaba 
lezo. Okubuhlungu nje ngukuthi zidalwa yizimfamona, 
azizenzakaleli.” 

“Lisho uliphinde lelo Nxamalala. Ngihlupheka nje kungenxa 
yabantu bakithi abamnyama. Usemkhulu umsebenzi okusafanele 
wenziwe ukuguqula izingqondo zabo zisebenzele intuthuko. 

110 



Ubandlululo lwazilimaza kakhulu izingqondo zabantu bakithi. 
Nanxa sesingenile embusweni wentando yeningi kodwa uyabona 
nje ukuthi ubuthi obadalwa wubandlululo busekhona kubantu. 
Uma umuntu omnyama ekhushulelwa esikhundleni esiphakeme, 
kusuka omunye umuntu omnyama amdonsele phansi ukuze 
ahluleke ukusebenza ngempumelelo.” 

“Yiqiniso lelo Qwabe. Kusekude phambili kumuntu 
omnyama. Kunensila embi emnamathele okuthiwa wumona 
nokungelula ukuba ikhuhleke. Bheka ngoba kumanje nje 
awukhululekile kodwa usemsebenzini. Nawa amaphoyisa 
akugadile. Kuseyiwona njalo umsebenzi womuntu omnyama.” 

“Kusinda kwehlela Nxamalala. Ngikubiza nje ngifuna 
ukukutshela ukuthi ngiqeda kuthola ucingo oluvela kuMabanga 
ummeli.” 

“Musa ukusho njalo Qwabe!” kusho uZuma ngokwethuka. 

“Kunjengoba ngisho Nxamalala.” 

“Uthini uMabanga?” 

“Ungitshele ukuthi uma inkantolo ike yamkhipha phambili 
umfana wakhe, uyosibopha izandla nezinyawo nala maphoyisa 
ami.” 

“Uyahlanya uMabanga. Ududwa ngukuthi ungummeli 
owaziwayo. Okokuqala nje lo mfana wakhe uyedelela akamazi 
umuntu omdala. UMabanga ufuna ukuthi sibuswe yilo mfana 
wakhe, agcagcaze phezu kwamakhanda ethu sithule? Usangene. 
Asizukuvuma thina ukudansela isigingci sendodana yakhe.” 

“Uqhubeke wathi kufanele sikhumbule njalo ukuthi njengoba 
eboshiwe lo mfana ziyamshiya izifundo. Uma eseyosimangalela, 
uzofuna zonke izinxephezelo zalokho kimi. Manje mfowethu 
ngifuna sibonisane ukuthi ngingasivika kanjani lesi simo.” Asho 
uMnguni echofochofoza iphepha ngepeni phezu kwetafula. 

“Yima isibindi Qwabe. Ngiyawathemba amaphoyisa. 

111 



Azomphenya umfana kaMabanga aze amehlule. Uzogcina 
eliphalaze lonke iqiniso.” 

“Wo, mina angisethembi lutho Nxamalala. Sesiside lesi 
sikhathi ephenywa lo mfana. Kufanele ukuthi ngabe aselitholile 
iqiniso kuye. Manje kubukeka sengathi asehlulekile.” 

“Akulula ukuphenya Qwabe. Nakhu phela kuwathathe 
isikhathi eside la maphoyisa ukuthola imoto yakho, yize eyithole 
isiyigobongo nje. Bekezela mfowethu, kuzolunga.” 

“Ukube awatholile amasela emoto yami, ngabe ngithi 
kuzolunga. Manje agcine ngalo igobongo lelo. Lutho ukuthola 
amasela.” 

“Yithemba kuphela eliyokusiza Qwabe. Uma umethemba 
uNkulunkulu ukuthi ungumenzi wezinto zonke, uyobe uqedile. 
Uzokulwela. Mina ngimsola kakhulu lo mfana wakwaMabanga. 
Unolwazi ngakho konke okwenzekayo lapha esikoleni. Nakuba 
ngingaqondile ukuthi nguyena yedwa owenza wonke lo 
monakalo, kodwa unesandla kuwo.” 

Engakaphenduli uMnguni, kukhale ucingo. Aluphakamise. 

“NguKaputeni uMchunu oshayayo.” 

“Wenzile washaya Macingwane. Zimbi izinto ngapha.” 

“Sengathi zimbi nhlangothi zonke Qwabe. Njengoba 
ngikuthinta nje ngifuna ukukwazisa ukuthi bengihlaselwe 
ngummeli uMabanga khona manje ezongitshela ukuthi 
uma inkantolo ike yayithola ingenecala indodana yakhe, 
siyowukhomba onotshwala.” 

“Kahleni bo! Yimihlola phela lena. Kanti weyisa ngempela 
uMabanga?” 

“Ukweyisa yinto yakhe. Akazikhohliwe engummeli womhlaba. 
Thina maphoyisa akasazi ukuthi siyini. Maningi kabi amaphoyisa 
asebhincele nxanye ngenxa yakhe. Manje usehlala ecabanga 

112 



ukuhlukumeza onke amaphoyisa.” 

“Uyazi Macingwane, ushaya ucingo nje nginothisha 
uZuma lapha ehhovisi. Sidingida udaba lwakhe uMabanga. 
Ubengishayele ucingo engitshela yona le nto akutshele yona. 

Ungisongele kanzima impela.”

ukuthi sisagoyele ukwenzani laphaya ehhovisi laso ngoba 
sesaphela kudala isikhathi saso. Ontanga baso badla endala, sona 
sisaxoshana nezigebengu.”

Angaphendulwa muntu uSayitsheni.

Kwaba lukhuni kuZondo ukunika isigebengu inombolo

133 



ISAHLUKO SESHUMI 

Wangena esangweni lesikole umfo kaZuma ubuso bujajile. 
Kwakusobala ngisho enyathela ukuthi unokuzethemba. 
Nabalingani bakhe ayefundisa nabo bakuqaphela ukwenza 
kwakhe. Baze bamhleba bathi mhlawumbe usethenjiswe ukuba 
yiphini likaMnguni ngokugcwele. Ziyenzeka izinto lapha 
ngaphandle. Ngeke ufunge ugomele uthi uyazazi ukuthi zihamba 
kanjani. Ziguquguquka mizuzu yonke yokuphila okwesondo 
lenqola. 

Ngesikhathi evula ihhovisi lakhe uZuma, umlomo 
wawumungunya ingoma eyayingezwakali ukuthi ithini. Yena 
wayengakunakile ukuthi kwakukhona okwakuwushintsho 
ekwenzeni kwakhe izinto nokwakubonwa ngabalingani bakhe. 
Eqinisweni uZuma wayethokoziswe wukubona uMnguni egadwe 
ngamaphoyisa. Indlela ayenza ngayo la maphoyisa yayimnika 
ithemba lokuthi uThish’omkhulu wakhe wayesezandleni 
eziphephile. Wangena ehhovisi uZuma wahlela umsebenzi 
wosuku. 

Ngokuqhubeka kosuku uZuma wakuqaphela ukuthi 
uThish’omkhulu wayengekho esikoleni. Kubona bonke othisha, 
akekho owabe azi ukuthi uMnguni wayesesibhedlela. Ngisho 
noSokhela uqobo wayengazi ukuthi uNguzunga wayesimise 
ngamanzonzo isimo. Kwase kuphele izinsuku impela engalwazi 
ucingo olwaluvela kuyena uNguzunga. Okwakumkhathaza 
kakhulu ngukuthi wayehlulekile ngosuku olwedlule 
ukuyombona ngenxa yekhehla lejazi. Kwakuphinde kumkhathaze 
nokubona amaphoyisa eqaphe uMnguni ngale ndlela ngoba 
kwakungezukuba lula kuNguzunga ukwenza umsebenzi 
wakhe. Wayewabone kahle la maphoyisa ukuthi ayengagayelwe 
mphako. Ayexosha ngisho nempukane eyayindizela ngasehhovisi 
likaMnguni. 

134 



Kwathi lapho engazelele uZuma, wezwa kukhala ucingo. 
Waluphakamisa ngomdlandla ecabanga ukuthi lwaluvela 
kuMnguni. Kwakungumkhuba wakhe uMnguni ukuthi uma 
ezophuza ukufika esikoleni, ashaye ucingo azise uZuma. 

“NguKaputeni uMchunu esiteshini samaphoyisa lona 
okhulumayo Nxamalala,” kuzethula uKaputeni ngomoya ophansi 
ogcwele umunyu nosizi. 

“Pho singakwenzelani wena wasemthethweni?” kubuza 
uZuma eshaywa wuvadlwana. Kucishe kumkhanyele ukuthi 
kukhona okungekuhle okwenzekile. Yena ubelindele ucingo 
oluvela kuMnguni. Lumphinde futhi uvalo. Nokho aziqinise 
angawuvumeli lo mcabango othi kungenzeka ukuthi uMnguni 
usesocongiwe. 

“Wo! MntakaZuma, ithi ingaba nkulu ivele igcwale umlomo 
nje ingabe isazekeka.” 

Lumphinde uvalo uZuma. Kumkhanyele ukuthi selidume 
ledlula naye uMnguni ebelihlome ngezikhukhula. Akusekho 
ukubuza ibhasi libe libhaliwe ukuthi liya eMtshezi. 

“Ingabe uqonde ukungitshela ukuthi sezize zamgojela 
izigebengu uThish’omkhulu Macingwane?” Ubuza lo mbuzo 
nje uZuma, isandla esibambe ucingo siqhoqhobelwe yidumbe. 
Kanjalo nezwi liyaqhaqhazela. 

“Cha, akunjalo Nxamalala. Yehlisa umoya mfowethu. Usaphila 
uMnguni.” 

Awudedele kakhulu umoya abesewubambile uZuma. Lwehle 
uvalo. “Usaphila uThish’omkhulu Macingwane?” 

“Usaphila Nxamalala nakuba kubonwa ngokusa kuyena 
esibhedlela saseMawozi lapho belaliswe khona nephoyisa 
uZondo,” kuchaza uKaputeni engazi ukuthi uzoyibeka kanjani le 
ndaba kuZuma ukuze ingamphithisi ikhanda. 

“Macingwane, kwenzekani ngoThish’omkhulu? Chaza 

135 



kahle phela ukuze ngicacelwe.” Abuze umfo kaZuma esethanda 
ukuphelelwa nayisineke. Wayezibuza ukuthi uqondeni uKaputeni 
uma ethi akehlise umoya kodwa abe ebika ukuthi kubonwa 
ngokusa kuMnguni esibhedlela. 

“UQwabe kanye namaphoyisa bahlaselwe yindoda engaziwa 
izolo ebusuku bengazelele. Kuthiwa le ndoda ibigqoke izingubo

ngendlov’iyangena yabampintshela ekhoneni kwancane indawo. 
Ngaleso sikhathi uMnguni ubezicambalalele ekamelweni engazi 
ukuthi kwenzekani endlini yokuphumula. Uze wavuswa yisona 
isigebengu sansondo sesiwabophe ngentambo amaphoyisa. Naye 
ube eseboshwa khona lapho. Sibe sesibagandaya, sabadovadova 
ngesibhakela isigebengu saze sadela. Sabephuca izibhamu nokhiye 
wemoto kahulumeni sabaleka ngayo. 

“Macingwane, usho ukuthi amaphoyisa amabili ahlomile, 
ahlulwe yisigebengu kalula kanjalo nje saze sawephuca imoto

nguKaputeni. 

“Impela Nxamalala,” kusho uKaputeni edliwa ngunembeza. 
Phela wayengeke ayilokothe indaba kaSayitsheni kuZuma. “Imoto 
itholakele. Yizibhamu kuphela ezingatholakalanga.” 

“Itholakale kanjani imoto?” 

“Singishayele sona ucingo isigebengu sangibikela yonke 
into nokuthi ngizoyithola kuphi inqola kahulumeni. Ngibe 
sengisuka ekhaya ngiphuthuma lo monakalo. Ngifike kwaMnguni 
ngathola ukuthi balimele kabi ababekade beshaywa yisigebengu. 
Ngenhlanhla uSayitsheni uNgubane ubengalimele. UZondo 
ubelimele impela. UMnguni-ke ubemubi ngendlela ethusayo. 
Ngibe sengibaphuthumisa esibhedlela. Ngemuva kwalokho 
ngathatha uSayitsheni sayolanda inqola kahulumeni kuleyo 
ndawo esingiyalele kuyo isigebengu.” 

136

bahlome baphelele uma bezimisele ukumbopha lo Nguzunga. 

“Akukho ukuxhumana okwaziyo phakathi kukaNguzunga 
nephini likaThish’omkhulu wasesikoleni senu?” 

“Cha, akukho engikwaziyo ngalokho.” 

“Akakaze asho lutho kuwena uNguzunga ngoSokhela?’ 

“Lutho Kaputeni.” 

Kuhlwe manje kuKaputeni, kodwa angalilahli ithemba. 
Acabange ukuthi uzosebenzisa liphi isu ukuthola umkhondo 
kaSokhela kulo mfana. Khona indlela ayephendula ngayo uBen 
yayikucacisa ukuthi wayengazi lutho ngoSokhela. 

Eseqedile ukubhala isitatimende uKaputeni, wacisha 
isiqophamazwi wase ebiza uSayitsheni ukuba azophindisela 
uBen esitokisini. Wazimisela ukuba athathe uSayitsheni banikele 
eBonokuhle, bayobopha uNguzunga baphenye noSokhela. 

USokhela akazihluphanga ngokuyobona uMnguni esibhedlela. 

147 



Wavele waqonda ekhaya kwakhe ngethemba lokuthi uzothola 
ucingo oluvela kuNguzunga. Wayekhululekile emoyeni ngoba 
uMaMhlongo wayesathe shelele ngakubo eMnambithi eyobona 
unina owayebangwa nezibi. 

Ukulimala kukaMnguni kwakumbikela uSokhela ukuthi 
lwalungaselude ukhalo afike emadlelweni aluhlaza. Nokho 
kwakuyobe kwenzeke into ayeyifisa ukuba angafi uMnguni kodwa 
azihambele. UMlangeni wadoda ngendlela emangalisayo ngoba 
akazange adaze inkani. Wazibonela nje ukuthi libukeka lizoduma 
kusiphuke izikhonkwane. Wanyakaza kusakhanya. 

“Uyobe wakhula elusa amabhubesi ngesiswebhu uMnguni 
uma engaqhubeka nokuqinisa ikhanda yize sezimnethe kangaka! 
Sengathi abakithi banami kule mpi. Indlela ezenzeka ngayo 
izinto manje, kukhomba ngokusobala ukuthi sekukhona 
nesandla sabaphansi. Angingabazi ukuthi umkhulu lapho ekhona 
ungibhekile. Ngifuna kucacele ngisho nezincelebane zakhe 
uMnguni ukuthi yimina kuphela inkunzi ekhonyayo.” 

Nangempela lwangena ucingo ayelulindele uSokhela. 
Wamkhinikela sonke isimo uNguzunga. Washo nokuthi yena 
usezibona esewuqedile owakhe umsebenzi. 

“Usho ukuthi sekufanele ngikukhokhele ndodana?” 

“Akujiki lokho Sikhulu.” 

Athule isikhashana uSokhela ecabanga. Uthe esuka wabe ethi, 

“Kodwa mina angikagculiseki ndodana ngoba akukangikhanyeli 
ukuthi uzohamba lo muntu noma cha. Angithi usesesibhedlela?” 

“Yebo.” 

“Mina ngibona ukuthi sike sithi ukulinda kancane sibone 
ukuthi uhamba ngempela yini lo muntu.” 

“We ndoda, usho ukuthi awukwethembi konke lokhu 
engikushoyo?” 

148 



“Cha, angisho ukuthi angikwethembi ndodana, kodwa…” 

“Yeyi wena! Kusasa lokhu okusayo ngifuna ukubona inkokhelo 
yami ihlezi ezandleni zami, ungizwa kahle?” 

“Ngiyakuzwa ndodana, kodwa usuyangixaka ngokuvukwa 
wulaka esikhaleni kungenzeke lutho.” 

“Ngicikwa nguwena ngokungangethembi. Angisafuni 
ukulokhu ngiqophisana nawe manje. Obekusihlanganisile 
kuphelile manje. Ngithi ngiyifuna yonke imali yami kusasa!” 
Washo eligcizelela elemali ephelele uNguzunga. 

“Kahle ndodana. Usuthini futhi manje? Usuyifuna yonke 
imali yakho? Angithi savumelana ngokuthi ngizokukhokhela 
ngamanconzunconzu ize iphelele?” 

“Ukhumbule ukuthi ngangingakawuqali lo msebenzi 
ngesikhathi sivumelana ngenkokhelo enjalo futhi ngangihlele 
ukuthi ngiyowenza nabafundi lo msebenzi. Ngeshwa-ke 
bangihlamuka. Angithi ngakushayela ucingo ngakwazisa ukuthi 

sengizowenza ngedwa?” 

“Yiqiniso lelo ndodana.” 

“Manje ubona ukuthi ngiyakuqola yini Sikhulu?” 

“Cha ndodana.” 

“Ikuphi-ke inkinga yakho?” 

“Inkinga yami isekutheni awungichazelanga ukuthi inkokhelo 
yakho izodingeka yonke ngesikhathi esisodwa uma kwenzeka 
usushintsha amasu okwenza lo msebenzi.” 

“Ayikho-ke le nto oyishoyo Sikhulu. Mina ngiwenzile 
umsebenzi. Angizimisele ukuqolwa nguwena. Ngifuna imali yami 
kwaphela nje.” Washo uNguzunga sekuzwakala ukuthi usedinwe 
kakhulu manje. 

“Cha, sengathi ngizokwehluleka.” 

“Ake ulokothe phela, uzongifunda ungiqonde. Angibhenywa 

149 



ngegudu ngingensangu. Awungitshelanga ngani kwasekuqaleni 
ukuthi uzokwehluleka ukungikhokhela? Ngangizoyeka konke 
phansi uzibonele ukuthi wenzenjani. Ubukade umkhulu lo 
msebenzi futhi unzima.” 

“Ngiyakwazi lokho ndodana, kodwa iqiniso lithi awukapheli.” 

“Lalela lapha-ke Sikhulu. Uma ungafuni ukungikhokhela 
lonke iholo lami kusasa, ngiyokungqokloza ngensimbi yomlungu 
khona esikoleni uyokwelusa amadada. Angibhedelwa mina. Kanti 
ungiphuza inyongo?” 

Ethuke uSokhela. “Kahle ngolaka ndodana. Usungaze 
ungibulale impela nje ungibulalele into engekho? Ubunswelaboya 
phela lobu obenzayo. Asivumelananga ngokuthi ngizokukhokhela 
yonke imali yakho ngoba uzobe usuwusebenza wedwa lo 
msebenzi. Ake ungitshele nje ukuthi ngizoyithathaphi le mali 
engaka njengoba ngingenalutho esandleni?” 

Athule uNguzunga aququde amathambo engqondo. 
Kumkhanyele ukuthi uma ezithambisa, uzogcina engasayitholanga 
yonke le mali. Indaba yamanconzunconzu ingumbhedo uma 
izinto sezimi ngalolu hlobo. Izolokhu imbambezela aze aficwe 
ngamathonsi abanzi. Uzimisele ukuyithola yonke le mali ukuze 
abone kusakhanya nje ukuthi wenzenjani. Uwenzile umsebenzi 
wakhe kodwa akanalo iqiniso lokuthi amaphoyisa awazukwazi 
ukuwuthola umkhondo womhlaseli. Uzoke athi ukushaya utshani 
kancane size sidambe isimo bese ebuya-ke ezokwenza lokhu afuna 
ukukwenza ngale mali. UBen uzozibona ukuqeda esitokisini. 
Uyothi eqambe emchaya emaphoyiseni, abe engasabonwa yena kule 
ndawo. Yena Nguzunga omnyama, akanaso isikhathi sezimpatha 
ezifana noBen ezingena kalula enethini njengezinhlanzi. Kuhle 
nje ngoba uzolokhu eqhethile esitokisini ecabanga ukuthi wenza 
umzamo wokumkhulula kantu useshaye phansi. Uyothi lapho ethi 
uvula amehlo uBen, libe selishonile ilanga. Cha, uyobe wephuzile 
uma engamcindezeli uSokhela ukuba amkhokhele ngokushesha. 

150 



“Sengiqedile ukukhuluma nawe Sikhulu. Siza-ke ungiphathele 
zonke izimfanelo zami kusasa. Ulimele kabi lo muntu. Ngeke 
akucabange ukubuyela eBonokuhle.” 

“Usho njalo ndodana?” 

“Yizwa mina wena. Uma ungezukuba nayo inkokhelo yami 
kusasa, kungakuhle ukuba uye koyeboleka ngoba kusasa ngizobe 
ngidinwe kakhulu ngingenanhliziyo nginjalo nje.” Aluvale ucingo 
uNguzunga. NoSokhela aluvale olwakhe. Athule isikhathi eside 
egqolozele ucingo. “Wo, sengathi zithanda ukungijikela izinto 
manje. Ngizoyithini indaba yalo mfana? Ngangimethemba 
ngithi ulungile kanti uzongijikela. Awu, ngaze ngazijuqa ngeklwa 
ngibhekile bakithi! Phela uzongibulala ngempela lo sathane!” 

Wabalisa njalo uSokhela. Pho-ke kwakusayomsiza ngani 
lokho ngoba wawusukhulumile umlomo ongathethi manga. 
Kwakumcacele ukuthi izwi likaNguzunga lingumnqamlajuqu. 
Ukuba wayesheshe waluthola ucingo kungakavalwa ebhange, 
wayezophuthuma khona ngokushesha ayokweboleka imali. Wo, 
wayesefe olwembiza umfo kaSokhela. Kwakungasekho ukuhlehla. 
Kwase kufanele ukuba asale eselidedela leli kloba lomlilo ayethi 
ulibasela uMnguni, limhashule izandla nezinyawo. Waqala manje 
ukuwakhumbula amazwi kaMaMhlongo. Wazibona nezinyembezi 
zidedelana ezihlathini zakhe. Impela wayeqinisile uMaMhlongo 
uma ethi uzomkhumbula ngolunye usuku. 

Khona manjalo uSokhela wafikelwa ngumqondo wokuba 
asheshe avuke ngakusasa ekuseni, aphuthume esikoleni 
bengakafiki abanye othisha. Wayehlose ukuthola ithuba lokuxoxa 
noNguzunga, amcele ukuba amlinde amahora ambalwa 
esayokweboleka le mali ebhange. Nakanjani wayezobuya 
ngokushesha amkhokhele yonke imali yakhe. Uma enze njalo, 
wayezobe ukwazile ukuwubhula lo mlilo owawusumhashula 
izandla nezinyawo. Walala enethemba lokuthi, wayesemnqobile lo 
sathane owayefisa impilo yakhe. 

151 



ISAHLUKO SESHUMI NANYE 

Esebuyile uSayitsheni ukuyohambisa uBen esitokisini, 
uKaputeni wahlala naye phansi wamdlalela isiqophamazwi. 
Ladlala ibhande laze lafika ekugcineni. Wabamba ongezansi umfo 
kaNgubane. 

“Usuyabona-ke manje Ngubane ukuthi ngisuke nginganethuki 
uma ngithi niyehluleka ukwenza umsebenzi wenu?” 

“Ewu, kulukhuni Kaputeni.” 

“Angithi yimina lo owenqaba usumdedela lo mfana 
kaMabanga ngoba uthi akalivumi icala?” 

“Kunjalo Kaputeni.” 

“Angishongo ukuthi akayedwa lo mfana kule nxushunxushu?” 

“Eyi, washo Macingwane.” 

“Nakho-ke. Ukuba nisebenza ngokuzimisela Ngubane, 
ngabe kudala zaboshwa lezi zigebengu. Ake ubheke nje ukuthi 
oZondo noMnguni bacishe bafa kabuhlungu kanjani, ngakho 
belu ukungasebenzi kwenu. Osekusele manje wukuba abanjwe lo 
mfana kuphenywe noSokhela. Uma isimo sivuma, kwaSokhela 
lowo siyobuya naye, ngimfunge uPhoshozwayo. Ushilo-ke umfana 
kaMabanga ukuthi lo Nguzunga ndini uyisigelekeqe esehlula 
ukwenza. Uma siphundulekile, siyosala enkundleni. Mina ngithi 
yize kunjalo, ngimdinga esitokisini.” 

Ajuluke ubala uSayitsheni. “Sizosibamba kanjani lesi sigelekeqe 
esichazwa ngalolu hlobo Kaputeni?” 

“Kulula lokho Ngubane. Siqeqeshiwe thina ukuze sikwazi 
ukubamba izigebengu ezanoma yiluphi uhlobo. Asiyi kosinisa 
amahleza laphaya esikoleni. Siyosebenza.” 

“Eyi kodwa Kaputeni, kulukhuni.” 

“Akusekho ukuhlehla Ngubane uma sekunjena. Yikhohlwe 

152 



nya le ndaba yakho yokucasha ngesidindi umzimba wonke uhleli 
obala. Kusasa lokhu okusayo, ngimfuna endlini emnyama lo 
Nguzunga ndini. Ngifuna ukuthi sibuye isithunzi salesi siteshi 
esaqedwa yinina. Okwamanje ngifuna ukuthi uhambe uyohlola 
izibhamu ukuthi zisakulungele yini ukuhlasela. Uma kungukuthi 
uyalwa lo mfokazi, kuyosala osalayo othulini, ngimfunge 
uPhoshozwayo. Hamba-ke Ngubane.” 

Ahambe uSayitsheni enokukhononda okukhulu enhliziyweni. 
Ubengubani yena ukuba angabhekana nomuntu ochazwa 
njengemamba ehlula izibiba? 

Ngakusasa ekuseni washeshe wafika uSokhela esikoleni. 
Wayecuthele uNguzunga ukuze amchazele kahle ngesu 
ayeselicabangile. Ngenhlanhla naye uNguzunga washeshe wafika. 
Wathi engena nje esangweni, wayembona uSokhela, wambizela 
ehhovisi lakhe. Wayengakachazi nakuchaza uSokhela ngalokhu 
ayesezimisele ukukwenza ngesikhathi uNguzunga elula isandla 
efuna inkokhelo yakhe. Kwaba wukulandula kuSokhela, sahlala 
sagcwala ubuso isibhakela. Akabange esakwazi ukuchaza kahle 
ngoba yonke into yayenzeka ngokushesha. 

“Kahle ndodana! Mana ngikuchazele!” 

“Ungichazeleni? Angithi ngikutshele kahle ukuthi ngizoyifuna 
yonke imali yami?” 

“Noma ngabe ngikone kangakanani mfana wami, kodwa 
usungaze ungibeke isandla pho, nginguthisha wakho?” 

“Usuyakwazi ukubona manje ukuthi ingane akufanele 
ishaye uthisha wayo ngoba sekushaywa wena? Uma kushaywa 
uThish’omkhulu akubi ndaba zalutho?” 

“Nginike ithuba phela ndodana ngichaze. Uzoyithola imali 
yakho, kodwa…” 

“Yeyi wena, guqa phansi uthandaze! Ulibuka uyaligcina 

153 



namuhla. Uhlala umbela abanye igodi nje, uzimbele wena 
namuhla,” kusho uNguzunga ekhipha u-machine-gun wakhe 
esikhwameni esikhulukazi ayesigaxile. 

Ngesikhathi ethi uhlohla u-machine-gun wakhe uNguzunga, 
abone sekutheleka amaphoyisa ehhovisi likaSokhela. Ayehehwe 
wumsindo owase uthe mukuthu ehhovisi likaSokhela, 
kubatshazwa, kukhuzwa umhlola. 

Kwathi lapho ethi nhla emnyango amaphoyisa, azithela 
kuNguzunga owaseyibhubesi elifuna ukuchobozela kwasani 
eyayiphambi kwalo. Wayesemnyama ngenkani umfo 
kaNyakanyaka. Agxuma amaphoyisa ahlehlela kude le emuva. 

“Yeyi wena mfana, lahla phansi leso sibhamu! Uma ungasilahli, 
ngizokuchitha ubuchopho!” kusho uKaputeni ekhombe 
uNguzunga ngesibhamu. 

“Ngeke ngikwenze lokho!” kuphendula uNguzunga ngolaka. 

Abafundi kanye nothisha abase belapho, babaleka bayomela 
kude. Babesadidekile bengaqondi ukuthi kwenzekani futhi 
kubangwani. Kwakungokokuqala ngqa emlandweni wakulesi 
sikole ukuthi umfundi ahlasele uthisha. 

“Ngithe lahla phansi leso sibhamu wena! Ngiyadubula-ke 
manje!” 

Njengemamba ithukutheliswe amanxeba, wagadla 
umfo kaNyakanyaka emaphoyiseni. Laduma izulu lezandla 
kwazamazama umhlaba. Kwasiza khona ukuthi amaphoyisa 
ayegqoke izingubo ezivikela izinhlamvu. Wagadla udede 
uNguzunga ahlukana phakathi amaphoyisa. Lokho kwamnika 
ithuba lokuphuma agelekeqeke ehhovisi likaSokhela. Athathana 
naye amaphoyisa ngezibhamu egcekeni lesikole kwabaleka bonke 
abantu. Zabubula izibhamu kwanuka isisi. 

Nakuba amaphoyisa ayemabili futhi eqeqeshwe ngokwenele 
ukubopha izigebengu, kodwa kulokhu azithola ebhekene 

154 



nomqansa. Yayisinda ngempela impi ayeyibambile. UNguzunga 
wayelwela ukufa nokuphila. Wayengaxhamazeli. Wayededela 
imbumbulu yezinhlamvu ebhekise emaphoyiseni avike ubala. 
Kwasiza imoto kahulumeni ayede evika ngayo. Lokho kwamnika 
ithuba lokucela empunzini uNguzunga. Isibhamu sakhe sase 
siphelelwe yizinhlamvu. 

“Yelekelelani! Nasi isigebengu sibaleka! Vimbani ngaphambili 
bo!” kumemeza uKaputeni. Wayememeza nje engazibekile 
phansi ngejubane ethe mbe ngemuva kukaNguzunga. 
Kwakungelula ukuba amxine eduze ngejubane ngoba nomkhaba 
wawumphazamisa. Amalungu omphakathi ayemi ngaphandle 
kwesango, awamsizanga ngalutho uKaputeni. Avele athi nhla 
abona insizwa igelekeqeka nesibhamu esandleni, abeletha 
izithende. Abaleka agcwala umgwaqo nokwadala ukuthi 
uKaputeni athi uyadubula, kunembeke elinye lawo engalweni. 

Lokhu kudubuleka kwelungu lomphakathi kwamthena 
amandla uKaputeni. Wavele wakhohlwa nguNguzunga, wanikela 
kulowo owayelimele. Ngaleso sikhathi uNguzunga wathola 
ukuphefumula. Kodwa akazithambisanga ngejubane nakuba 
wayesebonile ukuthi wayengasaxoshwa muntu. Waqinisa njalo 
ngejubane waze wayofika ngasesitolo sakwaBhengu. Khona 
manjalo weqa ucingo weqela kodukathole bamasimu ayeqala 
ngemuva kwesitolo ehle njalo aze ayoshona ezansi emfuleni. 
Wanyamalala emakhabeni. 

Nabanye othisha basondela kulo muntu owayelimele ukuze 
bamhlenge ngosizo lokuqala. Kwathi lapho othisha bethola 
ukuthi kwakuyikhehla lejazi leli elalidubulekile, bethuka kakhulu. 

“Hawu madoda! Kanti nguwena mkhulu odubulekile? Kodwa 
awulimalanga kakhulu?” kubuza uthisha uMazibuko ebhekisisa 
ingalo yekhehla lejazi eyase ibomvu tebhu yigazi. 

“Yimina thisha, bengithi ngizohlola uSokhela. Nakho-ke 

155 



sengithi ngiyamemfuka ensimini ngazithela phezu kwequlu 
labantu libaleka. Kuthe lapho ngisadidekile ngingazi ukuthi 
kwenzekani, ngezwa ngenhlamvu ihlala engalweni. Namanje 
angazi ukuthi iceze kanjani yangayinemba inhliziyo. Hhawu, 
beniyongithola sengibanda. Bheka-ke ngoba noSokhela 
ubezokhala azithulise ngoba bengizobe ngife singasaxoxanga.” 
Lisho ikhehla lejazi liziqinisa ezinhlungwini ezazilidla. 
Ngesikhathi lilandisa, abanye othisha babelihlenga ngosizo 
lokuqala. 

“Kodwa ube neshwa mkhulu kwavele kwanembeka wena 
kubona bonke laba bantu ebebekade bebaleka. Ngakolunye 
uhlangothi ukuqhamuka kwakho kusindise isigebengu esicishe 
sadubula yena lo Sokhela oze kuyena. Ukuba awumemfukanga 
ensimini, ngabe sishayekile ngoba besekuqala ukuvuleka 
isikhala ukuze uKaputeni akwazi ukudubula,” kuchaza uthisha 
uMazibuko. 

“Kahle thisha, uSokhela ucishe wabulawa yisigebengu?” 
kubuza ikhehla lejazi lithukile. 

“Ucishe wafa uSokhela mkhulu. Maphoyisa lawo amsizile. 
Wena uqhamuka nje kuxoshwa sona leso sigebengu.” 

“Simbangisani kodwa umzukulu kaSikhumbasebhubesi 
ezilungele kangaka bakithi?” 

“Asazi-ke lapho mkhulu. Nguyena lowo mzukulu 
kaSikhumbasebhubesi ongachaza kulokho.” 

“Mmm! Kusobala ukuthi usethengelwe izigebengu uSokhela 
ukuba abulawe ukuze angasitholi isikhundla sakhe.” Lisho 
ngokukhathazeka ikhehla lejazi. 

Akabange esaqhubeka nengxoxo uMazibuko. Amazwi ekhehla 
lejazi ayesethanda ukumbinda kanti wabe azi ukuthi lalincenga 
abanumzane bendawo ukuba bahambe bayobonga uMnguni 
eMnyangweni wezeMfundo. 

156 



UKaputeni wayesadidekile ngokudubuleka komuntu 
ongenacala ngesikhathi kufika omunye uthisha kuye ezombikela 
ukuthi uSayitsheni wayedubuleke ethangeni. UZuma kanye 
nabanye othisha besifazane ababili, babemhlenga bembopha 
inxeba. UKaputeni wamane wajiyelwa nje wangabe esazi ukuthi 
kufanele enzeni. Wasuka lapho waqonda kuSayitsheni. Lwehla 
uvalo uma esebona ukuthi akalimele ngendlela enyantisa igazi. 

Abafundi kanye nothisha ababebalekile ngesikhathi 
kudutshulwana, base bebuyile enkundleni. NoSokhela 
wabonakala esondela kancane esixukwini. Wayeqhaqhazela 
umzimba wonke. Izithukuthuku zaziqathaka ebusweni ezesula 
ngesandla. Wayede ephonsa amehlo ngakodukathole bamasimu 
lapho uNguzunga wayebalekele khona. Ngesikhathi eqa ucingo 
ngemuva kwesitolo sakwaBhengu eyongena emakhabeni, 
wayembuka uSokhela. 

Ngesikhathi ikhehla lejazi noSayitsheni benikwa usizo 
lokuqala, uKaputeni wathola ithuba lokusondela kuSokhela 
ambuze ngalesi sigebengu esasimvimbezele ngesibhamu. 

“Lo mfana ufunda khona lapha esikoleni Kaputeni,” 
kuphendula uSokhela ngezwi eliqhaqhazelayo. 

“Nibangani naye?” 

“Uma ngingathi ngiyazi mntakaMchunu, ngabe ngisenga 
ezingasengwa. Mina ngibone ngomfana esengena egulukudela 
ehhovisi lami, wangikhomba ngesibhamu wathi angithandaze 
ngoba ngilibuka ngiyaligcina namuhla.” 

“Kanjalo nje Sokhela?” kubuza uKaputeni ngelokusola 
sengathi kukhona amfihlela khona uSokhela. 

“Kanjalo Kaputeni. Namanje ngizibuza ngiyaziphendula 
ukuthi ungizweni lo mfana njengoba esecishe wangibulala nje. 
Ngisindele nina. Besengifile.” 

“Owaphi yena lo mfana?” 

157 



“Angimazi ukuthi ungowaphi. Isibongo sakhe 
ungowakwaNyakanyaka.” 

“Hhayo bo! Akuyena nje lo Nguzunga esimfunayo?” kubuza 
uKaputeni esewakhiphele ngaphandle onke amehlo. 

“Ngu…nguyena Kaputeni,” kuvuma uSokhela amehlo akhe 
ebalekelana nakaKaputeni. Wakuphawula lokho uKaputeni 
kodwa wangasho lutho. Ingqondo yakhe yayinamathele odabeni 
lukaNguzunga futhi ejahe ukuhambisa abalimele esibhedlela. 

“Kanti lo mfana uyingozi kangaka madoda! Awu, saze 
saphunyuka isigelekeqe sisifuna kangaka!” 

Asuke uKaputeni kuSokhela athi ukuzulazula egcekeni aqoqe 
amabhosho. Khona manjalo ezwakale ekhuza umhlola. “Habe! 
La mabhosho afana ncamashi nalawa atholakala mhla kubulewe 
unogada lapha esikoleni!” Asho uKaputeni ewabukisisa. Ahambe 
nawo aye kuSayitsheni nekhehla lejazi, abanxuse ukuba bangene 
emotweni. 

Yasuka ngelikhulu ijubane imoto yamaphoyisa yaqonda 
esibhedlela saseMawozi. Kwaba wukufika esibhedlela, bangeniswa 
egumbini labalimele oSayitsheni nekhehla lejazi. Ngemuva 
kokubhalisa imininingwane yabo, uKaputeni waqonda 
embhedeni okwakulele kuwo uZondo. Nokho wayesengcono 
kakhulu. Wafike wamlandisa ngakho konke okwakwenzekile, 
nangolwazi ayeluthole kuZuma noBen. Wamane wakhexa 
umlomo uZondo. 

“Zimbi izinto Mthiyane. Ngicabanga ukuthi ngithinte 
amaphoyisa asedolobheni ngiwacele ukuba azongisiza, sithungathe 
lesi sigebengu.” 

“Niyosithungatha emakhabeni Kaputeni?” 

“Cha. Phela naso Zondo, asiyona ingane ekhasela eziko. 
Sizobalekela endlini yaso ngoba asinalo ulwazi lokuthi besizofuna 
sona esikoleni. Asazi nokuthi umngani waso usinike yonke 

158 



imininingwane emayelana naso. Thina sizongena ngokuhlwa 
siyothungatha umuzi omkhulu wakwaMbhele kwaBhekuzulu. 
Uma sesiwutholile lowo muzi, kuzobe sekulula kithi ukuthola 
lapho ehlala khona uNguzunga. Hhawu, uzothi engazelele, 
athuke usukakwe wonke umuzi wakhe. Ziyobe sezimshele njalo.” 

“Mina angiboni kanjalo Kaputeni. Ngicabanga ukuthi 
asizukuya endlini yaso lesi sigebengu. Sizomane sishaye utshani 
siye lapho okungeyukuba lula khona ukuba sibanjwe. Kodwa-ke 
ngalawa mazwi angiqondile ukuphikisana nombono wakho. Nina 
ningaya kosibheka kwaBhekuzulu. Uma ningasitholi, nizame 
elinye isu.” 

“Ngiyakuzwa Mthiyane. Kungase kwenzeke ngempela lokhu 
okushoyo. Ukuba bengizokwazi, bengizothola isithombe sakhe 
uNguzunga ukuze ngisisebenzise uma kungukuthi siyehluleka 
ukumthola namuhla.” 

“Sengathi yisu elingcono lelo Kaputeni. Singathathwa leso 
sithombe sinikwe izintatheli ukuze kwaziswe umphakathi 
ngoNguzunga. Uma umphakathi uthuke wamelamela, uzobe 
usuthinta amaphoyisa aseduze bese eboshwa.” 

“Ngumbono omuhle lowo Zondo. Kodwa manje inkinga 
enginayo ngukuthi, sizotholakalaphi isithombe salo mfana?” 

“Kulula lokho Kaputeni. Njengoba abafundi baseBonokuhle 
benezigqebhezana ezinezithombe zabo, kusobala ukuthi zikhona 
ezinye izithombe zabo ezisala esikoleni. Uzosithola nesalo mfana.” 

“Uqinisile Mthiyane. Kuzomele ngisithole kusashisa nje. 
Ngimfuna phakathi esitokisini lo mfana.” 

“Utheni uSokhela lapho usumphenya?” Wabuza uZondo 
elangazelele ukuzwa ukuthi uzothini uKaputeni. 

“Uphenyo lubucayi kabi Zondo. Ludinga isikhathi 
nobunyoninco. Alukufuni ukuxhamazela. Angibange 
ngisamphenya ngoba besengijahe ukuphuthumisa laba abalimele 

159 



esibhedlela. Kodwa-ke uma ngisuka lapha, ngizoqonda khona 
esikoleni ngiyokwenza uphenyo. Ngiwabonile amehlo kaSokhela 
ukuthi angixoxela indaba.” 

Athule isikhashana uZondo, kubonakale ukuthi kukhona 
akuhlanganisayo engqondweni. Khona manjalo ezwakale esethi, 
“Pho, uthi akuyena nje lo Nguzunga ndini owasihlasela kuthangi 
kwaMnguni?” 

“Nguyena Zondo. Angikufuniseli lokho. Nonogada wesikole 
wabulawa nguyena. Amabhosho engiwatholile ayangifakazela. 
Ayefana nalawo enabuya nawo.” 

Koma amathe kuZondo uma ezwa uKaputeni ekhuluma 
kanjena. Wayefisa ukumbona kahle lo mfana wesikole onesibindi 
kangaka! Phela wayemuzwe kahle lo mfana lapho ebahlasela 
ukuthi uyinyakanyaka okwesibongo sakhe. Kazi lezi zibhamu 
ahlasela ngazo wazithathaphi? Zona-ke lezi abephuca zona, 
wazishonisaphi? Konje kungenzeka ukuthi nazo lezi ahlasela 
ngazo wazithola ngokuzephuca amaphoyisa? 

Ngemuva kokuthula isikhashana, uZondo wezwakala esethi, 
“Lonakele izwe Kaputeni. Lonakele sikhona sibhekile.” 

“Lonakele Mthiyane. Okumele sikwazi ngukuthi lonakele nje, 
lonakalele thina maphoyisa. Yithina esinamandla okulilungisa 
libuyele esimweni salo. Yinye kuphela indlela esizolilungisa ngayo, 
wukuba siqinise izifociya.” 

“Kunjalo Kaputeni. Umphakathi wethembele kithina.” 
Wawasho uZondo lawo mazwi, ewasho ngomlomo 
owawunokungabaza. Unembeza wawusho okwehlukile. 
Wawumlahla ngokungazinikeli kwabo ngokuphelele emsebenzini 
wabo. 

“Usenjani uMnguni, Mthiyane?” 

“Use-ICU Kaputeni. Kusekubi impela kuyena.” 

“Mina ngithandazela ukuthi aphile yize kubukeka sengathi 

160 



lokho kuzokwenzeka ngemuva kwesikhathi eside. Uma eke 
washona, kuyobe konakele. Uyophuma phambili uSokhela ngoba 
buzobe bungasekho ubufakazi obuphathekayo nobungamgquma 
ejele iminyaka.” 

“Ithemba kalilahlwa Kaputeni. Ngizizwa nginetheba lokuthi 
useyokumphonsa umbalane.” 

Abuke iwashi uKaputeni. “Isikhathi siyangishiya Mthiyane. 
Ngisaphuthuma eBonokuhle.” 

“Phuthuma Kaputeni. Sesiyozwa ngawe ukuthi uziphendulele 
wathini uSokhela. Ungakhohlwa ukucela isithombe sesigebengu 
esikoleni.” 

“Ngiyokwazisa Zondo. Ube ngcono-ke.” Asho ethatha 
izinyawo uKaputeni eyophuma emyango. 

UMaCele wavuka ekuseni umzimba utubekile. Kwakungathi 
ubebhonywa ngomshiza ubusuku bonke. Wayehlushwa 
ngamaphupho amabi. Kanti noMnguni wayesenyamalele 
engamshayeli ucingo. Wayengazi ngempela ukuthi 
kwakwenzekani. Lapha ekhaya kwaMnguni ucingo lwakhona 
lwalungaphumi. Lwalungena kuphela. UMaCele wayecabanga 
ukuthi avuke ekuseni alungisele izingane ukuya esikoleni bese 
ehamba eyoshayela uMnguni ucingo esigxotsheni socingo. 
Wayezomshayela enombolweni yaseBonokuhle ukuze ezwe 
ukuthi usaphila yini. Kwakunovadlwana olwalumshaya lumqede 
amandla. Wayengazi nokho ukuthi lwalubikani. 

Nebala, kwathi ukuba zihambe izingane ziye esikoleni, 
uMaCele wahluthulela endlini wanikela khona esigxotsheni 
socingo esasingasesangweni lesikole saseFezokuhle. Wafike 
wafaka inombolo yaseBonokuhle. Lwakhala ucingo lwaze 
lwadela lungabanjwa muntu. Ngaleso sikhathi ikhanda 
likaMaCele laligqamuka amalangabi, lisho ukumlahla phansi. 

161 



Waqalaza isitodlwana esasiseduze, wabona ukuthi sase sivuliwe. 
Wabuyisela isibambo socingo maqede washona khona. Wafike 
wathenga amaphilisi ekhanda wase ewaphuzela khona lapho. 
Wathi ukuphumula kancane laze laphola ikhanda. Wazihudula 
waphindela esigxotsheni socingo wafike wafaka inombolo 
yaseBonokuhle. 

“KuseBonokuhle, ngingakusiza?” kubuza umabhalane. 

“Sawubona dadewethu. Ngunkosikazi Mnguni okhuluma 
naye. Ngingamthola uThish’omkhulu?” kubuza uMaCele ebambe 
umoya. 

“UThish’omkhulu akekho esikoleni,” kuphendula 

umabhalane. 

“Uzobuya nini?” 

“Anginalo ulwazi ngalokho. Ngizocela ukuthi ubambe ukuze 
ngikubizele uthisha uZuma uzoxoxa naye. Nguyena ozokuchazela 
konke ngoThish’omkhulu.” Washo la mazwi umabhalane 
sekumcacela ukuthi wayekhuluma nonkosikazi kaMnguni. 

“Ngiyabonga dadewethu.” Lumuthi heqe uvalo uMaCele. 
Azibuze aziphendule ukuthi kungani le ntombi ithi izobiza 
omunye uthisha ukuze amchazele konke ngomyeni wakhe. Yini 
lena ezochazwa nguZuma yena umabhalane angenakukwazi 
ukuyichaza? Lumphinde futhi uvalo uMaCele. Zimfome izandla. 
Limshiye igazi. Azame ukuziqinisa. 

Ngemuva kwesikhashana elindile uMaCele, ezwakale uZuma 
ebingelela ngalena ocingweni. 

“Yebo mfowethu. Ngingunkosikazi Mnguni. Bengicela 
ukuxoxa noThish’omkhulu.” Asho ngeliphansi uMaCele. 
Abambe umoya alindele impendulo. Kufike kuZuma ukuthi, 
mhlawumbe ngunkosikazi kaThish’omkhulu wakhe lona 
akhuluma naye. Abuze. “Ingabe ngunkosikazi kaThish’omkhulu 
lona engikhuluma naye?” 

162 



“Impela mfowethu, kunjalo.” 

“Hawu! Ngiyabonga ukuthi usithinte dadewethu. 
Besisadidekile ukuthi sizokuthola kanjani ukuze sikwazise 
ngokwehlele uThish’omkhulu.” 

Lumshaye luphindelele uvalo uMaCele. “Kanti kwenzekeni 
ngomyeni wami?” 

Alizwe uZuma izwi likaMaCele ukuthi linokwethuka 
nokusaba okukhulu. “UThish’omkhulu usesibhedlela.” 

“Usesibhedlela? Kwenzenjani?” Abuze ngezwi eliqhaqhazelayo 
uMaCele. 

“Yindatshana elulekile dadewethu, kodwa ngizozama 
ukuyifingqa. Kuthangi ngovivi, uThish’omkhulu wathola 
ucingo olwaluvela kumuntu angamazi lumsongela ngokuthi 
uzokufa uma engashiyi lapha esikoleni. Ngaleso sizathu wabe 
esecela amaphoyisa ukuba amgade. Nebala amgade imini 
yonke lapha esikoleni, nasebusuku lapho ahlala khona. Kwathi 
ebusuku kungazelele muntu, bangenelwa yisigebengu sihlomile. 
Sababamba sababopha ngezintambo maqede sabashaya sabashiya 
beyizicaba. Bathathwa baphuthunyiswa esibhedlela saseMawozi 
lapho belaliswe khona.” 

“Awu kodwa Nkulunkulu wami! Ngangishilo ukuthi lo thisha 
ongamfuni ubaba kaNoluthando, uzogcina embulele. Uthi kodwa 
akalimalanga kakhulu umyeni wami, mfowethu?” 

“Yena ulimele ngokusho kwabahlengikazi. Nokho basinikile 
ithemba lokuthi uzosinda nakuba kuzothatha isikhathi ukuba 
alulame.” 

Zithi photho photho izinyembezi ezihlathini zikaMaCele. 
“Kodwa Nkosi yami, ubesengaze afe impela nje umyeni wami 
afele isikhundla? Bekunani ukuba asishiye leso sikole abuyele 
ekhaya? Ziningi izikole ezingcono kunalesi asifunayo.” Washo 
ebalisa uMaCele kwaze kwazwela kuZuma. 

163 



“Sonke sishaqekile dadewethu yilesi senzo ngoba asiqondi 
ukuthi ubangiswani uThish’omkhulu. Asazi ukuthi singathi 
woneni, kubani? Thina sazi imisebenzi yakhe emihle. Uhlala 
elwela umuntu omnyama ukuba afunde. Ngineqiniso lokuthi 
nabazali babafundi bangangifakazela kulokhu engikushoyo.” 

“Sikuphi sona leso sibhedlela akuso?” 

“Sikhona lapha esifundeni saseMtshezi. Uma uya khona, 
ungagibela amatekisi asuka lapho eMgungundlovu aye 
eMtshezi. Uma ufika edolobheni, uthathe aya eLoskop, bese 
ucela umshayeli ukuba akwehlise esikoleni saseBonokuhle. Uthi 
ungafika esikoleni, ucele uthisha uZuma. Ngizobe sengikulindele. 
Sizohamba ngemoto yomngani wami siyobona uThish’omkhulu 
esibhedlela. 

“Uyobe ungisizile mntanabantu. Ngisazokwazisa uMfundisi 
kuqala ngale nto esivelele. Mhlawumbe naye angafisa ukuhamba.” 

“Angiboni nkinga kulokho dadewethu. Mina ngiyokuzwa 
ngawe ukuthi nibonisane nafikaphi noMfundisi. Uzobe 
usungazisa ngocingo ukuze ngihlele konke.” 

“Ngiyawubonga umusa wakho mfowethu. Usuyokuzwa 
ngami-ke. Usale kahle.” 

Akabange esasuka esigxotsheni socingo uMaCele. 
Wamane wafaka inombolo kaMfundisi uDubazana. Ngeshwa 
akamtholanga. Ingane eyaphendula ucingo yabika ukuthi uqeda 
ukuphuma nonkosikazi wakhe ngemoto. Babehambisele omunye 
umzalwane umkhuleko. 

Wasuka esigxotsheni socingo uMaCele waphindela ekhaya. 
Laliphithene ikhanda. Ingqondo yayizula ezinkalweni, 
nobuhlungu bekhanda bungasezwakali. Wafika ekhaya 
wakhwishiza kwazise ukuthi wayehambe engayihlanzile indlu. 
Wayesebenza, ekhuluma yedwa okohlanya. Wayebalisa zigobhoze 
izinyembezi, zehle ezihlathini. Wayephinde amsole umyeni wakhe 

164 



ngokwala ukubophisa uSokhela, athi ukhona uNkulunkulu 
uzomlwela. 

Ayengakapheli amahora amabili ebuyile uMaCele ngesikhathi 
ezwa ukuduma kwemoto ngaphandle. KwakunguMfundisi 
uDubazana. Yangena esangweni imoto yafike yama egcekeni 
lomuzi. Wehla uMfundisi elandelwa ngunkosikazi wakhe 
uMaMthembu, baqonda endlini yokuphumula. Kwaba 
wukungena nje wabathela ngezinyembezi uMaCele bengakayibuzi 
nakuyibuza impilo. Bavele bafunda kwezabo ukuthi isimo 
sasimanzonzo kuleli khaya. UMaCele wababikela konke 
ayekuzwile ngomyeni wakhe. Wabachazela nangosizo uthisha 
uZuma alethembise kuye. 

“Awu, kuphela nasozwaneni kimi ndodakazi. Usathane 
usemzingele waze wamthola umzalwane madoda!” kubabaza 
umfundisi ngokumangala. 

“Umtholile Baba. Ngangishilo kubaba kaNoluthando ukuthi 
kudingeka alubikele amaphoyisa lolu daba lwalo thisha olwa 
naye. Pho-ke amadoda anenkani. Ngaso sonke isikhathi afuna 
kugcine wona ngisho sekungasafanele. Ukuba wangilalela ubaba 
kaNoluthando, ngabe akalimalanga.” 

“Kahle mntanami. Wayengeke abophise umuntu engenabo 
ubufakazi obuqanda ikhanda ngaye. Kodwa-ke uNkulunkulu 
ukhona. Uyomhlenga umzalwane wethu aze alulame. Ungalilahli 
ithemba ndodakazi. Mina ngibona ukuthi singabe sisachitha 
sikhathi. Asivele siphuthume khona esibhedlela njengamanje. 
Asizukumhlupha lo thisha okwethembise usizo. Ngiyasazi 
lesi sibhedlela asishoyo. Ngangijwayele ukuhambisela iziguli 
umkhuleko khona ngesikhathi ngisasebenzela eMazizini 
kwelaseBergville,” kuchaza uMfundisi. Kwakungumkhuba wakhe 
ukusukumela phezulu uma kunezinto ezibuhlungu ezehlele 
abazalwane. Wayengubaba ngeqiniso. 

165 



UMaCele wacela indodakazi kamakhelwane wakhe ukuba 
imbonele izingane uma sezibuyile esikoleni. 

Esekulungele ukuhamba uMaCele, bangena emotweni. Yasuka 
yashosholoza yabheka edolobheni laseMgungundlovu. Yathi 
ingangena edolobheni, yase ithatha umgwaqo obheke esiyingini 
lapho eyajikeleza khona yaze yathola umzila onguthelawayeka 
obheke phezulu eGauteng. Yawunamathela njalo yaze yawulahla 
isiqondene nedolobha laseMtshezi. Yachezukela ngasesandleni 
sobunxele, yathatha umgwaqo obheke eLoskop. Yashosholoza 
njalo yaze yayongena esibhedlela saseMawozi. 

Bangeniswa e-ICU, bamfica emubi kakhulu uMnguni. 
Wayendwazile engacwayizi. Lesi simo sabethusa kakhulu. 
UMaCele wethuka ngendlela yokuthi kwaze kwadingeka 
ukuba akhishwe e-ICU ngoba wayengasakwazi nokuzibamba. 
Wayekhala, kukubi impela. UMfundisi wenza umkhuleko 
omfushane esibhedlela maqede bangena emotweni bahamba. 

UMaCele wacela uMfundisi ukuba abedlulise eBonokuhle 
ukuze babonane noZuma, abachazele ukuthi amaphoyisa ayethini 
ngesimo somyeni wakhe. 

UMfundisi wacela iphoyisa elaliqaphe esangweni lasesibhedlela 
ukuba libayalele umgwaqo oya esikoleni saseBonokuhle. 
Nangempela labayalela kahle kakhulu. Yasuka imoto yaqonda 
esikoleni. Ngenhlanhla bamfica engakahambi uZuma ukuya 
ekhaya nakuba isikole sase siphumile. 

UZuma wabachazela oMaCele sonke isimo njengoba sinjalo. 
Wabachazela nokuthi amaphoyisa ayephezu kwalo lolu daba. 
Uphenyo lwalwenziwa nangaphakathi esikoleni. Wezwakalisa 
nethemba lokuthi babezoboshwa bonke ababethinteka kuzo 
zonke lezi zinto ezazenzeka kulesi sikole. 

UMfundisi wanika uZuma inombolo yocingo lakwakhe 
wamcela ukuba abazise ngokuqhubeka kwempilo kaMnguni 

166 



kanye nangophenyo lwamaphoyisa. Bavalelisa. 

Yasuka lapho imoto kaMfundisi uDubazana yabheka 
eMgungundlovu. Endleleni babengayivali imilomo 
oMaCele ngendlela ababemfice egula ngayo uMnguni kanye 
nangokucekeleka kwesikole phansi. UMfundisi wayelokhu 
ekhuleke njalo ngenhliziyo ukuba zibanjwe izelelesi ukuze zijeze 
ngendlela efanele. 

Sebefikile ekhaya oMaCele, uMfundisi wenza umkhuleko 
wethembisa nokuthi bazode bemhlola uMaCele bamlethele 
nomkhuleko. Wakubeka nokuthi bazode bemlanda okungenani 
kanye ngeviki bayohlola uMnguni esibhedlela aze alulame. 
Bavalelisa bahamba. 

167 



ISAHLUKO SESHUMI NAMBILI 

UKaputeni wehla emotweni waqonda ehhovisi likamabhalane. 
Wafike wacela ukubona uSokhela. Wamkhombisa umabhalane 
ihhovisi lelo. Wasuka lapho uKaputeni waqonda khona. 
Kwakuvaliwe kodwa uSokhela ekhona ngaphakathi. Phela unkabi 
lo wayengazange aye ekilasini ayofundisa izingane ngemuva 
kwesigameko esasimehlele ekuseni. Wayengafisi ngisho ukuvula 
umlomo axoxe nabalingani bakhe ngomkhuba kaNguzunga. 

Kwathi lapho esahlezi uSokhela ejulile ngomcabango, wezwa 
uKaputeni ezibika emnyango. 

“Ngena Kaputeni,” kusho uSokhela esukuma. Walungisa 
isihlalo ayezohlala kuso uKaputeni. Wangena uKaputeni waqonda 
kuSokhela. Baxhawulana base behlala phansi. 

“Sengibuyile Mahlobo. Ingabe sibaleke njalo isigebengu 
sangabheka emuva?” 

“Kunjalo Kaputeni. Asibonakali nangokhalo.” 

“Kufanele ngithole isithombe saso ukuze ngisisebenzise uma 
kungukuthi siyehluleka ukusithola. Sikhona nje isithombe saso 
eninaso lapha esikoleni?” 

“Ngethemba kanjalo Kaputeni. Umuntu ongakusiza 
nguZuma. Nguyena osebenza ngalezo zinto. Banjani 
oSayitsheni?” 

“Balaliswe esibhedlela. Bazohlinzwa kukhishwe izinhlamvu.” 

“Ewu, kulukhuni kulo mhlaba esiphila kuwo! Ngubani 
owabe azi ukuthi lesi sikhathi siyofika sesihlaselwa yizingane 
esizifundisayo zifune ukusibulala ngaphandle kwezizathu? Bheka 
nje uSayitsheni ulinyazwe yingane eluhlaza cwe ethi ulamulela 
uthisha. Impela lulahlekile usiko lokuhlonipha kubantwana bethu. 
Abasahlukile ezinjeni zona ezijika zilume izandla eziziphakelayo.” 

168 



“Yiqiniso lelo Mahlobo. Kodwa kwesinye isikhathi uthisha 
uba senkingeni ngoba kusuke kunento ethile embi emhlanganise 
nomfundi asuke exabene naye. Uma kukhona phakathi kwabo 
osephula izibopho abazenzile, kuyaliwa.” 

“Uthi kuyenzeka lokho Kaputeni, ukuthi uthisha ahlangane 
nomfundi ngobubi?” 

“Bakhohlakele abantu lapha ngaphandle Sokhela. 
Esikhundleni sokuthi bafundise izingane, bayazibulala. Ingane 
igcina isingungqondongqondo kwezobugebengu ngenxa kathisha 
ongcolile osuke efuna ukufeza izinhloso zakhe ngayo. Akubona 
bonke othisha abawenza ngokwethembeka umsebenzi wabo. 
Abanye balova bekhona esikoleni. Yinto endala lena eyayenzeka 
nathi sisafunda.” Asho uKaputeni entshontsha uSokhela 
ngamehlo. Amehlo kaSokhela ashalaze. Akuphawule lokho 
uKaputeni. 

“Ngidabukela leli khehla leNkosi elilimale ngephutha.” 
Asho uSokhela ezama ukugqiba unembeza owawumququda 
njengelumbo labathakathi. Wayengathandi ukuthi uKaputeni 
aqhubeke nale nkulumo yakhe emayelana nokonakala kothisha. 

“Ukuqhamuka kwalelo khehla kusiwezile isigebengu. 
Ukuba aliqhamukanga, ngabe ngisilahle phansi, ngimfunge 
uPhoshozwayo. Siyohamba sisinda.” 

“Kungcono nje ngoba alilimalanga kakhulu leli khehla,” 
kuphawula uSokhela ebheke phansi. 

Ekugcineni uKaputeni ahlale phezu kodaba olumlethe kuleli 
hhovisi likaSokhela. 

“Mfowethu, siyangishiya isikhathi. Eqinisweni ngize lapha 
ukuzokwenza uphenyo ngale ngxabano ebikade iphakathi kwakho 
noNguzunga.” 

Bushintshe ubuso bukaSokhela bube mnyama khwishi! 
Kulokhu amehlo akhe anamathela kuKaputeni. “Hawu! Yikuphi 

169 



futhi manje ofuna ukukwazi nokungaphezulu kwalokhu 
engikutshele khona ekuseni?” Awubuze lowo mbuzo uSokhela 
esewathe njo amehlo kuKaputeni. 

“Ngifuna ukwazi ukuthi nibangani?” 

“Hhayi bo! Ngishilo nje ekuseni.” 

“Ngingajabula uma ungase uphendule umbuzo wami 
Sokhela, usho konke okwaziyo ushiye ongakwazi.” Asho umfo 
kaMchunu evula idokodo ebhala okuthile kulona. Kuye ngokuba 
nzima kakhulu kuSokhela. Awasuse amehlo kuKaputeni abheke 
phansi. Azibuze ngenhliziyo ukuthi kanti lo muntu akezile yini 
ukuzofuna isithombe sikaNguzunga? Isingena ngakuphi manje le 
ndaba yasekuseni? 

“Shono-ke phela Sokhela sizwe. Nibangani noNguzunga?” 

“Angazi kuyena Kaputeni. Mina ngokwami ngazi ukuthi 

ayikho into esiyibangayo.” 

“Uqonde ukungitshela ukuthi uyakusukela nje?” 

“Ngingasho kanjalo Kaputeni.” 

“Kukhona yini lapho enake nahilizisana khona?” 

“Lutho Kaputeni.” 

Wayebuza imibuzo eminingi uKaputeni isandla sibhala igama 

negama alishoyo uSokhela. 

“Ukhona yini omunye uthisha owake wahlaselwa yilo mfana 
ngamazwi noma ngesikhali?” 

“Akekho Kaputeni. Ubeqala ngqa ngami selokhu afika lapha 

esikoleni. Mhlawumbe ubedle izidakamizwa nje.” 

“Uyazidla yini izidakamizwa?” 

“Wukucabangela nje Kaputeni. Ngingeze ngakuqinisekisa 

lokho.” 
“Ubumazi ukuthi uphatha izikhali?” 

170 



“Cha. Bengikuqabuka lokho namuhla.” 

“Kukhona ukuhlobana okwaziyo phakathi kukaBen Mabanga 

noNguzunga?” 

“Ngingeke ngikwazi lokho ngoba angijwayelene nezingane.” 

“Wazini ngokumiswa kukaBen esikoleni?” 

“UThish’omkhulu wasola ukuthi kwakunguyena lona 
owamsongela ngokumbulala, nokwakulandela ukungezwani 
kwabo ngesikhathi oBen bezoxoxa naye benguMkhandlu Omele 
Abafundi. Lezi zinsolo yizona kanye ezaba yimbangela yokumiswa 
kukaBen ukuza esikoleni.” 

“Bunjani ubudlelwano phakathi kwakho noThish’omkhulu?” 

Adonse kakhulu umoya uSokhela aphinde awudedele. “Buhle 
Kaputeni.” 

“Njengesekela likaMnguni, kwakuphatha kanjani ukufika 
kwakhe lapha esikoleni ezothatha izintambo zokuphatha?” 

Ambuke futhi uSokhela lo muntu omphenya kangaka! 
Lumshaye ome uvalo. Afikelwe yizinsolo zokuthi mhlawumbe 
uKaputeni usethole okuthile ngaye noNguzunga. Kodwa aphinde 
awuphebeze lowo mcabango ngoba uNguzunga usagcwele 

amathafa, akakabanjwa. Azihlele bese ephendula. 

“Kwakungiphatha kahle.” 

“Ingabe imfundo yakho yayingeke yini ikubeke ekutheni 

uma sekuqokwa uThish’omkhulu omusha ngemuva kokuhamba 
kukaChonco, kuqokwe wena?” 

“Ngifunde ngokwanele Kaputeni. Ngangingasibamba kuthule 
umoya lesi sikole.” 

Ambukisise uKaputeni. Aphawule ukukhathazeka 
okugqamayo ebusweni bukaSokhela uma echaza imfundo anayo 
kanye nekhono lokuphatha. Lokho kumnike ithemba lokuthi 
usahamba emgudwini okuyiwona nozomhlomulisa. 

171 



“Ngokwakho ukucabanga, ubona ukuthi kungani uMnyango 
wezeMfundo ukhethe ukuphumela ngaphandle uyofuna 
uThish’omkhulu kunokuba uqoke wena?” 

“Yikhona kanye lokho okwangimangaza nami Kaputeni.” 

“Waphatheka kabi?” 

Umethuse lowo mbuzo uSokhela. Abone ukuthi selucishe 
lwashelela ulimi. Azame ukuyilungisa impendulo yakhe. 
“Ngiqonde ukuthi kwabamangaza abaningi.” 

“Wazama ukuthola eMnyangweni wezeMfundo ukuthi 
kungani uqoke umuntu wangaphandle ube ukhona wena futhi 
ungowokuzalwa kule ndawo?” 

“Angikucabanganga lokho ngoba vele ngangingenandaba 
nalesi sikhundla. Mina ngiyasihlonipha isinqumo soMnyango 
wezeMfundo. Uma kungukuthi wona wambona engcono 
uMnguni kunami, yayingekho into engangingayenza.” 

“Kodwa wawungathokoza ukuba kwaqokwa wena, akunjalo?” 

“Ngicabanga ukuthi noma ngubani, wayengathokoza. Phela 
ukukhushulelwa esikhundleni esiphakeme kusho inqubekela 
phambili.” 

“Njengoba ungitshele ukuthi niphathene kahle 
noThish’omkhulu wakho, kungani pho aqoke uZuma ukuba 
ameseke okwesikhashana ube ukhona wena?” 

Kuntwele ezansi kuSokhela. Abone kahle ukuthi 
indaba yayinoZuma. Nguyena owabikela amaphoyisa 
ngokungabhemelani kwabo inqawe benoMnguni. Kwamcacela 
ukuthi lukhulu olusina lumjeqeza. Phela wayengumsolwa kukho 
konke okwakwenzeka lapha esikoleni. Wakhumbula ukuthi 
engakaqali ukumphenya uKaputeni, uke waphawula ngawothisha 
abakhohlakele nabasebenzisa izingane ukuze kufezeke izinhloso 
zabo. 

172 



“Ngicabanga ukuthi wambona engcono kunami.” 

“Kwakuphatha kabi lokho?” 

“Ngaphazamiseka.” 

“Wakuveza lokho kuphazamiseka kwakho kuyena noma 

kwabanye othisha” 

“Angizange Kaputeni.” 

“Wayekelani?” 

“Umuntu nomuntu unelungelo lokuziqokela lowo ambona 
engawenza kangcono umsebenzi kunalowo angamethembi. 
Mhlawumbe ngangingakuveza ukukhathazeka kwami ukuba 
iholo lami lalizokwehliswa.” 

“Ngiyakuzwa Sokhela, uyakhuluma. Pho awucabangi ukuthi 
lezi zigameko ezenzeka lapha esikoleni kungenzeka ukuthi 
zenziwa ngumphakathi ngoba ungamfuni lo Thish’omkhulu 
omusha?” 

“Uma ungamfuni umuntu olethwe nguMnyango 
wezeMfundo, uzobe ufuna bani ngoba awazi lutho ngokuphathwa 
kwezikole?” 

“Asazi phela Sokhela, yibona abantu abaziyo.” 

“Angiboni kanjalo Kaputeni. Umphakathi walapha awusoze 
wazifaka ezintweni ezingaqondene ngqo nawo.” 

“Uzothini uma ngithi wawungakwenza lokho umphakathi 
ngoba ulwela wena njengomfana wendawo ukuze uqokwe ube 

nguThish’omkhulu.?” 

“Angazi-ke lapho Kaputeni.” 

Alivale idokodo uKaputeni. “Ngiyasibonga isikhathi ongiphe 
sona Sokhela. Ngaphambi kokuba ngiphume kuleli hhovisi, 
ngifisa ukukutshela ukuthi angikaqedi ukukuphenya. Okwamanje 
ngizothatha lesi sitatimende sakho ngisisebenzise ophenyweni 
lokulimala kukaMnguni. Uma kukhona okuhlanganayo, 

173 



kuyoqhuma nhlamvana dadewethu kababa! Uyoyikhotha 
imbenge yomile.” 

“Phela usuyangisongela manje Kaputeni. Ngichazile ukuthi 
angazi lutho ngokulimala kukaThish’omkhulu.” 

Asukume uKaputeni. “Nami angisho ukuthi kukhona 
okwaziyo Sokhela. Bengikwazisa ukuthi uphenyo lusazoqhubeka. 
Lokhu kuseyisiqalo.” 

Avalelise uKaputeni, aphume ahambe. 

“Yehheni! Zashintsha izinto madoda! Konje ibizwa ngokuthini 
into enjena? Phela ayangena manje amanzi kule ndlu. Kusobala 
ukuthi kukhona lapho evuza khona. Ngihle ngabona kwasekuseni 
ukuthi kukhona okusolekayo ngami. Phela utsheliwe lo 
muntu ngami. Yimisebenzi kaZuma yonke lena. Sekuyacaca 
manje ukuthi la maphoyisa abezongiphenya ekuseni. Nakhoke 
esezithela kule mpi yethu nalolu hlanya. Kanti ngempela 
ungifunani uZuma? Akumanelisi yini ukuhlwitha isikhundla 
sami? Akafi ngani kodwa bakithi? Kufa, luphi udonsi lwakho na?” 

Asukume uSokhela ayovala isicabha sehhovisi lakhe. Abuyele 
esihlalweni sakhe afike ahlale phansi. 

“EkaNguzunga indaba iyangihlanyisa. Kuthi angihayize uma 
ngiyicabanga. Ngimbone kahle ukuthi uyimamba egadla igijima. 
Uyingozi ngazo zonke izindlela kimi. Uma embopha amaphoyisa, 
uyongembula izinqe zihlale obala okwento yembuzi. Zonke lezi 
zigameko ezenzekile lapha esikoleni ngenxa yami, ziyongibhadlisa 
ejele iminyakanyaka. Amajaji ayongibona ngingasakufanele 
ukuphila nomphakathi. Ngakolunye uhlangothi, uma amaphoyisa 
ehluleka ukumbopha uNguzunga, uyongibulala. Impela basuke 
beqinisile abadala uma bethi, akukho qili lazikhotha emhlane. 
Bheka manje ukuthi ngikuphi. Angifuni ukuboshwa kanti nokufa 
ngiyakwesaba. Ngizokwenzenjani ukuze ngiphephe kulezi zinto 
zozimbili? Wo, ngaze ngaziyala bakithi!” 

174 



Asukume futhi uSokhela athi ukuzulazula ehhovisi lakhe abuye 
ahlale phansi. 

“Akusaphephile nokuba lapha esikoleni. Angangena noma 
nini uNguzunga angibulale. Bekungcono kusekhona onogada. 
Ubengeke angene kalula nesibhamu. Ngikhuluma nje angimazi 
ukuthi ukuphi futhi ucabangani ngemali yakhe. Nasekhaya 
akusaphephile. Angase angihlasele khona. Ngiyotholwa 
sengazipholela kudala njengoba noMaMhlongo engekho nje. 
Nalapha esikoleni akusafanele ukuba ngisale ngemuva. Kufanele 
ngihambe kuqala singakaphumi isikole. Ngisola sengathi uzobuya 
lo mfana azongisoconga.” 

Yathi ingakhala insimbi eyala abafundi ukuba bahlanze 
amakilasi abafundela kuwo, wasukuma uSokhela. Waqoqa zonke 
izinto ayefike nazo maqede wahluthulela ehhovisi wahamba. 

Wathi angafika esiteshini samaphoyisa uKaputeni, wathatha 
ucingo waxhumana nesiteshi sasedolobheni laseMtshezi. Walubika 
lonke udaba kumphathisiteshi. Wase emcela ukuba amthumelele 
idlanzana lamaphoyisa ayezohamba nalo kusihlwa bayohlasela 
uNguzunga kwaBhekuzulu. Umphathisiteshi wamethembisa 
ukumthumelela amaphoyisa ayisikhombisa ayezosebenza naye 
uKaputeni aze abuye lawa awakhe esibhedlela. 

Nangempela atheleka ngehora lesihlanu ntambama 
amaphoyisa eLoskop. Amfica uKaputeni esemi ngomumo. 
Ngenhlanhla elinye lawo la maphoyisa lalingelakhona 
kwaBhekuzulu futhi liwazi umuzi wakwaMbhele. 

Alinda amaphoyisa kwaze kwagamanxa ihora lesikhombisa 
kusihlwa. Angena ezinqoleni zomsebenzi anikela khona 
kwaBhekuzulu. Afika kahle sekuhlwile. Izimoto azishiya 
budebuduze nomuzi wakwaMbhele, ase ehla ngezinyawo 
aqonda khona kwaMbhele. Afike abuza lapho okwakuhlala 

175 



khona uNguzunga. Bawayalela. Asuka lapho aqonda khona. 
Lase ligamenxe ihora lesishiyagalombili, nawo esenethemba 
lokuthi azomfica esekhona uNguzunga. Noma ngabe wayebaleke 
ngezinyawo uNguzunga wadabula izinkalo eya kwaBhekuzulu, 
wayezobe esefikile ngaleso sikhathi. 

Esefikile amaphoyisa endlini kaNguzunga, amanye awukaka 
umuzi. UKaputeni nelinye iphoyisa baqonda ngqo emnyango 
wendlu. Babecabanga ukuthi wayeselele uNguzunga ngoba 
kwakumnyama ngaphakathi. Uma befika emnyango, bakhangwa 
yingidi. Abaqondanga ukuthi yayisho ukuthini. Babengaqondi 
noma wayeseke wafika uNguzunga waphinde wahamba noma 
wayengazange afike nhlobo. Kwahlwa ngempela kuKaputeni. 
Wawabiza amaphoyisa wawayala ukuba abekezele kuze kushaye 
okungenani ihora leshumi nambili ebusuku, kubonakale ukuthi 
uyafika yini uNguzunga noma cha. 

Asuka amaphoyisa aphindela ezikhundleni zawo. Alinda 
ungolinda laze lagamanxa ihora leshumi nambili. Lutho 
ukufika uNguzunga. Lase liphelile ithemba lokuthi usazofika. 
Kwawakhanyela amaphoyisa ukuthi ayesebambe isisila sehobhe, 
wayeshaye utshani umfo kaNyakanyaka. 

Aqoqana amaphoyisa, ahamba ayongena ezimotweni. Zasuka 
zashosholoza seziphindela eLoskop. 

UMgqibelo kwakuwusuku lokuphumula kothisha. 
Babethola ithuba lokuhlala nemindeni yabo bathokoze. Abanye 
babelisebenzisa lolu suku ukuyolungisa izinto ezithile ezazidinga 
isikhathi esanele. Kwesinye isikhathi babevakashela izihlobo zabo 
ezikude ngalolu suku, kujatshulwe kube kuhle. Kwabanye lolu 
suku lwalusetshenziselwa ukuya emingcwabeni. 

Kumfo kaSokhela impilo yayingqabashiya, ivutha ulaka. 
Wayewubona lo Mgqibelo wehluke kakhulu kweminye. 

176 



Wayengezukuhamba aye kodoba izinhlanzi njengasemihleni 
lapho ayehamba zibuya inhlazane aze aphindele ekhaya 
selibantubahle. Wayezohlala ekhaya alalele ukucobeka komzimba. 
Wayelibona liqoqa amafu ahlonga imvula, liye ngokuguqubala 
lihlome. Kwakubonakala ukuklwebha konyazi oluthuthumelisa 
umzimba kulandele ukuduma okuphelekezelwa yisiphepho 
esinamandla. Wayengazi ukuthi njengoba laliduma nje lalibika 
ukuthi liyomthatha nini. Ngakho-ke kwakufanele ahlale elindile. 
Izikhonkwane ezazimelusile zase ziphelelwe yisikhathi. 

Ngobusuku bangayizolo akalalanga uSokhela. Wayenovalo 
lokuthi uNguzunga wayezomhlasela uma kungukuthi amaphoyisa 
ayegcine engamtholanga. Kanti uma kungukuthi ayegcine 
emtholile, lokho kwakuzobe kuchaza ukuthi lase lingangaye ijele. 

Wayehleli edliwa ngumzwangedwa uSokhela endlini 
yokuphumula. Kwakudlala ifilimu engqondweni yakhe. Wayefisa 
sengathi angafa uNguzunga ukuze angalitholi ithuba lokumbulala 
noma lokumdalula emaphoyiseni. Kwakuthi uma ecabanga 
ngokwakumehlele ngayizolo, kuvele kuhlambuluke isisu. Umfana 
wesikole amkhombe ebusweni ngesibhamu pho? Impela ingane 
yingane. Awusoze wathemba lutho kuyona. Wayehlala ewuzwa 
ngendaba umshophi ofana nalona omehlele. Nokho wayengakaze 
akucabange ukuthi naye wawuzomehlela ngolunye usuku. Bheka 
ngoba wayesesaba ngisho nokunyakaza ngenxa kaNguzunga. 
Funa athi welula izinyawo upholisa nekhanda kanti useziholela 
emlonyeni wengwenya, imxhakathise kuphele ngaye. 

Wo, indaba yekhehla lejazi! Kwakuthi uma eyicabanga 
uSokhela kudume ikhanda. Kwakungasekho-ke nokuyolihlola 
esibhedlela ukuthi linjani ngenxa yesimo ayesezithole esekuso 
uSokhela. Wayekhathazwe ngukuthi lalilimale liza kuye esikoleni. 
Ngeshwa akakwazanga ukuthola ukuthi lalizokwenzani. 
Mhlawumbe lalizombikela izindaba ezimnandi njengoba 
lalihlukane naye limethembise ukuyoncenga amadoda endawo 

177 



ukuba abhukule kuliwe le mpi yokuhambisa uMnguni. 
Waphinde wabuzwa kakhulu ubuhlungu ngoba lalilimale ngenxa 
yengxabano eyabe iphakathi kwakhe noNguzunga. 

Lwalumbambe phansi usizi uSokhela. Bheka-ke ngoba 
wayengekho owayengamthwalisa lona ngoba lwaluyisifuba 
sakhe. Kwakungaziwa ukuthi le mfihlo yayizodaluleka nini futhi 
kanjani. Khona wayenalo ithemba lokuthi uMnguni wayengeke 
abuye esaphila kahle emqondweni esibhedlela ngendlela othisha 
ababembabaze ngayo ngesikhathi beyomhlola okokuqala. Kodwa 
futhi ukuphanjanelwa yingqondo kukaMnguni kwakungeke 
kusamsiza ngoba wayesephakathi kwetshe nesisekelo. 

Lwahamba usuku lizimukile ikhanda likaSokhela. Wayeke 
andwaze nje alandele impukane izidlulela ize inyamalale. Kwaze 
kwafika ukuhlwa engazange aphumele ngaphandle komuzi wakhe. 
Walala umzimba uthuthumela ngenxa yokwesaba ukuhlaselwa. 

178 



ISAHLUKO SESHUMI NANTATHU 

Ngosuku abaphindela ngalo emsebenzini oSayitsheni 
noZondo, uKaputeni wababizela ehhovisi lakhe waxoxa nabo. 

“Madoda, ngiyabona ukuthi seniluleme ngokwanele manje. 
Yingakho ngiwaphindisele edolobheni la maphoyisa abengisiza 
ngesikhathi ningekho. Okubuhlungu ngukuthi izigebengu 
zisidalulile emphakathini. Ziwukhombisile umphakathi ukuthi 
uthembe ubala, asimaphoyisa alutho. Asiwazi umsebenzi 
wethu. Kudala umphakathi ukhala ngobelelesi obudlangile kule 
ndawo. Izigebengu ziyatamasa nje zizenzela umathanda kodwa 
amaphoyisa akhona. Namuhla kwasanina ningofakazi kule nto 
engiyishoyo. Niphuma esibhedlela ngenxa yazo izigebengu. 
Nekhehla leNkosi lithelwe ngamachaphazelo lalimala ngenxa 
yezigebengu. Ngibonga ukuthi nalo seliphumile esibhedlela. 
Angingabazi ukuthi nalo lilindele ukusibona leso sigebengu 
sishushiswa. Manje-ke bafowethu, ngithi kini, ake sisebenze 
ngendlela engakaze ibonwe. Ababanjwe abenzi bokubi.” Asho 
uKaputeni kuthule umoya. 

Indlela ayekhuluma ngayo uKaputeni, yayehluke kakhulu 
kuleya ayeyijwayele amaphoyisa. Wayenomoya wobuntu, 
engathethi njengakuqala. Nawo amaphoyisa azizwa esefikelwa 
wumfutho wokusebenza kanzima ukuze amthokozise umphathi 
wawo. Enkulumweni yakhe wayekhombisa ukuwathemba futhi 
ewakhuthaza ngomoya omuhle. 

“Luselude ukhalo okusafanele luhanjwe zinsizwa zami. 
Nokho sengiyenzile imizamo eminingi engase iholele ekutheni 
aboshwe uNguzunga. Amaphephandaba asebhalile ngaye, 
aveza nesithombe sakhe. Imisakazo imemezela mihla yonke 
ngomklomelo oyizinkulungwane ezinhlanu zompondo 
kulowo ozoyalela amaphoyisa lapho ecashe khona. Iziteshi 

179 



zikamabonakude zisivezile isithombe sakhe. Ngiqinisile ngithi, 
ngeke adabule ngisho esethanda.” 

“Mina ngesaba ngisho nokukubheka Kaputeni. Ngizizwa 
nginesikweletu esikhulu enhliziyweni yami. Angikwenzanga 
ukuthembeka emsebenzini engawufungela ngathi ngizowenza 
ngokwethembeka. Ngixolisa kakhulu kulokho Macingwane. 
Ngifunde isifundo ngokudlala ngomsebenzi. Ngicishe ngafa 
nokufa. Awu, ngiyabuzonda utshwala! Buyazona izinto,” kusho 
uSayitsheni ngokuzisola. 

“Ithuba lisekhona Ngubane. Usenokuwukhombisa 
umphakathi ukuthi uyawazi umsebenzi wakho futhi 
uyawuhlonipha. Ngalawo mazwi ngiqonde ukusho ukuthi 
akekho umuntu ongenalo iphutha emhlabeni. Uma umuntu 
ekhombisa ukuthi uyalibona iphutha lakhe, kumele axolelwe. 
Nami ngiyakuxolela mfowethu. Ubobuqaphela kakhulu utshwala 
bungakufaki esilingweni uze uzithole usubuphuza nangesikhathi 
esingafanele.” 

“Ngiyabonga Macingwane. Ngiyazibonga nezeluleko zakho 
ezakhayo.” 

“Nami ngiyambongisa uSayitsheni, Kaputeni. 
Okungijabulisayo ngukuthi uzibonele yena amaphutha akhe. 
Nguyena futhi ozisholo ngowakhe umlomo ukuthi usezimisele 
ngokuwenza ngokwethembeka umsebenzi,” kugcizelela uZondo. 

UMnguni wayelulama ngokushesha esibhedlela. 
Nomndeni wakhe wakuphawula lokho ezinsukwini ezimbili 
ezedlule ngesikhathi uzomvakashela. Nokuvuvuka ebusweni 
kwase kwehlile. Noma odokotela babengamkhulula ukuba 
ayolulamela ekhaya, kwakungeke kusaba yinkinga. Wayesekwazi 
nokuzihambela ayoshayela umndeni wakhe ucingo khona 
lapha esibhedlela. Isikhathi esiningi wayesichitha ngokufunda 

180 



amaphephandaba namaphephabhuku. Enhliziyweni yakhe 
kwakunesifiso sokuphindela emsebenzini ngokushesha. 
Wayezimisele ukumkhipha inkani uSokhela. Wayefisa nokuthi 
sibanjwe lesi sigebengu esabahlasela ukuze kubonakale ukuthi 
yikuphi ngempela okwakuyikhona. Wayenezinsolo zokuthi 
ukulimala kwakhe kwakuncikene nokuzondwa nguSokhela. 

Ngemuva kwezinsuku ezimbili uMnguni evakashelwe 
ngumndeni wakhe noMfundisi, wethuka sekutheleka umhloli 
omkhulu uMseleku esibhedlela. Kwakungokokuqala ngqa 
ezomhlola selokhu alimala njengoba wayengekho eyothuthukisa 
ulwazi lwakhe ePitoli. Wayevamise ukumshayela ucingo ambuze 
ukuthi usenjani. 

“Namuhla ngibone kungcono ukuba ngizizele mina mathupha 
ngizokubona ngoba nakhu sengibuyile ePitoli,” kusho uMseleku 
egoba amadolo esihlalweni esasiseduze kombhede kaMnguni. 

“Usebenzile mfowethu, ungezwa ngendaba ukuthi ngangilele 
kulo mbhede,” kusho uMnguni emamatheka. 

“Kodwa usunjani emzimbeni, Qwabe?” 

“Ngizizwa ngingcono kakhulu. Angiboni ukuthi iviki elizayo 
liyongifica ngisekhona lapha esibhedlela. Ukuba kuya ngami 
ngabe ngiyadedelwa khona manje okungenani ngiyoziqedela 
ekhaya izinsuku zikadokotela. Manje udokotela ungitshele 
ukuthi kuzodingeka ukuba ngiphindele kwi X-ray ezinsukwini 
ezimbili ezizayo. Uthe ufuna ukwenza isiqiniseko sokuthi ngiphile 
ngokwanele ukuthi ngingadedelwa.” 

“Uqinisile udokotela Qwabe. Akusizi ukujaha ukuphuma 
esibhedlela singekho isiqiniseko sokuthi uphile ngokwanele. Funa 
uthi usaziphumulele ekhaya kukujikele ukufa.” 

“Khona kunjalo mfowethu, kodwa inhliziyo yami ibuhlungu 
kabi ngalesiya sikole. Ngiyazi ukuthi uZuma uthwele kanzima 
njengoba ngilapha nje. Sengimane ngiduduzwe ngukuthi othisha 

181 



abaningi bayamthanda futhi bayamhlonipha. Munye kuphela 
ongaba yinyongo kuyena.” 

“Kanti ungesabi Qwabe. UZuma usibambile isikole. UChonco 
uke wavakashela khona esikoleni izolo eyobheka ukuthi kuqhubeka 
kanjani ukufunda nokufundisa. Ubuye nombiko omuhle kakhulu.” 

“Kuyangithokozisa lokho mfowethu. Kodwa uyingozi 
uSokhela. Kofanele amqaphele kakhulu.” 

“Selimshonele lowo. Aphezu kwakhe amaphoyisa.” 

“Kuhlupha khona ukuthi abukho ubufakazi obuphathekayo 
ekutheni unesandla ekuhlukumezekeni kwesikole. Kodwa 
ngiyethemba ukuthi uma engase abanjwe lo mfana 
wakwaNyakanyaka, impela liyobe limshonele ehlane uSokhela. 
Uyodonsa iminyaka eminingi ejele, esemdalule saze sakhexa

akakwazi ukusebenzisana nabantu. Uyabathethisa, abathathe

khona esikoleni ozothatha izintambo, wawuchitha lowo mbono.

Aqalaze iwashi uMseleku abone ukuthi sesiya ngokuphela

sekunzima kanjani.”

Mina ngiyamethemba uNkulunkulu. Ngiyethemba ukuthi

abantu engisebenza nabo. Angisoze ngafana noJona owathunyelwa

engikushoyo kuzofakazeleka khona manje ngingakaphumi lapha 
esibhedlela.” 

Athule uMnguni abuke umngani wakhe emehlweni. 
Ayemphica amazwi kaMseleku. Ekuqaleni wayecabanga ukuthi

nguMnyango wezeMfundo ukuba ngizokunika nansi incwadi.” 
Asho emnika.

183

UMnguni akazikholwanga izindlebe zakhe. Wakubona

Wayenakho enhliziyweni ukuthi mhlawumbe ukuhlupheka

ukuthi ukuthatha kwakho isikhundla sokuphatha iBonokuhle

Thina-ke siyobe sesimbhalela incwadi yoMnyango wezeMfundo
