ISAHLUKO SESHUMI NANE 

Amaphoyisa ayengqubuzana ngamakhanda esiteshini 
saseLoskop. Ayemthungatha imini nobusuku uNguzunga 
kodwa engamtholi. Nokho lalisekhona ithemba lokuthi 
kwakuyokwenzeka ngolunye usuku ucilo azishaye endukwini. 
Lelo themba laliwamisa isibindi amaphoyisa futhi likhuthaza 
ubunye kuwona. USayitsheni wayenogqozi olumangalisayo. 
Wayefisa sengathi kungaba nguyena osibambayo lesi sigebengu 
ukuze akhombise uKaputeni ukuthi wayengadlali uma ethi 
uyawabona amaphutha akhe. Wayefisa nokubuyisa isithunzi 
sesiteshi saseLoskop nokwakubonakala ukuthi sasiqedwe 
wukungaziphathi kahle kwakhe. 

Ngolunye usuku kunguMgqibelo ekuseni, uSayitsheni 
wahlela ukuba adlule kwaMkhize eMandabeni ngaphambi 
kokuba aye emsebenzini. Wayefisa ukuyohlola imoto yakhe 
ukuthi yayisilungisiwe yini. Yayishayiswe ngunkosikazi wakhe 
esigxotsheni socingo. Ngenhlanhla yena akalimalanga. Selokhu 
abuya esibhedlela uSayitsheni, wayengakaze aye koyihlola. 
Nangempela wayishaya yazula imoto kahulumeni uSayitsheni 
yaqonda khona kwaMkhize. 

UMkhize wayeqeda kuvulela izinkomo ukuba ziyophunga 
imikhonto ngesikhathi kutheleka imoto yamaphoyisa emzini 
wakhe. Wavele wama ngasesangweni lesibaya okomuntu 
owayebanjwe yinomfi. Wayethukile. Uvalo lwaze lwehla lapho 
esebona ukuthi kwakungumuntu amaziyo lona owayehamba 
ngale moto . Wasondela emotweni. 

“Khabazela kaMavovo! Sikhulekile ekhaya! Isisu somhambi 
asingakanani, singangenso yenyoni!” kukhuleka uSayitsheni ehla 
emotweni eyoxhawula kuMkhize. 

“Siyabonana Mbomvu. Ewu, alusangishayanga uvalo. Ucishe 

188 



wangibona sengiqimuleka phansi nje.” 

“Uqimulwa yini?” 

“Engani phela yile moto ohamba ngayo. Zinesithunzi 
esisabekayo lezi zimoto. Ayisaphathwa-ke eyokubonakala kwazo 
sezicothoza nje ekuseni egcekeni lomuzi kusalelwe. Bonke 
omakhelwane bavele baphumele ngaphandle bafune ukubona 
kahle ukuthi kwenzekani.” 

“Musa wena bo! Imoto yomthetho iyefana nje nezimoto 
zonke. Nayo ihamba ngamasondo njengalena eyakho. Futhi 
ihamba ngawo la mafutha ehamba ngawo neyakho. Ukuphike 
lo mahluko owubabazayo Khabazela?” kubuza uSayitsheni 
emamatheka encike ngesicabha semoto. 

“Ayikho le nto oyishoyo Mbomvu. Nakuba zifana izimoto, 
kodwa lena yomthetho isebenza umsebenzi ohlukile nonesithunzi. 
Yisona-ke leso sithunzi salowo msebenzi engikhala ngaso.” 

“Uyadlala wena Khabazela. Mina ngazi ukuthi imoto 
enesithunzi yileyo yasemakhazeni. Hhayi lena oyishoyo.” 

“Kungashona ilanga siphikisana mntakaNgubane. Kakade 
sadalwa sehlukana. Nemibono yethu yehlukene.” Asho ahleke 
uMkhize. Idlule indaba yokubanga imoto. 

Ngemuva kwemizuzwana embalwa kungekho okhulumayo, 
wezwakala uMkhize esethi, “Sesilibele wukuncokola nje 
umuntu useze wakhohlwa ukuthi kade usesibhedlela Mbomvu. 
Kululamekile kodwa?” 

“Eyi, ungayiphathi leyo Khabazela. Ingifikisela usizi 
nezinyembezi. Selokhu ngawujoyina umbutho wamaphoyisa, 
angikaze ngihlangabezane nobunzima obufana nalobuya 
engahlangabezana nabo mhla nginembeka ethangeni.” Asho 
uSayitsheni ebalekisa amehlo ewabhekisa kude le ezinkalweni, 
kubonakale ukuthi kukhona lapho okuthinteke khona enxebeni. 
Yayingekho enye into eyayingaselapha lesi silonda esasihlale 

189 



sibhibha enhliziyweni ngaphandle kokuthi asibophe lesi 
sigebengu esasimdubulile. Wayesesibona kahle isizathu esasidala 
ukuba uKaputeni athethe ngale ndlela. Ukuba wayezinikela 
ngokuphelele emsebenzini, kwakungeke kube lula kuNguzunga 
ukubahlasela abanqobe bobathathu kwaMnguni. UNguzunga 
wayinqoba le mpi ngenxa yokuthi yena uSayitsheni wayengekho 
ethathwe yizindlela zakhe ngesikhathi somsebenzi. Kwase 
kumkhanyele kahle nokuthi ukudubuleka kwakhe kwakuyisijeziso 
sokudlala kwakhe ngomsebenzi. 

“Ngakhona Mbomvu. Sonke kwasithinta kakhulu 
ukudutshulwa kwakho uzama ukuvikela uthisha ekuhlaselweni 
yingane yesikole. Phela lo muntu weNkosi wasindela nina. 
Ukuba naningekho, hhawu, ngabe sikhuluma indaba yokuthi 
usawushiya lo mhlaba. Impela ngiyabadabukela othisha. Bathi 
bafundisa izingane bazinika ifa laphakade ezingenakuliphucwa 
muntu, zona zibashaye ngalo ebusweni. Zenza sengathi zifundela 
othisha noma abazali bazo kanti zizifundela zona. Ngelazo leli 
kusasa ezilihudula edakeni. Mina ngithi umuntu othatha isinkwa 
asicwilise emanzini, akayekwe asidle simanzi sinjalo. Nazo lezi 
zingane ezihlupha othisha zizozibona ukuqeda. Kuyeza ukuhlwa. 
Ziyosikhumbula lesi sikhathi ezidlala ngaso.” 

“Ngingaka nje Khabazela, angikaze ngiyibone ingane yesikole 
eyisigelekeqe njengalowaya mfana. Ngisafisa nokho ukwazi ukuthi 
ingabe lokhu kuchaza ukuthi zonke izikole zalapha eNingizimu-
Afrika zinezigebengu eziyingozi ngale ndlela? Phela uma kunjalo, 
kuyobe kuchaza ukuthi asikho ndawo thina sizwe esimnyama.” 

“Yizwi lelo mntakaNgubane.” 

“Into engikhathaza kakhulu emoyeni Khabazela, yikhona 
ukuthi sagcina siphunyukile isigebengu. Saphunyuka unomphela. 
Kumanje nje akwaziwa lapho sikhona. UKaputeni uwuhlabe ngazo 
zonke izindlela umkhosi kodwa kuze kube yinamuhla asitholakali.” 
Awasho lawo mazwi uSayitsheni maqede abheke phansi. 

190 



“Usho ukuthi akukho ngisho nomncane nje umkhondo

“Lutho Khabazela. Ngendlela engifisa ngayo ukuba atholakale 
lo mfana, ngiyabona ukuthi ngingabulala behle ubuthongo 
ebusuku uma kungase kwenzeke lokho. Sengiquba kuse ngilokhu 
ngilwa nesu lokumbamba.” 

“Kufanele Mbomvu. Akumngani wamuntu ukudutshulwa 
yisigebengu.” 

“Ngifuna ukusibamba mina mathupha lesi sigebengu. 
Uma ngingasibhadama ndaweni thizeni, hhawu, kungabe 
kusishele. Impela kungamane kufe ofayo. Ngizizwa nginecala 
elikhulu kabi enhliziyweni yami uma lo mfana esajangaza 
ngaphandle.” Awasho lawo mazwi uSayitsheni maqede abeke

kumcacele uMkhize ukuthi kwakukhona okwakudla uSayitsheni

nje ukudubuleka kwakhe, kodwa indlela ayebalisa ngayo yayixoxa

“Mina angihambisani nalesi sifiso sakho sokubhudukeza

buhlungu obusenhliziyweni. Inhliziyo iyisilima ngoba kwesinye

“Kimi ukufa nokuphila kuyefana Khabazela. Nanamuhla 
ngisazisola ngephutha engalenza mhla sijutshwe ukuba siyoqapha 
uThish’omkhulu waseBonokuhle. Ukuba angilishiyanga lodwa 
iphoyisa ngaya ezindaweni zami, babengeke balimale oZondo 
noMnguni. Phezu kwalelo phutha engalenza, ngabuya sengidle

zomsebenzi.” 

191 



“Hhayi bo Ngubane! Uthini manje?” Abuze uMkhize ethukile. 

“Impela Khabazela, kunjengoba ngisho nje. Angingabazi 
ukuthi lo mfana owangidubula kusenguye lona owasephuca 
izibhamu. Ukudubuleka kona, ngadubuleka kungafanele. 
Ukuba ngangikhona mhla ehlasela kwaMnguni lo mfana futhi 
ngingadakiwe, nakanjani sasizomehlula, aboshwe. Namanje 
ngidutshulwe ngumuntu okwakufanele ukuthi ngabe waboshwa 
kudala.” 

“Cha, angisenamlomo Mbomvu, ngiyisimungulu. Yingakho 
inhliziyo yakho ingenakukuthola ukuthula.” 

“UKaputeni wayehlala engithethisa nsuku zonke 
engibiza ngazo zonke izinto ezingasile. Wayesho nokuthi 
ukungawuhloniphi kwami umsebenzi wokuvikela umphakathi 
kuguqule igama lesiteshi samaphoyisa laba libi emphakathini. 
Konke lokhu ngangikushaya indiva ngithi wenziwa yilokhu 
kuguga ayikhona. Ngangingamboni engumuntu okhathazekile 
ngenxa yokuhlukumezeka komphakathi sibe sikhona 
singamaphoyisa. Mina ngaleso sikhathi ngangimane ngibuke 
izimvu ekhanda lakhe ngizitshele ukuthi ubulawa wukuguga 
kanye nokusebenzisa izindlela zakudala zokuphatha. Kafushane 
nje ngangimbona engihlukumeza ngoba ngisebenza ngaphansi 
kwakhe. Ngikhumbula kahle mhlazane sizithela kulo mfana 
owayefuna ukudubula uthisha. Nalapho ngangingafuni 
ukuyokwenza uphenyo esikoleni ngokuhlukumezeka 
kwaso ngakho njalo ukuthi ngangimbona engihlukumeza 
nje uKaputeni engiqhatha nezigebengu. Kodwa ngemuva 
kokuba sengidubulekile, kwangikhanyela ukuthi uKaputeni 
wayengangihlukumezi kodwa wayefuna ukuthi ngiwenze 
ngokwethembeka umsebenzi wami. Ngalezi zizathu, lokhu 
okwangehlela kwakungifanele. Ngangizicabangela mina, 
ngingawucabangeli umphakathi engiwusebenzelayo.” 

“Musa ukukhuluma kanjalo Mbomvu. Akekho umuntu 

192 



ofanelwe wukudutshulwa,” kusho uMkhize ebheke phansi. 
Wayesekutholile lokhu ayekubona kuququda uSayitsheni 
ngaphakathi. Wazizwa emdabukela kakhulu. Naye uMkhize 
wayenesifuba ayengazi ukuthi uzosithulula kanjani emaphoyiseni 
ngoba wayethembisile kuMaMthiyane, unkosikazi wakhe ukuthi 
akazukusivulela muntu. Kodwa manje indlela ayebalisa ngayo 
uSayitsheni yayinokumlinga ukuba ayidalule le mfihlo ayehlezi 
phezu kwayo. 

Wazibamba kaningana impela ukuba angaphahluki 
kuSayitsheni, kodwa wagcina ehlulekile. Phela uSayitsheni 
kwakungumngani wakhe omdala besengabafundi esikoleni 
esiphakeme, iSizanathi Secondary School. Babedume ngokudlala 
ibhola likanobhutshuzwayo. Ngesikhathi uSayitsheni eyofundela 
ubuphoyisa, yena wahamba wayofundela ukukhanda izimoto. 

“Mfowethu, nawe waba ngumkhandi wezimoto odumile ngoba 
umsebenzi wakho wabe uwenza ngokuzinikela nangokwethembeka. 
Ukuba nawe wawenza njengami, ngabe awuzange ulivule leli 
galaji. Ngikhathazekile mfowethu. Uma ngingase ngizithele phezu 
kwakhe lo mfana, ngingafela phezu kwakhe.” 

UMkhize wabonakala esesula izithukuthuku ezingekho 
ebusweni. Wathi esuka wayethi, “Uyazi Ngubane, njengoba 
ukhuluma nje ngizizwa nginecala ngaphambi kwamehlo omhlaba. 
Nakuwe imbala ngizizwa nginecala. Khona ngiyafisa ukukusiza 
kule nkinga yakho kodwa ngiyesaba.” Asho la mazwi uMkhize 
maqede athi voshosho etsheni eliseduze kwakhe. Abeke izandla 
ebusweni, abusule maqede aphonse amehlo kude le ezinkalweni. 
Kwakungathi umqondo umhlamukile, wadazuluka wayozula 
emathafeni lapho kungakhali ngcede khona. 

Lokhu kukhathazeka kukaMkhize kanye namazwi 
ayesewashilo, kwamethusa uSayitsheni. Wazama ukuqoqa 
umqondo wakhe ukuze ezwe kahle ukuthi wayefuna ukuthini 
uMkhize. 

193 



“Ngubane mfowethu,” kusho uMkhize ngezwi eliphansi 
nelimumethe usizi kuhlangene novalo. “Sengathi lesi sigebengu 
okhuluma ngaso sike sabonakala khona lapha kwelakithi.” 

“Hhayi bo Khabazela! Uthi sibonakelephi lesi sigebengu?” 
kubuza uSayitsheni ngokwethuka. Wayesehlahle amehlo 
engacwayizi. 

“Sibonakele lapha eMandabeni.” 

“Ngiyadideka Khabazela.” 

“Musa ukudideka mfowethu. Kunjengoba ngisho nje. Futhike 
ngibeka kabi uma ngithi sike sabonakala. Sengathi sikhona 
njengoba ngikhuluma nje.” 

“Sikhona kuphi Khabazela? Shesha mfowethu, sikuphi 
isigebengu?” Wabuza uSayitsheni maqede wakhipha iduku 
ekhukhwini wasula ubuso. Kwavevezela ngisho nebhulukwe 
manje. Kwakungelona uvalo lolu olwalumqhaqhazelisa kodwa 
kwakuyintukuthelo. 

“Mbomvu, nami angisibonanga ngamehlo lesi sigebengu 
kodwa indaba yaso ngayizwa ngonkosikazi. Naye wayithola 
ezinganeni. Kuthiwa sicashiswe khona lapha kwamakhelwane 
endlini ehlala ikhiyiwe.” Asho uMkhize ekhomba umuzi oseduze 
nakwakhe. 

“Sihlobene kanjani nalo mndeni wakwamakhelwane wakho 
lesi sigebengu Khabazela?” 

“Sengathi sithandana nentombi engumzukulu wesalukazi 
sakhona lapha kwaSokhela. Ngiyabona ukuthi le ntombi 
isicashisile njengoba sifunwa ngabomthetho nje.” 

“Uphi umnumzane wakhona?” 

“Washona kudala. Lesi salukazi sesizihlalela nalo mzukulu 
waso kanye nenye intombazanyana ecishe ibe seminyakeni 
elishumi ubudala. Lo mzukulu waso ukhulelwe. Ngicabanga 

194 



ukuthi umnikazi womonakalo yisona lesi sigebengu.” 

“Awu kodwa izingane zethu bakithi! Zihamba ziziphonsa nje 
ngale kokubukisisa izinto. Ake ungitshele nje ukuthi likuphi 
ikusasa lale ntombi kulesi sigebengu esinjena?” 

“Izingane ziyiziphoxi Mbomvu. Zona zijatshuliswa 
wukuthanda izinswelaboya ngoba zithola ukuhlonishwa 
ngabangani bazo. Azikwazi ukuhlukanisa into embi kwenhle. 
Ngake ngezwa ngonkosikazi ukuthi le ntombi yakwamakhelwane 
yaxoshwa esikoleni ngoba ikhulelwe. Sengathi noyise wayixosha 

ekhaya njengoba isihlala lapha kwagogo wayo nje.” 

“Kanti ingakanani le ntombi, Khabazela?” 

“Hhawu, yingane leya Mbomvu. Icishe ibe seminyakeni 
elishumi nesikhombisa. Nakho nje ukufihla kwayo isigebengu 
esiyingozi kangaka kuseyikhona ukuthi ayazi lutho. Phela kuyicala 
elinzima kabi lokhu ekwenzayo.” 

“Kodwa aniwabikelanga ngani amaphoyisa Khabazela? 
Mhlawumbe sikhuluma nje sesibalekile.” 

“Angiboni kanjalo Mbomvu. Sisekhona.” 

“Sekuphele isikhathi esingakanani sibonakele?” 

“Alikapheli iviki Mbomvu. Sibonakele ngoMsombuluko.” 

“Awu kodwa bakithi! Nangawabikela ngani amaphoyisa nibe 
nazi kahle ukuthi sifunwa phansi phezulu lesi sigebengu?” 

“Mfowethu, kwabhoka uvalo kunkosikazi. Mina ngangithi 
akuhlatshwe umkhosi kwabomthetho, siboshwe isigebengu. 
Hhawu, unkosikazi wavele wakhuza wababaza wathi akuwona 
umsebenzi wethu ukubopha abantu. Kungumsebenzi 
wamaphoyisa ukuthungatha izigebengu aze azithole. Washo 
nokuthi uma beke bathola lapha kwaSokhela ukuthi yithina 
esibophise umkhwenyana wabo, siyoshela endlini. Ngalezo 
zizathu ngagcina sengiququda imihlathi nje ngingazi ukuthi 

195 



ngizothini futhi ngenzenjani. Ngagcina sengithulile-ke.” 

“Khabazela, uhlezi nendaba enkulu kangaka?” 

“Impela mfowethu. Nami iyangishisa manje le ndaba.” 

“Ake ungichazele kahle Khabazela ukuthi izingane 
zakuthathaphi konke lokhu ongitshela kona?” 

“Unkosikazi wangitshela ukuthi ngoMsombuluko ngemuva 
kwamadina, kwafika le ntombazanyana yakhona kwamakhelwane 
izocela uthunjana wakwami, uNgcosana, ukuba ayiphelekezele 
iye esitolo. Babezoyothengela isigebengu leso ugwayi. Zahambake 
izingane. Kuthe lapho sezibuya esitolo, zayifica ingekho 
intombi yesigebengu iyokha amanzi esiphethwini. Izingane-ke 
ngokungazi, zathatha ukhiye wokuvula elawini lentombi phezu 
kwetafula ekhishini, zanikela khona. Zafike zasivula isicabha 
zasho phakathi endlini. Zamnika-ke umbhemu ugwayi.” Asho 
bese ethula isikhashana uMkhize. 

“Kusobala ukuthi le ntombi ikhiyele ukuthi kungezeki 
nangephutha athuke ebonakala lo mlisa wayo lapha elawini.” 

“Yiqiniso lelo Mbomvu.” 

“Ake uqhubeke Khabazela, ngizwe.” 

“Uma esho-ke unkosikazi uthi ukungena kwezingane kule 
ndlu kwasicasula kabi isigebengu. Samane sazithethisa izingane 
saziyala ukuba zingaphinde ziyibeke imiconjwana yazo lapha 
elawini. Sazitshela nokuthi uma zike zaphinda, siyozinquma zife 
nya. Saphinde sazixwayisa ngokuthi zize zingalokothi ziyixoxe le 
ndaba emakhaya. Zithule nayo zize zife.” 

“Ake nizwe nje. Sasizethusa lezi zingane.” 

“Kunjalo Mbomvu. UNgcosana wabukhumbula lobu buso 
obabuthetha. Wathi babufana ncamashi nobesigebengu esavezwa 
kumabonakude kuthiwa sifunwa ngamaphoyisa.” 

“Ngikuzwile konke okushoyo Khabazela. Sengathi abakithi 

196 



bangibhekile namuhla, ngiwafunge amaBomvu! Siyolala 
esitokisini namuhla lesi sigebengu. Kwasayona le ntombi 
yakhona, iyoboshwa izandla nezinyawo ngokufihla isigelekeqe

amanqe. Okungikhathaza kakhulu emoyeni ngukuthi akekho

“Kuhle-ke ngoba usuyakubona nalokho Khabazela. Ukuthula

Ngiyasibonga nokho isibindi sakho ngokuyidalula le nto. 
Ungakhohlwa futhi ukuthi ngokwenzenjalo, usuphule abantu 
abaningi engozini abebekade belengele kuyona. Nomndeni wakho 
uwophulile engozini.” 

“Kunjalo Mbomvu. Kukini-ke ukuthi nimisa kanjani. 
Beningasithola kahle lesi sigebengu kusalelwe nje.” 

“Njengamanje nje nginikela khona Khabazela. Kuyofa ofayo 
ngiyakutshela.” Asho uSayitsheni kucace ukuthi usesifuna 
lapha isigebengu. Aphuthaze ivolovolo alungele ukuyohlasela 
kwamakhelwane kaMkhize. Ayaluze okwenkunzi izohlatshwa. 

Lokhu kuzinikela kukaSayitsheni ngokuyobamba isigebengu 
esiyingozi kangaka ehamba yedwa, kwamethusa uMkhize. 
Ingqondo yakhe yaqala phansi yaqoqa konke lokhu ayekushilo 
uSayitsheni ngalesi sigebengu, ikakhulukazi ubungozi baso. 
Wacabanga ukuthi uma kuyisona ngempela lesi sigebengu 

197 



esashaya amaphoyisa sawephuca izibhamu, pho wayezosinqoba

sokuthi lesi sigebengu sasingahlomile. Ayedingeka ngempela 
amanye amaphoyisa ukwelekelela uSayitsheni. 

Wakucabanga konke lokhu uMkhize maqede wezwakala

thinta abalingani bakho khona manje ngomsakazo wokuxhumana 
ubanxenxe ukuba baphuthume bazokwelekelela. Ngeke usibambe 
wedwa lesi sibebengu.” 

“Kahle-ke Khabazela.” Asho uSayitsheni emkhuza ngesandla. 
“Yindaba endala lena oyicabangayo. Siyahamba isikhathi. Uma 
abantu bakulo muzi beyibona le moto kahulumeni, angingabazi

Siyophinde sisitholephi-ke njengoba kuyilizwe lezintaba leli?” 

“Angikuvimbeli Mbomvu ekutheni ungayenzi into oyifisayo. 
Uma kungukuthi uyazethemba futhi uyalibona iqhinga

ukuba unyawo lwakho lungasheleli.” Washo lawo mazwi uMkhize

“Khabazela, besengike ngakuchazela ukuthi ngidlalile

isithunzi sesiteshi samaphoyisa emphakathini. Uma kube 

198 



yinhlanhla yaso lesi sigebengu, sizonginqoba. Kodwa nakhona 
lapho singanginqoba sizwile. Yinye kuphela into engiyaziyo

“Yini leyo Mbomvu.” 

“Ayinyonki kabili! Angisiniki lutho.” 

“Cha mfowethu, angisenawo amaningi.” 

“Yiliphi ilawu lale ntombi Khabazela?” 

“Yileliya elinomnyango obheke ezansi emhosheni. Isalukazi 
nentombazanyana bahlala kuleya ndlu efulelwe ngothayela

“Ngiyabonga Khabazela, ngisanikela khona.” Washo ethatha 
izinyawo ngokushesha uSayitsheni eselibambe ngesandla 
ivolovolo. 

“Baze bahambe nawe abakini Mbomvu,” kusho uMkhize 
emphelekezela ngamehlo. Wasukuma kancane etsheni ayehlezi 
kulo okomuntu ofelwe yizwe. Wezwa ikhanda limsinda, 
linkenketha sengathi kade likhobolwa ngezinguzunga zamatshe. 
Khona manjalo wawuzwa umsakazo wokuxhumana emotweni 
kahulumeni ubiza uSayitsheni. Wathula uMkhize wawubuka 
ngokuwudabukela ngoba wawungezukuphendulwa muntu. 
Wamemeza umsakazo waze wadela. 

USayitsheni wahamba ngokushesha nangokucophelela 
waze wayoma ngasemnyango welawu likaNcamsile. Wahlohla 
ivolovolo. Ngenhlanhla yayingekho inja lapha kwaSokhela 
neyayingaba yisiphazamiso emsebenzini wakhe. Nabomndeni 
babesalele bengazi ukuthi kwenzekani ngaphandle. 

Wacutha uSayitsheni emnyango ebeke indlebe esicabheni. 
Wayefuna ukuthola kahle ukuthi kwakwenzekani ngaphakathi 
endlini. Nangempela wawezwa amazwi abantu ababili, owesilisa 
nowesifazane bexoxa. Babexoxela phansi, behleka kumnandi 
impela nje. Akakungabazanga uSayitsheni ukuthi laba ababexoxa 

199 



kwakunguNcamsile noNguzunga. Lwamgabha ulaka. Umzimba 
wathuthumela. Izandla zajuluka. Ivolovolo laqhaqhazela. Amehlo 
amvezela umhlaba uyibhola elizungezayo. Nezindlebe zakhe zase 
ziziqambele eyazo imisindo engaqondakali ukuthi iqhamukaphi. 
Ngemuva kwemizuzwana kwaphinde kwedlula konke. 

Wazibamba uSayitsheni wangalulalela ulaka olwalulwa naye 
lumthuma ngaphakathi endlini. Wayeyibona ingozi eyayingase 
imehlele uma engqongqoza ngesankahlu ephoqa abasendlini 
ukuba bavule isicabha. Wabe azi ukuthi uNguzunga uhlomile 
lapha endlini kodwa wayengazi ukuthi uzonyakaza ngayiphi 
indlela uma sekonakele. Ngaleyo ndlela kwakudingeka ukuba 
avule amehlo angacwayizi. Wayenqume ukuba aqhubeke 
nokucutha emnyango aze avule uNcamsile. 

Akuphelanga mizuzu mingaki ecuthile uSayitsheni, 
kwezwakala umsindo wokuvuleka komshudo wesicabha. 
Walibambisisa ivolovolo. Wayehlose ukuthi sithi singavuleka 
isicabha, angene naso ngaphakathi endlini. Wakubonga ukuphuza 
kwesalukazi nentombazanyana ukuvuka. Ukuba babevuke kuqala 
kunoNcamsile, kwakuzokonakala izinto eziningi. Iphupho 
lakhe lokubuyisa isithunzi sesiteshi samaphoyisa kwakufanele 
lifezeke, kumnyama kubomvu. Washaya umthandazo omncane 
uSayitsheni. 

Sathi singathi gekle isicabha, wasuka amagonso uSayitsheni 
waphonseka ngaphakathi endlini. UNcamsile wavele 
waphonseka laphaya ezansi kombhede washaya amankeyana 
khona. Wayedunyelwa yikhanda engazi ukuthi kwenzekani. 
Akaqondanga noma wayeshaywe yimpundulu ayehlala eyizwa 
ngendaba. Konke kwakwenzeka ngokushesha. 

Engqondweni kaNguzunga kwakudlala ifilimu. Wayebukeka 
edidekile engazi noma wayephupha yini. Ngeshwa wayesalele, 
engaphansi kwezingubo. Lokho kwaba wusizo olukhulu 
kuSayitsheni ngoba kwawenza waba lula umsebenzi wakhe. Wathi 

200 



uqambe uyahleleka umqondo kuNguzunga, base bebenyezela 
ezandleni ozankosi. Wamane wakhamisa nje amehlo acweba 
izinyembezi. 

“Yebo-ke mfo kaNyakanyaka. Uthi wawazi nje ukuthi

“Kodwa muntu womthetho, wangibopha kabuhlungu kangaka

“Usenesibindi sokubuza umbuzo onjenga lona? Bengicabanga

“Angikwazi mina phoyisa.” 

“Uzongazi-ke namuhla. Ngingumenziwa! Ukuba 
wawuhlakaniphile, wawuzomane ungidubule ngifele khona lapho 
esikoleni. Iba yingozi inyoka ogcina ngokuyinyathela emsileni

Kubo lobo bunzima, avuke phansi uNcamsile asho ngengila

201 



izandla ekhanda ekhala ewuqanduqandu. Singabe sisazihlupha

“Ubokhuluma uwakhethe amazwi akho wena mfana. Kuyicala 

202 



kwakhona lokhu ongibelesela ngakho. Wakuzwaphi ukuthi

“Lalela-ke ntombazane. Sengibona kahle manje ukuthi nina

yona uyoyibikela inkantolo. Izitatimende niyozibhala esiteshini 
samaphoyisa. Kuyophela nya lokhu kusa eninakho.” 

“Hhayi bo! Anginacala mina!” Asho ahlahle amehlo

203 



ungikhulumele naleli phoyisa lingangibophi. Angazi lutho mina

“Ngavele ngasho ukuthi lo mfana ofuywe imini nobusuku

“Hawu kodwa bakithi! Nawe Gogo uyangilahla?

“Uzenzile akakhalelwa Ncamsile,” kusho isalukazi maqede

nginesandla ekucashiseni isigebengu kanti akunjalo. Kwasamina 
bengihlezi kabuhlungu ngingazi ukuthi ngizokwenzenjani. 
Le ngane mntanami ayingazi nokuthi ngingubani. Ngisho 
noyise akakhulumi nami ngale ndlela yona ekhuluma ngayo. 
Ngikhuluma nje iyiqede yonke imali yami ebhange yondlana 
nalesi sigebengu sayo esihlala endlini imini nobusuku sengathi 
yinkukhu edla imeshi. Uma ngiyikhuza ngalezi zinto ezenzayo, 
iyangibhodlela isho ukungiqeda. Angiyingeni nakancane 
nje indaba yayo nalo mgulukudu wayo. Bathathe impela 
bayobhekana nomthetho. Nale ngane azethwele yona uNcamsile 
useyoyitholela khona ejele.” Sasho isalukazi sathi khenye khenye 
sayongena endlini yaso. 

Amazwi esalukazi amthukuthelisa kakhulu uSayitsheni. Lwaqala 
phansi ulaka. Wasuka lapho ayemi khona wathatha izingubo 
zikaNguzunga nezicathulo wajikijela ngakho uNcamsile. Wafola 
uNcamsile elokhu ekhale lokho, wazicosha izimpahla maqede 
kwahanjwa. Kwakuhamba uNguzunga phambili elandelwa 
nguNcamsile. USayitsheni wayebaqhuba ngevolovolo ephethe 
no machine-gun kaNguzunga owawungasenazo izinhlamvu. 
Wabakhombisa imoto kahulumeni lapho yayipake khona. 

204 



Wacishe waquleka uNcamsile uma ebona umndeni 
wakwaMkhize ngothi lwawo umi egcekeni ubabuka ngamehlo 
adabukile. Wayengazi ukuthi uzowubhekelwa ngubani. 
Kwavele kwamcacela ukuthi kwakuyiwona owawubabizele 
amaphoyisa. Wambona noNgcosana, angananazanga ukuthi 
kwakunguyena owayebikele abazali bakhe ngoNguzunga. Ngaleso 
sikhathi amehlo kaNgcosana ayenamathele kulo Nguzunga 
owayebathembise ukubenzakalisa uma beke babatshela abazali 
babo ngaye. 

Kwathi lapho bengena kwaMkhize oSayitsheni neziboshwa, 
uSayitsheni waqonda emotweni wafike wavula isicabha 
sangemuva maqede zangena iziboshwa. Washuda isicabha wase 
ephendukela kuMkhize. 

“Khabazela, ungizele mfowethu. Ngaphandle kwakho, 
belingeke lifezeke iphupho lami.” 

“Bamba ithambo mfo kaMbomvu.” Washo emxhawula 
uMkhize. “Uyindoda emadodeni. Awu, kodwa isibindi sakho! 
Ngiyakwesaba Mbomvu.” 

Bahleka bobabili oSayitsheni noMkhize. Bavalelisana. 
Wangena emotweni uSayitsheni, wayishaya yazula eseyikhohliwe 
nendaba yemoto yakhe ayezoyihlola lapha kwaMkhize. 
Ngaphakathi emoyeni wayenokujabula nokuthula. Wayeseqala 
nokuzizwa ukuthi wayeyiphoyisa loqobo. Phela wayekwazile 
ukubopha umuntu owayebahlule bancama noKaputeni. 

Yaklwebha imoto yamaphoyisa yaze yayofika esiteshini. 
Yangena ngolukhulu ulaka yayokuma ngasehhovisi likaKaputeni. 
Wayehamba nje engazi ukuthi uKaputeni wayeke wambiza 
kaningana emoyeni wangasabela. NoMkhize wayengamtshelanga. 

“Ngubane, kanti unjani nje wena? Zolo lokhu kade 
uzibhongqa phansi uxolisa, waze wathembisa nokuzinikela 
ekusebenzeleni umphakathi ngokwethembeka. Akukapheli 

205 



nsuku zingaki ukwenzile lokho, nakhu manje usuphindele shi 
emkhubeni wakho omdala. Uyimfene yini yona engalulahli 
ukhopho lwayo?” Washo uKaputeni egcizelela nangezandla. 
Wamane wazihlekela nje uSayitsheni wadonsa isihlalo wahlala 
phansi. UZondo yena wayethukile. Eqinisweni wayeswele indlela 
ayengambonisa ngayo uSayitsheni ngoba ecabanga ukuthi udlala 
ngomsebenzi. 

“Ngenzeni kodwa nsizwa endala njengoba usungiphuthuma 
ngamazwi aqine kangaka nje ngingakanibuzi nempilo?” 

“Kungani ungawuphendulanga umsakazo wokuxhumana 
ngesikhathi ngikubiza emoyeni?” kubuza uKaputeni ngomoya 
ophansi. Wayezama ukugqiba intukuthelo eyase ilokoza 
ngaphakathi. 

“Angiwuzwanga Macingwane. Ngiyaxolisa mfowethu.” 

“Ake ungitshele ukuthi uphumaphi njengoba ufika ngalesi 
sikhathi emsebenzini?” 

“Bengisemsebenzini Kaputeni.” Asho asukume uSayitsheni. 
“Ngicela ukuthi nisukume ningilandele ukuze nibone ukuthi 
ngempela bengisemsebenzini.” 

Basukume oKaputeni noZondo baphume balandele 
uSayitsheni. Uma befika emotweni, uSayitsheni avule isicabha 
sangemuva maqede athi, “Nakhu-ke Kaputeni okudale ukuba 
ngifike ngalesi sikhathi lapha esiteshini. Bengingahlezi kodwa 
bengisebenza. Mhlawumbe umsakazo ungimemeze ngesikhathi 
ngisasebenza.” 

“Hha…wu! Ngubane, kodwa ngibonani ngamehlo ami? 
Ngiyaphupha yini?” Waqhubeka wababaza into engapheli 
uKaputeni. 

“Awuphuphi Kaputeni. Nguyena ngempela lo feleba obekade 
esibulalisa ngamakhanda singazi ukuthi siyomthola kuphi izwe 
lingaka nje.” 

206 



“Nguyena lo Nguzunga Sayitsheni?” kubuza uZondo esondela 
emotweni embukisisa kahle lo mfana owayebukeka elungile. 

“Nezinqotho Zondo.” 

“Usitholephi lesi sigebengu, Ngubane?” kubuza uKaputeni. 

“Ngisithole sicashe ekhweni laso, sicashiswe nguyena lo makoti 
waso enimbonayo.” 

“NguPhoshozwayo! Njengoba egqoke amaphijama nje lo 
mfokazi, ubelele yini ngesikhathi umbopha?” 

“Usushilo Kaputeni. Kunjalo nje.” 

“Cha, ungehlulile namuhla Ngubane. Phela wena 
awusakufanele ukuba nguSayitsheni. Angazi ukuthi ngizothi 
ufanelwe yisiphi isikhundla. Kufanele uklonyeliswe ngezindondo 
eziphambili nezihlonishwayo. Wena Zondo, thatha lezi ziboshwa 
uyozivalela. Uthi ungaqeda bese uya ehhovisi lami lapho uyosifica 
khona noNgubane ukuze asixoxele kahle ukuthi usibambe kanjani 
lesi sigebengu esiyingozi kangaka!” Asho uKaputeni maqede 
aqhwebe uSayitsheni bahambe baye ehhovisi lakhe. 

Waziqhuba iziboshwa uZondo wayozivalela. Wathi angaqeda 
wase eya ehhovisi likaKaputeni. USayitsheni wabalandisa lonke 
udaba waze wayoluphetha esebabophile oNguzunga noNcamsile. 
Babamba ongezansi oKaputeni noZondo. Abayivalanga imilomo 
bebabaza isibindi sikaSayitsheni. 

UKaputeni wahlela indumezulu yomcimbi wokwethwesa 
uSayitsheni izindondo zobuqhawe. Waphinde wamhlelela ukuba 
akhushulelwe esikhundleni esiphakeme. 

UMnguni waphuma esibhedlela waqonda ekhaya. Wahlala 
izinsuku ezine engakabuyeli esikoleni nokwabe kungumyalelo 
kadokotela. Ukufika kwakhe ekhaya kwaba yinjabulo kunkosikazi 
wakhe kanye nezingane zabo ezimbili, uNoluthando noNduduzo. 

207 



Omakhelwane nabazalwane, nabo babejabule kakhulu. 

NgeSonto ekuseni inkonzo yabanjelwa ekhaya kwakhe 
uMnguni. Wayezoqiniswa ngezwi leNkosi ngoba kwakuwusuku 
lwakhe lokugcina esezophindela emsebenzini ngakusasa. Yasha 
inkonzo kwabaleka amadimoni. NoMaCele wayesemethemba 
kakhulu uNkulunkulu. Phela wayezibonile izimangaliso zakhe. 

“Uyizwile mzalwane inkonzo ukuthi ibikade imnandi 
kanjani?” kubuza uMfundisi uDubazana kuMnguni. Ngaleso 
sikhathi babesendleleni beya kwaNtabamhlophe eMtshezi. 
UMfundisi wayemhambise ngemoto yakhe, kwazise ukuthi 
wayengakayitholi enye uMnguni. Uma eseya emsebenzini, 
wayezosebenzisa ekaMseleku ngoba yena wayesebenzisa 
eyoMnyango wezeMfundo. 

“Angikwazi okunjeya Baba. Bashumayela abazalwane ngezwa 
ukuthi akusakhulumi bona kodwa sekukhuluma uNkulunkulu 
uqobo.” 

“Kumnandi ukukholwa mzalwane. Umuntu ongamazi 
uNkulunkulu ufana nofileyo. Kwathi lapho engibikela 
undodakazi ukuthi usuqokelwe esikhundleni esiphakeme, ngasho 
ngezwi elikhulu ngathi, makadunyiswe ophezu kwezinto zonke! 
Ngempela akekho ofana naye kulo mhlaba.” 

Yaqombola njalo izintaba imoto kaMfundisi. Yangena 
kwaMseleku selilengele ezintabeni. Bamfica eziphumulele 
uMseleku. 

“Zaze zamnandi izindaba esizizwe ngokusa kwanamuhla,” 
kusho uMseleku ekhombisa ukwenama. 

“Zindaba zini lezo?” kubuza uMnguni. 

“Ngisho indaba yokuboshwa komfana owacishe wadubula 

uSokhela.” 

“Hhayi bo! Useboshiwe umfana wakwaNyakanyaka?” Wabuza 
ngokwethuka uMnguni. 

208 



“Zimkhalele Qwabe.” 

“Ubanjwe nini?” 

“Kuthiwa ubanjwe izolo ekuseni ecashe emzini mumbe 
eMandabeni.” 

“Akehlulwa lutho uThixo bantabami. Ngangihlala ngisho 
kundodana uMnguni ukuthi zonke lezi zinto ezimvelelayo 
nezixova isikole sakhe, uyozichitha uNkulunkulu ngolunye 
usuku. Bonke labo abamhlukumezayo bayohlala obala. Nakhu 
phela aseqalile manje ukufakazeleka amazwi ami. Uma uke 
wathinta umuntu kaThixo, usuke usuthinte yena uqobo,” kusho 
uMfundisi. 

Bazithamunda ezoNguzunga bagcina sebeziphanyeke ethala. 
OMnguni noMseleku babonisana ngosuku okwakufanele 
zidalulwe ngalo izindaba zezikhundla ezintsha esikoleni. 
Bavumelana ngokuthi lokho kwenziwe ngakusasa. 

Sebexoxile oMnguni noMseleku, uMfundisi wacela indlela. 
Bamphelekezela wayongena emotweni. Yasuka yaphindela 
eMgungundlovu. 

209 



ISAHLUKO SESHUMI NANHLANU 


Wayejuluke emanzi uKaputeni ephenya uNguzunga. Wayefuna 
ukulithola kahle lonke iqiniso, ikakhulukazi leli elalizoholela 
ekuboshweni kukaSokhela. Wayemfuna phakathi esitokisini. 

“Uyabona-ke mfana wakwaNyakanyaka, anzima kakhulu 
amacala obhekene nawo. UBen Mabanga usesitshele okuningi 
ngawe okumayelana nokuhlukumeza kwenu uThish’omkhulu. 
Uma ulikhipha lonke iqiniso okomuntu efa, angingabazi ukuthi 
inkantolo iyothi ikugweba ibe ikucabanga ukuthi ujike waba 
ngufakazi wayo. Angithi uyangizwa mfana?” 

“Ngiyakuzwa Kaputeni.” 

“Uzimisele ukusho konke okwaziyo njengoba kunjalo?” 

“Akusekho ukucasha Kaputeni. Kakade selingishonele mina 

kababa! Nonembeza uyangidla.” 

“Kuhle-ke mfana uma ukubona lokho.” 

Avule isiqophamazwi sakhe uKaputeni kanye nedokodo 

alungele ukubhala. 

“Ake usho-ke mfana wakwaNyakanyaka, kukuphi ekhaya?” 

“KuseThekwini kwaMashu.” 

“Uhlobene kanjani nalo muzi otholakale kuwo eMandabeni?” 

“Kukwagogo wentombi engithandana nayo.” 

“Ibikade yazi yini intombi yakho ukuthi icashise isigebengu 

esadubula iphoyisa sacishe sadubula nothisha?” 

“Yebo Kaputeni, kodwa angiyitshelanga ukuthi kwakungubaba 
wayo lona engangifuna ukumdubula.” 

“Uthini futhi manje wena mfana? Kanti kukwabani kulo muzi 
obukade ucashe kuwo?” 

“KukwaSokhela lapho okuzalwa khona uthisha uSokhela, 

210 



ongubaba wale ntombi engithandana nayo.” 

“Uyinja mfana ndini! Ungizwa kahle ukuthi ngithini? 
Ukhomba umukhwe wakho ngesibhamu! Wawukwenzelani 
lokho?” Wabuza uKaputeni esegqolozele uNguzunga emehlweni. 

“Wayengafuni ukungikhokhela imali yami eyizinkulungwane 

ezimbili, namakhulu amahlanu ompondo ayengethembise yona.” 

“Imali engaka! Kwakungeyani leyo mali?” 

Wayilanda indaba uNguzunga kwaba sengathi kukhona 
okuthile ayekudlile nokwakumphalazisa onke amaqiniso njengoba 
enjalo. Wazibala izigameko ngokulandelana kwazo waze wafika 
lapho ebanjwe khona nguSayitsheni. 

“Wawuzoyenzani le mali engaka?” 

“Ngangifuna ukukhokhela ngayo umonakalo engangiwenze 
kuNcamsile.” 

“Hhawu! Unesibindi mfana wakwaNyakanyaka, ngiyakwesaba. 
Yake yenzekaphi into enjalo?” 

“Ngiyamthanda uNcamsile Kaputeni. Yayingekho into 
engangingayenza ukuze ngithole imali yokuvala ihlazo. Lokho 
kwakuzomkhombisa ukuthi ngiyamthanda.” 

“Uthi uyazi nje uSokhela ukuthi ingane yakhe yakhuleliswa 
nguwena sigebengu ndini?” Wawubuza lowo mbuzo uKaputeni 
esedinwe efile. 

“Lutho Kaputeni. Ngamgqiba uNcamsile ukuba angangidaluli 
kubazali bakhe ngoba ngangingaxoshwa esikoleni. Ngase 
ngimethembisa ukuthi ngizozama imali bese ngiyihambisa kubo 
ukuze akwazi ukubuyisana nabazali bakhe ngoba base bemxoshile 
ekhaya. Ukuziveza kwami kubazali bakhe sengizokhokhela 
umonakalo, kwakuzongibeka ethubeni lokuba ngingalahlekelwa 
nguyena.” 

“Uzimisele yini ngale ntombi yakho?” 

211 



“Ngiyamthanda uNcamsile Kaputeni. Angifisi ukulahlekelwa 
nguyena.” 

“Awu! Yimbi kodwa indlela owazama ngayo ukuthola imali. 
Bheka-ke manje ukuthi usubhukuda esizibeni esinjani.” 

“Elokufa kalitsheli Kaputeni.” 

“Umthetho wakho awusile ngempela ekhanda. Wawucabanga 
ukuthi ungavala ihlazo olenze enganeni yomuntu ngemali 
oyikhokhelwe nguyena? Wayezojabula yini uSokhela ngaleso 
senzo?” 

“Wayengeke Kaputeni. Kodwa nami yayingekho into 
engangingayenza. Nami ngangifisa ukuba ngigcine sengiganiwe 
nginomuzi njengabo bonke abantu, ngivuse umuzi kababa.” 

“Uwuvuse ngehlazo pho?” 

Athule uNguzunga angawuphenduli lowo mbuzo. 

“Baphi abazali bakho?” 

“Bashona Kaputeni. Ngasala ngedwa ngoba yayingekho enye 

ingane ababenayo ngaphandle kwami.” 

“Uhlala wedwa nje ekhaya kini?” 

“Cha. Ngihlala nomzala.” 

“Wayishonisaphi imali owayithola ngokudayisa izinsimbi 
zemoto kaMnguni? Angithi ungitshele ukuthi izinsimbi zayo 
zathengwa ngabantu ongabazi?” 

“Kunjalo Kaputeni. Kodwa angiyitholanga yonke imali 
yakhona. Lo muntu owaletha abathengi kimi, wanyamalala 
nabo ngemuva kokucwiya imoto lapho engangiyifihle khona 
ehlathini. Banginika imadlana bangethembisa ukuthi bazobuya 
sebengilethele esele.” 

“Ngimdala uma ngingaka. Angikaze ngiyizwe into enjena.” 
Wawasho lawo mazwi uKaputeni enwaya ikhanda. Waphinde 
waqhubeka nemibuzo. 

212 



“Ake ungitshele kahle manje ukuthi wasithathaphi lesi 
sibhamu sakho?” 

“Ngasithatha komunye umuzi esasihlasele kuwo kwaMashu, 
sithungatha izikhali ezingekho emthethweni. Ngaleso sikhathi 
ngangiyisosha.” 

“Maye! Maye! Maye! Washo ngabona Nyakanyaka ndini! 
Yingakho uyingozi kangaka! Washiyelani emasosheni?” 

“Ngangifuna ukuqhuba izifundo zami.” 

“Pho uzihlanganiselani nobugebengu ngoba uyakuthanda 
ukufunda? Angithi ubuzofunda ugogode bese uzakhela kahle-ke 
umuzi wakwenu ususebenza kahle?” 

Athule uNguzunga abheke phansi. 

“Nalezi ezinye izibhamu onazo wazithola ngaleso sikhathi 

useyisosha?” 

“Yebo Kaputeni.” 

“Wazishonisaphi izibhamu owazephuca amaphoyisa?” 

“Ngazifihla endlini engihlala kuyo kwaBhekuzulu.” 

“Zingatholakala njengamanje?” 

“Yebo Kaputeni.” 

“Wazini ngokubulawa komndeni wakwaMpungose 

eZakhiweni?” 

“Wo, Nkosi yami! Ngangifuna impahla engangingayidayisa 
ukuze uNcamsile athole imali yokuya kwadokotela 
nasemtholampilo njengoba ekhulelwe nje.” 

“Uqonde ukungitshela ukuthi kusenguwena futhi lona 
ohlukumeza umphakathi?” Akhombise ukuphelelwa yisineke 

uKaputeni. 

“Ngiyaxolisa Kaputeni.” 

“Sengibuzwile ubufakazi bakho mfana wakwaNyakanyaka. 

213 



Usungaphindela esitokisini.” 

Wasicisha isiqophamazwi uKaputeni, wavala nedokodo. 
Wamemeza uZondo ukuba aphindisele uNguzunga esitokisini. 
Wathi angabuya uZondo, uKapteni wabalandisa benoSayitsheni 
ngobufakazi ayebutholile kuNguzunga. 

“Niyabona-ke manje zinsizwa zami, iyaphuma impi 
iyohlasela eBonokuhle. Usibulele isikole uSokhela. Ngikhuluma 
nje sibole phuhlu ngenxa yakhe. Ugeqe amagula umfana 
wakwaNyakanyaka. Ngimfuna phakathi esitokisini lo thisha. 
Uyomangala futhi uma esezwa ukuthi uNguzunga lona 
ungumkhwenyana wakwakhe nokuthi nguyena owakhulelisa 
indodakazi yakhe. Uzoboshwa yimina mathupha uSokhela. Nina 
nizohamba noNguzunga niye kwaBhekuzulu ukuze anikhombise 
lapho azifihla khona lezi zibhamu anephuca zona. Nimphoqe 
ukuba aninike nalezi ahlasela ngazo umphakathi. Ningalingi 

nimkhumule amaketango ezinyaweni. Yisosha leli. Liyingozi.” 

Avume amaphoyisa. 

“Njengamanje ngithi, ayiphume impi iyohlasela!” Washo 

uKaputeni esukuma. 

Zaphuma zilandelana izimoto zamaphoyisa. Enye yayiqonde 
kwaBhekuzulu, enye iqonde eBonokuhle. 

Babebuthene ngothi lwabo othisha endlini yokuhlanganela 
esikoleni belalele ukuqhubeka kwenkulumo kaMseleku. 

“Ngiyambonga uSomandla ngokusihlengela le nsizwa 
yakwaMnguni ethunzini lokufa ebikade ingaphansi kwalo. 
Mhlawumbe abanye bethu base belilahlile ithemba lokuthi 
usazophinde abuyele esimweni sakhe sempilo esasimazi ekuso. 
Kodwa ngenxa yokuthi bekungakabi yisikhathi sokuthi sihlukane 
naye kulo mhlaba, usindile. Nangu phela simbona namuhla 
esengumqemane phambi kwethu. Ubukhona bakhe namuhla 

214 



buwuphawu lokuthi emhlabeni izinto azihambi ngokuthanda 
kwabantu. Zihamba ngokuthanda kwalowo ongumdali wazo.” 
Wawasho ngokugcizelela lawo mazwi uMseleku. 

Bashaya izandla othisha. 

“Ngibonga isibindi asikhombisile uMnguni ngokumela iqiniso 
aze anqobe nokufa. Ukuba ubengomunye umuntu, ubezothi 
angabona ukuthi wehlelwa yizigigaba ezinzima bese ecela umaluju 
ahambe. Ukuzinikela kwakhe ekufeni, kusichazele ngokusobala 
ukuthi akayena umuntu othanda izikhundla ngaphezu 
komsebenzi aqashelwe wona. NoMnyango wezeMfundo 
ukuphawulile lokho.” 

Bashaye izandla futhi othisha. Selokhu beqalile ukushaya 
izandla, uSokhela wayezithulele nje esonge izandla. Inhliziyo 
yayigaya izibozi. 

Waqhubeka uMseleku. “UMnguni ubeseqalile ukufeza 
izinjongo zokuza kwakhe lapha eBonokuhle. Ngikhuluma 
nje besekufikile kithi ukuthi izinga lokufunda kulesi sikole 
seliphakeme kakhudlwana kunakuqala. Awu! Ngiyanibongela 
bothisha ngokuthola uThish’omkhulu onjenga lona. Engethemba 
ukuthi sekukhona okuningi okuhle enikufundile kuye.” 

Athathe ingilazi phezu kwetafula uMseleku athele amanzi 
aphuze. Athi angaqeda, aqhubeke nenkulumo. 

“Ukusebenza ngokuzikhandla nangokwethembeka, 
ekugcineni kuyamhlomulisa umuntu. Imisebenzi yakhe emihle 
iyamvulela amasango enkululeko. Njengoba sihlangene namuhla 
bothisha, ngizonibikela ngezindaba ezimnandi ezithinta yena 
uMnguni nomunye wabalingani benu. UThish’omkhulu wenu 
useqokelwe esikhundleni sokuba ngumhloli wezikole zaseMtshezi 
namaphethelo.” 

Kwathi woklo ihlombe endlini. Kwathatha isikhashana 
ukuba bathule othisha ngenxa yenjabulo behalalisela uMnguni. 

215 



Babhiyoza baze badela. Bathula balalela. 

“Uzoqala-ke esikhundleni sakhe esisha ekuqaleni 
kukaNtulikazi. Siyakubongela Qwabe. Uqhubeke njalo 
nokusebenza ngokuzikhandla nakusona lesi sikhundla oqokelwe 
sona.” Washo uMseleku emamatheka. 

“Okunye-ke bothisha engifisa ukuthi nginibonge kukhona, 
wukuzinikela kwenu emsebenzini nibambisene nothisha uZuma 
ngesikhathi uThish’omkhulu wenu esesibhedlela. Nikukhombisile 
ukuthi niyakwazi ukusebenza ngokwethembeka yize engekho 
uThish’omkhulu. Yikhona-ke ukuvuthwa emiqondweni lokhu 
enikwenzile. Njengoba uZuma ekhombisile ukuthi unalo ikhono 
lokuphatha isikole siqhubekele phambili, naye-ke uMnyango 
wezeMfundo umklomelisile. Yena-ke uqokelwe esikhundleni 
sokuba nguThish’omkhulu wenu. Naye-ke uzoqala ngokugcwele 
esikhundleni esisha ekuqaleni kukaNtulikazi. Siyakubongela 
kakhulu nawe mfo kaZuma. Sibadinga kakhulu othisha abafana 
nawe. Ngisho labo abanikwa umsebenzi bawenzisise ngale 
kokulindela inkokhelo.” Washo maqede wanika uZuma incwadi 
eyayingubufakazi balokhu ayesekushilo. 

Bamhalalisela othisha uZuma. Yena-ke uZuma wavele 
wathuka ngoba wayeqala ukuyizwa le ndaba. Kodwa ekugcineni 
wakhombisa ukujabula. 

Kwathi kusenjalo, wasukuma uSokhela wama ngezinyawo 
wathi, “Yifa likaMdliwayini phela leli. Kwabelwana ngesikhundla 
sikhona!” Washo waphuma endlini. Basala bebukana othisha. 
UMseleku wayiqeda inkulumo yakhe engasekho umfo kaSokhela. 
Nangesikhathi sekuphuzwa itiye elalilungiselwe lo mhlangano, 
akazange abe khona. 

Kusemnandi kuphuzwa itiye, yangena isindiza imoto 
yamaphoyisa esikoleni. Wehla uKaputeni waqonda lapho 
okwakuphuzelwa khona itiye wafike wacela ukuxoxa noMnguni. 

216 



Wamchazela ukuthi uzobopha uSokhela ngenxa yobufakazi 
ayesebutholile kuNguzunga ukuthi uthinteka kakhulu 
ekuhlukumezekeni kwesikole. 

Kwasuka esikhulu isidumo bebabaza othisha. Khona manjalo 
wezwakala uZuma esethi, “Ngavele ngasho ukuthi umkhuba 
usekhaya. Kuthomba okhiye emaphoyiseni nje, umthakathi 
ufukanyelwe yithina.” 

Kwabakhanyela nabanye othisha ukuthi kungani uSokhela 
engayanga esibhedlela ukuyohlola uMnguni. Kusobala ukuthi 
wayefisa sengathi angafa ukuze asithole lesi sikhundla ayesifuna. 

“Akagananga udadewethu, walahleka. Kazi uyothini uma ezwa 
ukuthi umyeni wakhe uboshiwe? Kusuke kushiwo into enje-ke 
uma kuthiwa umuntu usuzele emoyeni kwajike kwanukela yena,” 
kusho umfo kaMhlongo. 

“Cha, ngiyamhlonipha umfo kaMnguni. Ukhombisile ukuthi 
uyinkunzi emidwayidwa. Phela bekunzima ukuqagula ukuthi 
iyozala nkomoni ekugcineni njengoba kade kubonakala sengathi 
zindala zombili nje,” kuphawula umfo kaMazibuko. 

“Uphi yena uSokhela?” kubuza uMnguni. 

“Mhlawumbe uzivalele ehhovisi lakhe. Akezwani nabantu 
kulezi zinsuku. Sengathi wabulawa ngabo,” kuphendula uZuma 
ehola uKaputeni phambili beqonde ehhovisi likaSokhela. 
Babelandelwa ngoMnguni noMseleku kanye nabanye othisha. 

UZuma owayehamba phambili, akawakholwanga amehlo akhe 
lapho efika emnyango wehhovisi likaSokhela. Isicabha sasivulwe 
kancane. Walunguza ngaphakathi maqede wakhuza umhlola. 
Wasuka ngelikhulu ijubane wayomela kude. Bathi nhla emnyango 
nalaba abanye, kwayiso leso. Bamemeza othisha besifazane, 
bagijima bethwele izandla emakhanda bengazi ukuthi bayaphi. 
Babodwa ababehlaba umkhosi, bememeza abasebenzi abangebona 
othisha ukuba bazobona umhlola! 

217 



Lokhu kuhayiza kothisha, kwamema amalungu omphakathi 
owabe wakhe eduze kwesikole kanye nalawo ayezidlulela 
ngendlela. Nezingane zaphuma ngamajubane emakilasini 
zizobona lo mhlola okwakukhalwa ngawo. Yase yenzekile 
inkanankana. USokhela wayelenga ngentambo eyayisetshenziswa 
ngabafundi ukudlala umdlalo wokudonsana. Kwakugqobhozwe 
usilingi yase iboshelwa epulangweni. Bavele bankema oMnguni 
noMseleku. Koma amathe kuKaputeni. 

UKaputeni waphindela emotweni eyolanda ikhamera kanye 
nebhukwana elalinepeni phakathi. Waqonda nakho ehhovisi 
likaSokhela. Wafike wathwebula izithombe ezimbalwa wase 
ebhala imininingwane ethile. Sathulwa isidumbu sangeniswa 
enqoleni kahulumeni. Washo phezulu uKaputeni. 

Yasuka imoto, yanyobozela sengathi ngumakoti engena emzini. 
Yaphuma ngesango, yajubalala. 

Phakathi esixukwini sababebukela okwakwenzeka, kwezwakala 
izwi lithi, “Ngabe akafanga uSokhela ukuba angivinjwanga 
esangweni ngaqhethiswa khona. Kudala ngilokhu ngizama 
ukungena. Wo, kulukhuni kulo mhlaba bakithi! Useze wafa 
impela umzukulu kaSikhumbasebhubesi ngenxa yamaqili 
angafuni nesikhundla sakhe? Impela kalikho iqiniso kulo 
mhlaba.” 

Baguquka bonke abantu babheka ngalapho okwakuqhamuka 
ngakhona izwi. Laqhubeka futhi izwi lathi, “Siyokwethemba 
obani kulo mhlaba uma nezifundiswa zakithi seziphenduke 
amaqili nababulali? Ingabe kuseyikhona ukuphucuka 
kwezifundiswa lokhu esekukhiphe isidumbu? Wo, injaloke 
impilo bakwethu!” Lasho ikhehla lejazi ligodle ingalo 
enokhonkolo maqede lakhipha ishungu lalo esikhwameni 
lathi hlwi hlwi kabili. Lanikina ikhanda. Labophisisa ijazi lalo 
ngentambo yokubopha utshani bezinkomo. Lasithwalisisa 
isigqoko salo sikathekwane. Lathi ukusineka kancane, kwavela 

218 



ugqinsi lwezisini ezimnyama. Lafulathela izindonga zesikole. 
Laphinda futhi lazibheka kokugcina. Lazifulathela. Lacothoza 
layophuma ngesango. 

219
